 yuṣmad asmad pratyaya gocarayoḥ viṣaya viṣayiṇoḥ tamaḥ prakāśavat viruddha svabhāvayoḥ itaretara bhāva anupapattau siddhāyām tad dharmāṇām api sutarām itaretara bhāva anupapattiḥ iti atas  asmad pratyaya gocare viṣayiṇi cit ātmake yuṣmad pratyaya gocarasya viṣayasya tad dharmāṇām ca adhyāsaḥ tad viparyayeṇa viṣayiṇaḥ tad dharmāṇām ca viṣaye adhyāsaḥ  mithyā iti bhavitum yuktam tathā api anyonyasmin  anyonya ātmaka tām anyonya dharmān  ca adhyasya itaretarā vivekena atyanta viviktayoḥ dharma dharmiṇoḥ mithyājñāna nimittaḥ satya anṛte mithunīkṛtya ‘aham idam ‘mama idam iti naisargikaḥ ayam loka vyavahāraḥ āha kaḥ ayam adhyāsaḥ  nāma iti ucyate smṛti rūpaḥ paratra pūrva dṛṣṭa avabhāsaḥ tam kecid  anyatra anya dharma adhyāsa iti vadanti kecid tu yatra yad adhyāsaḥ tad viveka agraha nibandhanaḥ  bhrama iti anye tu yatra yad adhyāsaḥ tasya eva viparīta dharma tva kalpanām ācakṣate sarvathā api tu anyasya anya dharma avabhāsa tām na vyabhicarati tathā ca loke anubhavaḥ śuktikā hi rajatavat avabhāsate ekaḥ candraḥ sa dvitīyavat iti katham punar  pratyak ātmani aviṣaye adhyāsaḥ  viṣaya tad dharmāṇām sarvaḥ  hi puras avasthita eva viṣaye viṣaya antara madhyasyati yuṣmad pratyaya apetasya ca pratyak ātmanaḥ aviṣaya tvam bravīṣi ucyate na tāvat ayam ekāntena aviṣayaḥ asmad pratyaya viṣaya tvāt aparokṣa tvāt ca pratyak ātma prasiddheḥ na ca ayam asti niyamaḥ puras avasthita eva viṣaye viṣaya antaram adhya sitavyam iti apratyakṣe api hi ākāśe bālāḥ talamalina tā ādi adhyasyanti evam aviruddhaḥ pratyak ātmani api anātma adhyāsaḥ tam etam evaṃlakṣaṇam adhyāsam paṇḍitā avidyā iti manyante tad vivekena ca vastu svarūpa avadhāraṇam vidyām āhuḥ tatra evam sati yatra yad adhyāsaḥ tad kṛtena doṣeṇa guṇena vā aṇu mātreṇa api sa na sambadhyate tam etam avidyā ākhyam ātmānātmanoḥ ita retarādhyāsam puraskṛtya sarve pramāṇa prameya vyavahārā laukikā vaidikāḥ ca pravṛttāḥ sarvāṇi ca śāstrāṇi vidhi pratiṣedha mokṣa parāṇi katham punar avidyāvat viṣayāṇi pratyakṣa ādīni pramāṇāni śāstrāṇi ca iti ucyate deha indriya ādiṣu ahaṃmama abhimāna rahitasya pramātṛ tva anupapattau pramāṇa pravṛtti anupapatteḥ na hi indriyāṇi anupādāya pratyakṣa ādi vyavahāraḥ sambhavati na ca adhiṣṭhānam antareṇa indriyāṇām vyāpāraḥ sambhavati na ca anadhyasta ātma bhāvena dehena kaścid vyāpriyate na ca etasmin sarvasmin  asati asaṅgasya ātmanaḥ pramātṛ tvam upapadyate na ca pramātṛ tvam antareṇa pramāṇa pravṛttiḥ asti tasmāt avidyāvat viṣayāṇi eva pratyakṣa ādīni pramāṇāni śāstrāṇi ca iti paśu ādibhiḥ ca aviśeṣāt yathā hi paśu ādayaḥ śabda ādibhiḥ śrotra ādīnām sambandhe sati śabda ādi vijñāne pratikūle jāte tatas  nivartante anukūle ca pravartante yathā daṇḍa udyata karam puruṣam abhimukham upalabhya ‘mām hantumayam icchati iti palāyitum ārabhante harita tṛṇa pūrṇa pāṇim upalabhya tam prati abhimukhībhavanti evam puruṣā api vyutpanna cittāḥ krūra dṛṣṭīn ākrośataḥ khaḍga udyata karān balavata upalabhya tatas  nivartante tad viparītān prati pravartante atas  samānaḥ paśu ādibhiḥ puruṣāṇām pramāṇa prameya vyavahāraḥ paśu ādīnām ca prasiddhaḥ aviveka pūrvakaḥ pratyakṣa ādi vyavahāraḥ tad sāmānya darśanāt vyutpattimatām api puruṣāṇām pratyakṣa ādi vyavahāraḥ tad kālaḥ samāna  iti niścīyate śāstrīye tu vyavahāre yadi api buddhi pūrva kārī na aviditvā ātmanaḥ para loka sambandham adhikriyate tathā api na vedānta vedyam aśanāya ādi atītam apeta brahma kṣatra ādi bhedam asaṃsārya ātma tattvam adhikāre apekṣyate anupayogāt  adhikāra virodhāt ca prāk  ca tathābhūta ātma vijñānāt pravartamānam śāstram avidyāvat viṣaya tvam na ativartate tathā hi ‘brāhmaṇaḥ  yajeta ityādīni śāstrāṇi ātmani varṇa āśrama vayaḥ avasthā ādi viśeṣa adhyāsam āśritya pravartante adhyāsaḥ  nāma atasmin  tad buddhiḥ iti avocāma tad yathā putra bhārī ādiṣu vikaleṣu sakaleṣu vā aham eva vikalaḥ sakalaḥ  vā iti bāhya dharmān ātmani adhyasyati tathā deha dharmān ‘sthūlaḥ aham kṛśaḥ aham gauraḥ aham tiṣṭhāmi gacchāmi laṅghayāmi ca iti tathā indriya dharmān ‘mūkaḥ kāṇaḥ klībaḥ  badhiraḥ andhaḥ aham iti tathā antaḥkaraṇa dharmān kāma saṅkalpa vicikitsādhya vasāya ādīn evam ahaṃpratyayinam aśeṣa sva pracāra sākṣiṇi pratyak ātmani adhi asya tam ca pratyak ātmānam sarva sākṣiṇam tad viparyayeṇa antaḥkaraṇa ādiṣu adhyasyati evam ayam anādiḥ anantaḥ  naisargikaḥ adhyāsaḥ  mithyā pratyaya rūpaḥ kartṛ tva bhoktṛ tva pravartakaḥ sarva loka pratyakṣaḥ asya anartha hetoḥ prahāṇāya ātmā eka tva vidyā pratipattaye sarve vedāntā ārabhyante yathā ca ayam arthaḥ sarveṣām vedāntānām tathā vayam asyām śārīrakamīmāṃsāyām pradarśayiṣyāmaḥ vedāntamī māṃsā śāstrasya vyāci khya asitasya idam ādimam sūtram vedāntamī māṃsā śāstrasya vyāci khya asitasya idam ādimam sūtram tatra atha abda ānantarya arthaḥ parigṛhyate na adhikāra arthaḥ brahma jijñāsāyāḥ anadhikārya tvāt  maṅgalasya ca vākya arthe samanvaya abhāvāt  artha antara prayukta eva śrutyā maṅgala prayojanaḥ  bhavati pūrva prakṛta apekṣāyāḥ ca phalata ānantarya avyatirekāt  sati ca ānantarya artha tve yathā dharma jijñāsā pūrva vṛttam veda adhyayanam niyamena apekṣata evam brahma jijñāsā api yad pūrva vṛttam niyamena apekṣate tad vaktavyam svādhyāya ānantaryam tu samānam nanu iha karma avabodhana artham viśeṣaḥ na dharma jijñāsāyāḥ prāk api adhīta vedāntasya brahma jijñāsā upapatteḥ yathā ca hṛdaya ādi avadānānām ānantarya niyamaḥ kramasya vivakṣita tvāt na tathā iha kramaḥ  vivakṣitaḥ śeṣa śeṣi tve adhikṛta adhikāre vā pramāṇa abhāvāt  dharma brahma jijñāsayoḥ phala jijñāsasya bhedāt ca abhyudaya phalam dharma jñānam tad ca anuṣṭhāna apekṣam niḥśreyasa phalam tu brahma vijñānam na ca anuṣṭhāna antara apekṣam bhavyaḥ ca dharmaḥ  jijñāsyaḥ  na jñāna kāle asti puruṣa vyāpāra tantra tvāt iha tu bhūtam brahma jijñāsyam nitya tvāt na puruṣa vyāpāra tantram codanā pravṛtti bhedāt ca yā hi codanā dharmasya lakṣaṇam sā sva viṣaye niyuñjānā eva puruṣam avabodhayati brahma codanā tu puruṣam avabodhayati eva kevalam avabodhasya codanā janya tvāt na puruṣaḥ  avabodhe niyujyate yathā akṣa artha saṃnikarṣeṇa artha avabodhe tadvat  tasmāt kim api vaktavyam yad anantaram brahma jijñāsā upadiśyata iti ucyate nitya anitya vastu vivekaḥ iha amutra artha bhoga virāgaḥ śama dama ādi sādhana saṃpad  mumukṣu tvam ca teṣu hi satsu prāk api dharma jijñāsāyā ūrdhvam ca śakyate brahma jijñāsitum jñātum ca na viparyaye tasmāt atha abdena yathā ukta sādhana saṃpatti ā anantaryam upadiśyate atas śabdaḥ  hetu arthaḥ yasmāt veda eva agnihotra ādīnām śreyaḥ sādhanānām anitya phala tām darśayati ityādiḥ tathā brahma vijñānāt api param puruṣa artham darśayati ityādiḥ tasmāt yathā ukta sādhana saṃpatti anantaram brahma jijñāsā kartavyā brahmaṇaḥ  jijñāsā brahma jijñāsā brahma ca vakṣyamāṇa lakṣaṇam ajanmādyasya yataḥ iti ata eva na brahma śabdasya jāti ādi artha antaram āśaṅkitavyam brahmaṇa iti karmaṇi ṣaṣṭhī na śeṣe jijñāsā apekṣya tvāt jijñāsāyāḥ jijñāsya antara anirdeśāt ca nanu śeṣa ṣaṣṭhī parigrahe api brahmaṇaḥ  jijñāsā karma tvam na virudhyate saṃbandha sāmānyasya viśeṣa niṣṭha tvāt evam api pratyakṣam brahmaṇaḥ karma tvam utsṛjya sāmānya dvāreṇa parokṣam karma tvam kalpayataḥ  vyartha prayāsaḥ syāt  na vyarthaḥ brahma āśrita aśeṣa vicāra pratijñāna artha tvāt iti ced na pradhāna parigrahe tad apekṣitānām artha ākṣipta tvāt brahma hi jñānena āptum iṣṭatama tvāt pradhānam tasmin pradhāne jijñāsā karmaṇi parigṛhīte yaiḥ jijñāsitaiḥ vinā brahma jijñāsitam na bhavati tāni artha ākṣiptāni eva iti na pṛthak sūtrayitavyāni yathā rājā asau gacchati iti ukte sa parivārasya rājñaḥ  gamanam uktam bhavati tadvat  śruti anugamāt ca ayataḥ  vā imāni bhūtāni jāyante ityādyāḥ śrutayaḥ atad vijijñāsasva tad brahma iti pratyakṣam eva brahmaṇaḥ  jijñāsā karma tvam darśayanti tad ca karmaṇi ṣaṣṭhī parigrahe sūtreṇa anugatam bhavati tasmāt brahmaṇa iti karmaṇi ṣaṣṭhī jñātum icchā jijñāsā avagati paryantam jñānam sanvācyāyāḥ  icchāyāḥ karma phala viṣaya tvāt icchāyāḥ jñānena hi pramāṇena avagantum iṣṭam brahma brahma avagatiḥ hi puruṣa arthaḥ niḥśeṣa saṃsāra bīja avidyā ādi anartha nibarhaṇāt tasmāt brahma vijijñāsitavyam tad punar brahma prasiddham aprasddham vā syāt  yadi prasiddham na jijñāsitavyam atha aprasiddham na eva śakyam jijñāsitum iti ucyate asti tāvat brahma nitya śuddha buddha mukta svabhāvam sarvajñam sarva śakti samanvitam brahma śabdasya hi vyutpādyamānasya nitya śuddha tvāt ayor athāḥ pratīyante bṛhateḥ dhātoḥ artha anugamāt sarvasya ātma tvāt ca brahma astitva prasiddhiḥ sarvaḥ  hi ātma astitvam pratyeti na na aham asmi iti yadi hi na ātma astitva prasiddhiḥ syāt  sarvaḥ  lokaḥ  na aham asmi iti pratīyāt  ātmā ca brahma yadi tarhi loke brahma ātma tvena prasiddham asti tatas  jñātam eva iti ajijñāsya tvam punar āpannam na tad viśeṣam prati vipratipatteḥ deha mātram caitanya viśiṣṭam ātmā iti prakṛtā janā laukāyatikāḥ ca pratipannāḥ indriyāṇi eva cetanāni ātmā iti apare mana iti anye vijñāna mātram kṣaṇikam iti eke śūnyam iti apare asti deha ādi vyatiriktaḥ saṃsārī kartā bhoktā iti apare bhoktā eva kevalam na kartā iti eke asti tad vyatirikta īśvaraḥ sarvajñaḥ sarva aktiḥ iti kecid  ātmā sa bhoktuḥ iti apare evam bahavaḥ  vipratipannā yukti vākya tad ābhāsa samāśrayāḥ santaḥ tatra avicārya yad kiñcit pratipadyamānaḥ  niḥśreyasāt pratihanyeta an artham ceyāt  tasmāt brahma jijñāsā upanyāsa mukhena vedānta vākya mīmāṃsā tad avirodhi tarka upakaraṇā niḥśreyasa prayojanā prastūyate janma utpattiḥ ādiḥ asya iti tad guṇa saṃvijñānaḥ  bahuvrīhiḥ janma sthiti bhaṅgam samāsa arthaḥ janmanaḥ ca ādi tvam śruti nirdeśa apekṣam vastu vṛtta apekṣam ca śruti nirdeśaḥ tāvat  ayataḥ  vā imāni bhūtāni jāyante iti asmin vākye janma sthiti pralayānām krama darśanāt  vastu vṛttam api janmanā labdha sattākasya dharmiṇaḥ sthiti prayasaṃbhavāt  asya iti pratyakṣa ādi saṃnidhāpitasya dharmiṇa idamā nirdeśaḥ ṣaṣṭhī janma ādi dharma saṃbandha arthā yata iti kāraṇa nirdeśaḥ asya jagataḥ  nāma rūpābhyām vyākṛtasya aneka kartṛ bhoktṛ saṃyuktasya pratiniyata deśa kāla nimitta kriyā phala āśrayasya manasā api acintya racanā rūpasya janma sthiti bhaṅgam yatas  sarvajñāt sarva śakteḥ kāraṇāt bhavati tad brahma iti vākya śeṣaḥ anyeṣām api bhāva vikārāṇām triṣu eva antarbhāva iti janma sthiti nāśānām iha grahaṇam yāska paripaṭhitānām tu ajāyate asti ityādīnām grahaṇe teṣām jagataḥ sthit kāle saṃbhāvyamāna tvāt mūla kāraṇāt utpatti sthiti nāśām jagataḥ  na gṛhītāḥ syuḥ iti āśaṅkyeta tad mā śaṅkī iti yā utpattiḥ brahmaḥ tatra eva sthitiḥ pralayaḥ ca ta eva gṛhyante na yathā ukta viśeṣaṇasya jagataḥ  yathā ukta viśeṣaṇam īśvaram muktvā anyatas  pradhānāt acetanāt aṇubhyaḥ  abhāvāt saṃsāriṇaḥ  vā utpatti ādi saṃbhāvayitum śakyam na ca svabhāvataḥ viśiṣṭa deśa kāla nimittānām iha upādānāt etad eva anumānam saṃsāri vyatirikta īśvara astitva ādi sādhanam manyanta īśvara kāraṇinaḥ nanu iha api tad eva upanyastam janma ādi sūtre na vedānta vākya kusuma grathana artha tvāt sūtrāṇām vedānta vākyāni hi sūtraiḥ udāhṛtya vicāryante vākya artha vicāraṇa adhyavasāna nivṛttā satsu tu vedānta vākyeṣu jagataḥ  janma ādi kāraṇa vādiṣu tad artha grahaṇa dārḍhāya anumānam api vedānta vākya avirodhi pramāṇam bhavat na nivāryate śrutyā eva ca sahāya tvena tarkasya abhyupeta tvāt tathā hi iti śrutiḥ apaṇḍitaḥ  medhāvī gandhārān eva upasaṃpadyeta evam eva iha ācāryavān puruṣaḥ  veda iti ca puruṣa buddhi sāhāyyam ātmanā ūr dāyati na dharma jijñāsāyām iva śruti ādayo anubhava ādayaḥ ca yathāsaṃbhavam iha pramāṇam anubhava avasāna tvāt bhūta vastu viṣaya tvāt ca brahma jñānasya kartavye hi viṣaye na anubhava apekṣā asti iti śruti ādīnām eva prāmāṇyam syāt puruṣa adhīna ātma lābha tvāt ca kartavyasya kartum akartum anyathā vā kartum śakyam laukikam vaidikam ca karma yathā aśvena gacchati padbhyām anyathā vā na vā gacchati iti tathā aatirātre ṣoḍaśinam gṛhṇāti na atirātre ṣoḍaśinam gṛhṇāti audite juhoti anudite juhoti iti vidhi pratiṣedhāḥ ca atra arthavantaḥ syuḥ vikalpa utsarga apavādāḥ ca na tu vastu evam na evam asti na asti iti vā vikalpyate vikalpanāḥ tu puruṣa buddhi apekṣāḥ na vastu yāthātmya jñānam puruṣa buddhi apekṣam kim tarhi vastu tantram eva tad  na hi sthāṇau  ekasmi sthāṇuḥ vā puruṣaḥ  anyaḥ  vā iti tattva jñānam bhavati tatra puruṣaḥ  anyaḥ  vā iti mithyājñānam sthāṇuḥ eva iti tattva jñānaṃvastu tantra tvāt evam bhūta vastu viṣayāṇām prāmāṇyam vastu tantram tatra evam sati brahma jñānam api vastu tantram eva bhūtavastu viṣaya tvāt  nanu bhūta vastu tve brahmaṇaḥ pramāṇa antara viṣaya tvam eva iti vedānta vākya vicāraṇa anarthikā eva prāptā na indriya aviṣaya tvena saṃbandha agrahaṇāt  svabhāvataḥ  viṣaya viṣayāṇi indriyāṇi na brahma viṣayāṇi sati hi indriya viṣaya tve brahmaṇa idam brahmaṇā saṃbaddham kāryam iti gṛhyeta kārya mātram eva tu gṛhyamāṇam kim brahmaṇā saṃbaddham kim anyena kenacid vā saṃbaddham iti na śakyam niścetum tasmā janma ādi sūtram na anumāna upanyāsa artham kim tarhi vedānta vākya prardāna artham kim punar tad vedānta vākyam yad sūtreṇa eha lila kṣayiṣitam abhṛguḥ vai vāruṇiḥ varuṇam pitaram upasasāra adhīhi bhagavaḥ  brahma iti iti upakramya tasya ca nirṇaya vākyam anyān ya api evan jātīyakāni vākyāni nitya aśuddha buddha mukta svabhāva sarvajña svarūpa kāraṇa viṣayāṇi udāhartavyāni mahata ṛgveda ādeḥ śāstrasya aneka vidyā sthāna upabṛṃhitasya pradīpavat sarva artha avadyotinaḥ sarvajña kalpasya yoniḥ kāraṇaṃbrahma na hi īdṛśasya śāstrasya ṛj veda ādi kṣaṇasya sarvajña guṇa anvitasya sarvajñāt anyatas  saṃbhavaḥ  asti yad yat vistara artham śāstram yasmāt puruṣa viśeṣāt saṃbhavati yathā vyākaraṇa ādi pāṇini ādeḥ jñeya eka deśa artham api sa tatas  api adhikatara vijñāna iti prasiddham loke kim u vaktavyam aneka śākhā bheda bhinnasya deva tiryak manuṣya varṇa āśrama dipravibhāga hetoḥ  ṛgveda ādi ākhyasya sarva jñāna ākarasya aprayatnena eva līlā nyayena puruṣa niḥśvāsavat yasmāt mahataḥ  bhūtādyoneḥ saṃbhavaḥ aasya mahataḥ  bhūtasya niḥśvasitam etad yadṛgvedaḥ ityādi śruteḥ tasya mahataḥ  bhūtasya niratiśayam sarvajña tvam sarva śaktimat tvam ca iti athavā yathā ukta ṛgveda ādi śāstram yoniḥ kāraṇam pramāṇam asya brahmaṇaḥ  yathāvat sva rūpa adhigame śāstrāt eva praṇāṇāt jagataḥ  janma ādi kāraṇam brahma adhigamyata iti abhiprāyaḥ śāstram udāhṛtam pūrva sūtre ityādi kimartham tarhi idam sūtram yāvatā pūrva sūtra eva evañjātīyakam śāstram udāha ratā śāstra yoni tvam brahmaṇaḥ  darśitam ucyate tatra pūrva sūtra akṣareṇa spaṣṭam śāstrasya anupādānāt janma ādi kevalam anumānam upanyastam iti āśaṅkyeta tām āśaṅkām nirvartayitum idam sūtram pravavṛte śāstra yoni tvāt iti yadyāna ātmā eva pradhānam sat śabda vācyam asa ātmā tad tvam asi iti iha upadiṣṭam syāt sa tad upadeśa śravaṇāt anātma jña tayā tad niṣṭhaḥ  mā bhūt iti mukhyam ātmānam upadidikṣuḥ tasya heya tvam brūyāt  yathā arundhatīm didarśayiṣuḥ tad samīpa sthām sthūlām tārām amukhyām prathamam arundhatiti grāhayitvā tām pratyākhyāya paścāt arundhatīm eva grāhayati tadvat na ayam ātmā iti brūyāt  na ca evam avocat  sat mātra ātmā avagati niṣṭhā eva hi ṣaṣṭha prapāṭhaka parisamāptiḥ dṛśyate caśabdaḥ pratijñā virodha abhyuccaya pradarśana arthaḥ sati api heya tva vacane pratijñā virodhaḥ prasajyeta kāraṇa vijñānāt hi sarvam vijñātam iti pratijñātam auta tam ādeśam aprākṣyaḥ  yena aśrutam śrutam bhavati amatam matam avijñātam vijñātam iti katham nu bhagavaḥ sa ādeśaḥ  bhavati iti yathā somya ekena mṛd piṇḍena sarvam mṛd mayam vijñātam syāt vācā ārambhaṇam vikāraḥ  nāmadheyam mṛttikā iti eva satyam aevam somya sa ādeśaḥ  bhavati iti vākya upakrame śravaṇāt  na ca sat śabda vācye pradhāne bhogya varga kāraṇe heya tvena āheya tvena vā vijñāte bhoktṛ vargaḥ  vijñātaḥ  bhavati apradhāna vikāra tvāt bhoktṛ vargasya tasmāt na pradhānam sat śabda vācyam kutas ca na pradhānam sat śabda vācyam tad eva sat śabda vācyam kāraṇam prakṛtya śrūyate iti eṣā śrutiḥ svapiti iti etad puruṣasya loka prasiddham nāma nirvakti sva śabdena iha ātmā ucyate yaḥ prakṛtaḥ sat śabda vācyaḥ tam apītaḥ  bhavati apigataḥ  bhavati iti arthaḥ apipūrvasya eteḥ larya artha tvam prasiddham prabhava apyayau  iti utpatti pralayayoḥ prayoga darśanāt  manaḥ pracāra upādhi viśeṣa saṃbandhāt indriya arthān gṛhyan  tad viśeṣa āpanno jīvaḥ  jāgarti tad vāsanā viśiṣṭaḥ svapnān paśyat manaḥ śabda vācyaḥ  bhavati sa upādhi dvaya uparame suṣupta avasthām upādhi kṛta viśeṣa abhāvāt sva ātmani pralīna iva iti asvam hi apītaḥ  bhavati iti ucyate yathā hṛdaya śabda nirvacanam śrutvā darśitam iti yathā vāśanāya udanyā śabda pravṛtti mūlam darśayati śrutiḥ ateja eva tad pītam nayante iti ca evam svam ātmānam sat śabda vācyam apītaḥ  bhavati iti imam artham svapiti nām nirvacanena darśayati na ca cetana ātma acetanam pradhānam svarūpa tvena pratipadyeta yadi punar  pradhānam eva ātmīyātvāt sva aśabdena eva ucyeta evam api cetano acetanam api eti iti viruddham āpadyeta śruti antaram ca iti suṣupta avasthāyām cetane api ayam darśayati atas  yasmin  apyayaḥ sarveṣām cetanānām tad cetanam sat śabda vācyam jagataḥ kāraṇam na pradhānam yadi tārkika samaya iva vedānteṣu api bhinnā kāraṇa avagatiḥ abhaviṣyat kvacid cetanam brahma jagataḥ kāraṇam dhvacid anyat eva iti tatas  kadācid pradhāna kāraṇa vāda anurodhena api īkṣati ādi śravaṇam akalpayiṣyat na tu etad asti samānā eva hi sarveṣu vedānteṣu cetana kāraṇa avagatiḥ ayatha agneḥ jvalataḥ sarvā diśaḥ  visphuliṅgā vipratiṣṭheran  evam eva etasmāt ātmanaḥ sarve prāṇā yathā āyatanam vipratiṣṭhante prāṇebhyaḥ  devāḥ  devebhyaḥ  lokāḥ iti atasmāt vā etasmāt ātmana ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ iti aātmata eva idam sarvam iti aātmana eṣa prāṇaḥ  jāyate iti ca ātmanaḥ kāraṇa tvam darśayanti sarve vedāntāḥ ātma śabdaḥ ca cetana vacana iti avocāma mahat ca prāmāṇya kāraṇam etad yad veda anta vākyānām cetana kāraṇa tve samāna gati tvam cakṣuḥ ādīnām iva rūpa ādiṣu atas  gati sāmānyāt sarvajñam brahma jagataḥ kāraṇam sva śabdena eva ca sarvajña īśvaraḥ  jagataḥ kāraṇam iti śrūyate śveta aśvatarāṇām mantra upaniṣadi sarvajñam īśvaram prakṛtya asa kāraṇam karaṇa adhipa adhipaḥ  na ca asya kaścid janitā na ca adhipaḥ iti tasmāt  sarvajñam brahma jagataḥ kāraṇam na acetanam pradhānam anyat vā iti siddham itas ca prācurya arthe mayaṭ  yasmāt ānanda hetu tvam brahmaṇaḥ  vyapadiśati śrutiḥ iti ānandayati iti arthaḥ yaḥ  hi anyān ānandayati sa pracura ānanda iti prasiddham bhavati yathā loke yaḥ  anyeṣām dhanika tvam āpādayati sa pracura dhana iti gamyate tadvat  tasmāt prācurya arthe api mayaṭaḥ saṃbhavāt ānanda mayaḥ para eva ātmā māntra varṇikam eva ca gīyate itas ca ānanda mayaḥ para eva ātmā yasmāt  abrahma vid āpnoti param iti upakramya asatyam jñānam anantam brahma iti asmin mantre yad prakṛtam brahma satya jñāna ananta viśeṣaṇaiḥ nirdharitam yasmāt ākāśa ādi krameṇa sthāvara jaṅgamāni bhūtāni ajāyanta yad ca bhūtāni sṛṣṭvā tāni anupraviśya guhāyām avasthitam sarva antaram yasya vijñānāya aanyaḥ  antara ātmā anyaḥ  antara ātmā iti prakrāntam tad māntra varṇikam eva brahma iha gīyate aanyaḥ  antara ātma ānanda mayaḥ iti mantra brāhmaṇayoḥ ca eka artha tvam yuktam avirodhāt  anyathā hi prakṛta hānā prakṛta prakriye syātām na ca anna maya ādibhya iva ānanda mayāt anyaḥ  antara ātmā abhidhīyate etad niṣṭhā eva ca asā eṣā bhārgavī vāruṇī vidyā tasmāt ānanda mayaḥ para eva ātmā itas ca ānanda mayaḥ para eva ātmā na itaraḥ itara īśvarāt anyaḥ saṃsārī jīva iti arthaḥ na jīva ānanda maya śabdena abhidhīyate kasmāt  anupapatteḥ ānanda mayam hi prakṛtya śrūyate kāmayata bahu syām prajāyeya iti sa tapaḥ  atapyata sa tapaḥ taptvā idaṃsarvam asṛjata yad idam kiñca iti tatra prāc śarīra ādi utpatteḥ abhidhyānam sṛjyamānānām ca vikārāṇām sraṣṭuḥ avyatirekaḥ sarva vikāra sṛṣṭiḥ ca na parasmāt ātmanaḥ  anyatra upapadyate bheda vyapadeśāt  ca itas ca na ānanda mayaḥ saṃsārī yasmāt ānanda maya adhikāre iti jīva ānanda mayau bhedena vyapadiśati na hi labdhā eva labdhavyaḥ  bhavati katham tarhi aātmā anveṣṭavyaḥ aātma lābhāt na param vidyate iti śruti smṛtī yāvatā na labdhā eva labdhavyaḥ  bhavati iti uktam bāḍham tathā api ātmanaḥ  apracyuta ātma bhāsya eva sataḥ ta tvānavabodha nimittaḥ  deha ādiṣu anātma sva ātma tva niścayaḥ  laukikaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ tena deha ādi bhūtasya ātmanaḥ  api ātmān anviṣṭo anveṣṭavyaḥ  alabdhaḥ  labdhavyaḥ  aśrutaḥ śrotavyaḥ  amataḥ  mantavyaḥ  avijñātaḥ  vijñātavya ityādi bheda vyapadeśa upapadyate pratiṣidhyata eva tu paramārthataḥ sarvajñāt parameśvarāt anyaḥ  draṣṭā śrotā vā anānyaḥ  atas  asti draṣṭā ityādinā parameśvaraḥ tu avidyā kalpitāt śarīrāt kartṛ bhoktṛ vijñāna ātmā ākhyāt anyaḥ yathā māyā vinaḥ carma khaḍga dharāt sūtreṇa ākāśam adhirohataḥ sa eva māyāvī parama artha rūpaḥ  bhūmiṣṭhaḥ  anyaḥ yathāvā dhaṭa ākāśāt upādhi paricchinnāt anupādhiḥ aparicchinna ākāśaḥ  anyaḥ īdṛśam ca vijñāna ātma paramātma bhedam āśritya anetaraḥ  anupapatteḥ abheda vyapadeśāt ca iti uktam ānanda maya adhikāre ca asaḥ  akāmayata bahusyām prajāyeya iti kāmayitṛ tva nirdeśāt na anumānikam api sāṃkhya parikalpitam acetanam pradhānam ānanda maya tvena kāraṇa tvena vā apekṣitavyam aīkṣateḥ na aśabdam iti nirākṛtam api pradhānam pūrva sūtra udāhṛtām kāmayitṛ tva śrutim āśritya prasaṅgāt punar nirākriyate gati sāmānya prapañcanāya asmin   asya ca tad yogam śāsti itas ca na pradhāne jīve vā ānanda maya śabdaḥ yasmāt asmin  ānanda maye prakṛta ātmani pratibuddhasya asya jīvasya tad yogam śāsti tad ātmanā yogaḥ tad yogaḥ tad bhāva āpattiḥ muktiḥ iti arthaḥ tad yogam śāsti śāstram na ātmye anirukte anilayane abhayam pratiṣṭhām vindate atha saḥ  abhayam gataḥ  bhavati yadā hi eva eṣa etasmin  udaram antaram kurute atha tasya bhayam bhavati iti etad uktam bhavati idam āmananti iti tatra saṃśayaḥ kim ākāśa śabdena param brahma abhidhīyata uta bhūtākāśam iti kutas  saṃśayaḥ ubhayatra prayoga darśanāt  bhūta viśeṣe tāvat su prasiddhaḥ  loka vedayoḥ ākāśa śabdaḥ brahmaṇi api kvacid prayujyamānaḥ  dṛśyate yatra vākya śeṣa vaśāt asādhāraṇa śravaṇāt vā nirdhāritam brahma bhavati yathā iti aākāśaḥ  vai nāma nāma rūpayoḥ nirvahitā te yad antarā tad brahma iti ca evamādau atas  saṃśayaḥ kim punar atra yuktam bhūtākāśam iti kutas  tad hi prasiddhatareṇa prayogeṇa śīghram buddhim ārohati naca ayam ākāśa śabda ubhayoḥ sādhāraṇaḥ śakyaḥ  vijñātum aneka artha tva prasaṅgāt  tasmāt brahmaṇi gauṇa ākāśa śabdaḥ  bhavitum arhati vibhu tva ādibhiḥ hi bahubhiḥ dharmaiḥ sadṛśam ākāśena brahma bhavati na ca mukhya saṃbhave gauṇoḥ atho grahaṇam arhati saṃbhavati ca iha mukhyasya eva ākāśasya grahaṇam nanu bhūta ākāśa parigrahe vākya śeṣaḥ  na upapadyate ityādiḥ na eṣa doṣaḥ bhūta ākāśasya api vāyu ādi krameṇa kāraṇatva upapatteḥ vijñāyate hi ityādi jyāyaḥ tu aparāyaṇa tve api bhūta antara apekṣayā upapadyete bhūta ākāśasya api tasmāt ākāśa śabdena bhūta ākāśasya grahaṇam iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ ākāśa śabdena brahmaṇaḥ  grahaṇam yuktam kutas  tad liṅgāt  parasya hi brahmaṇa idam liṅgam iti parasmāt hi brahmaṇaḥ  bhūtānām utpattiḥ iti vedānteṣu maryādā nanu bhūta ākāśasya api vāyu ādi krameṇa kāraṇa tvam darśitam satyam darśitam tathā api mula kāraṇasya brahmaṇaḥ  aparigrahāt ākāśāt eva iti avadhāraṇam sarvāṇi iti ca bhūta viśeṣaṇam na anukūlam syāt  tathā aākāśam pratyastam yanti iti brahma liṅgam aākāśaḥ  hi eva ebhyaḥ  jyāyān ākāśaḥ parāyaṇam iti ca jyāyaḥ tu aparāyaṇa tve jyāyaḥ tvam hi ānāpekṣikam paramātmani eva ekasmin  āmnātam iti tathā parāyaṇa tvam api parama kāraṇa tvāt paramātmani eva upapannataram śrutiḥ ca bhavati iti api ca antavat tva doṣeṇa śālāvatyasya pakṣam ninditvā anantam kiñcid vaktu kāmena jaivalinā ākāśaḥ parigṛhītaḥ tam ca ākāśa mudgīthe saṃpādya upasaṃharati nantaḥ iti tad ca ānantyam brahma liṅgam yad punaruktam bhūta ākāśam prasiddhi balena prathamataram pratīyata iti atra brūmaḥ prathamataram pratītam api sat  vākya śeṣa gatān brahma guṇān dṛṣṭvā na parigṛhyate darśitaḥ ca brahmaṇi api ākāśa śabdaḥ iti ādau tathā ākāśa paryāya vācinām api brahmaṇi prayogaḥ  dṛśyate asā eṣā bhārgavī vāruṇī vidyā parame vyoman pratiṣṭhitā aom kam brahma khaṃbrahma akham purāṇam iti ca evamādau vākya upakrame api vartamānasya ākāśa śabdasya vākya śeṣa vaśāt yuktā brahma viṣaya tva avadhāraṇā aagniḥ adhīte anuvākam iti hi vākya upakrama gataḥ  api agni śabdaḥ  māṇavaka viṣayaḥ  dṛśyate tasmāt ākāśa śabdam brahma iti siddham udgīthe iti upakramya śrūyate katamā sā devatā iti prāṇā iti ha uvāca sarvāṇi ha vā imāni bhūtāni prāṇam eva abhisaṃviśanti prāṇam abhyujjihate sā eṣā devatā prastāvam anvāyattā iti tatra saṃśaya nirṇayau pūrvavat eva draṣṭavyau aprāṇa bandhanam hi somya manaḥ aprāṇasya prāṇam iti ca evamādau brahma viṣayaḥ prāṇa śabdaḥ  dṛśyate vāyu vikāre tu prasiddha taraḥ  loka vedayoḥ ata iha prāṇa śabdena katarasya upādānam yuktam iti bhavati saṃśayaḥ kim punar atra yuktam vāyu vikārasya pañca vṛtteḥ prāṇasya upādānam yuktam tatra hi prasiddhataraḥ prāṇa śabda iti avocāma nanu pūrvavat iha api tad liṅgāt brahmaṇa eva grahaṇam yuktam iha api vākya śeṣe bhūtānām saṃveśana udgamanam pārameśvaram karma pratīyate na mukhyaḥ  api prāṇe bhūta saṃveśana udgamanasya darśanāt  evam hyāmnāyate iti pratyakṣam ca etad svāpa kāle prāṇa vṛttau  aparilupyamānāyām indriya vṛttayaḥ parilupyante prabodha kāle ca prādurbhavanti iti indriya sāra tvāt ca bhūtānām aviruddhaḥ  mukhye prāṇe api bhūta saṃveśana udgama na vādī vākya śeṣaḥ apicā ādityaḥ  annam ca udgītha pratihārayoḥ devate prastāva devatāyāḥ prāṇasi antaram nirdiśyete na ca tayoḥ brahma tvam asti tad sāmānyāt ca prāṇasya api na brahma tvam iti evam prāpte sūtrakāra āha iti atad liṅgāt iti pūrva sūtre nirdiṣṭam ata eva tad liṅgāt prāṇa śabdam api param brahma bhavitum arhati prāṇasya api hi brahma liṅga saṃbandhaḥ śrūyate iti prāṇa nimittau sarveṣām bhūtānām utpatti pralayau  ucyamānau prāṇasya brahma tām gamayataḥ nanu uktam mukhya prāṇa parigrahe api saṃveśana ud gamana darśanam aviruddham svāpa prabodhayoḥ darśanāt iti atra ucyate svāpa prabodhayoḥ indriyāṇām eva kevalānām prāṇa āśrayam saṃveśana udgamanam dṛśyate na sarveṣām bhūtānām ihatu sa indriyāṇām sa śarīrāṇām ca jīva āviṣṭānām bhūtānām asarvāṇi ha vā imāni bhūtāni iti śruteḥ yadā api bhūta śrutiḥ mahābhūta viṣayā parigṛhyate tadā api brahma liṅga tvam aviruddham nanu saha api viṣayaiḥ indriyāṇām svāpa prabodhayoḥ prāṇe api ayam prāṇāt ca prabhavam śṛṇumaḥ iti tatra api tad liṅgāt prāṇa śabdam brahmā eva yad punar anna āditya saṃnidhānāt prāṇasya abrahma tvam iti tad ayuktam vākya śeṣa balena prāṇa śabdasya brahma viṣaya tām pratīyamānāyām saṃnidhānasya akiñcitkara tvāt yad punar  prāṇa śabdasya pañca vṛttau prasiddhatara tvam tad ākāśa śabdasya iva pratividheyam tasmāt siddham prastāva devatāyāḥ prāṇasya brahma tvam atra kecid udāharanti aprāṇa bandhanam hi somya manaḥ iti ca tad ayuktam śabda bhedāt prakaraṇāt ca saṃśaya anupapatteḥ yathā pituḥ pitā iti prayoge anyaḥ pitā ṣaṣṭī nirdiṣṭaḥ  anyaḥ prathama anirdiṣṭaḥ pituḥ pitā iti gamyate tadvat  aprāṇasya prāṇam iti śabda bhedāt prasiddhāt prāṇāt anyaḥ prāṇasya prāṇa iti niścīyate na hi sa eva tasya iti bheda nirdeśa arhe bhavati yasya ca prakaraṇe yaḥ  nirdiśyate nāma antareṇa api sa eva tatra prakaraṇī nirdiṣṭa iti gamyate yathā jyotiṣṭoma adhikāre iti atra jyotiḥ śabdaḥ  jyotiṣṭoma viṣayaḥ  bhavati tathā parasya brahmaṇaḥ prakaraṇe aprāṇa bandhanam hi somya manaḥ iti śrutaḥ prāṇa śabdaḥ  vāyu vikāra mātram katham avagamayet  atas  saṃśaya viṣaya tvāt na etad udāharaṇam yuktam prastāva devatāyām tu prāṇe saṃśaya pūrva pakṣa nirṇayā upapāditāḥ idam āmananti iti tatra saṃśayaḥ kim iha jyotiḥ śabdena āt ityādi jyotiḥ abhidhīyate kiṃvā paramātmā iti artha antara viṣayasya api śabdasya tad liṅgāt abrahma viṣaya tvam uktam iha tu tad liṅgam eva asti na asti iti vicāryate kim tāvat prāptam āditya ādikam eva jyotiḥ śabdena parigṛhyata iti kutas  prasiddheḥ tamaḥ  jyotiḥ iti hi imau śabdau paraspara pratidvandvī vīṣayau prasiddhau cakṣuḥ vṛtteḥ nirodhakam śārvara ādikam tama ucyate tasyāḥ  eva anugrāhakam āditya ādikam jyotiḥ tathā adīpyate iti iyam api śrutiḥ āditya ādi viṣayā prasiddhā na hi rūpa ādi hīnam brahma adīpyate iti mukhyām śrutiḥ mahati dyu maryāda tva śruteḥ ca na hi carācara bījasya brahmaṇaḥ sarva ātmakasya dyauḥ maryādā yuktā kāryasya tu jyotiṣaḥ paricchinnasya dyauḥ maryādā syāt  aparaḥ  divaḥ  jyotiḥ iti ca brāhmaṇam nanu kāryasya api jyotiṣaḥ sarvatra gamyamāna tvāt dyumaryādāvat tvam asamañjasam astu tarhi atrivṛt kṛtam tejaḥ prathama jam na atrivṛt kṛtasya tejasaḥ prayojana abhāvāt iti idam eva prayojanam yad upāsya tvam iti ced  na prayojana antara prayuktasya eva āditya deḥ upāsya tva darśanāt atāsām trivṛtam trivṛtam ekaikām karavāṇi iti ca aviśeṣa śruteḥ naca atrivṛt kṛtasya api tejasaḥ  dyu maryāda tvam prasiddham astu tarhi trivṛt kṛtam evat tejaḥ  jyotiḥ śabdam nanu uktam arvāk api divaḥ  avagamyate agni ādikam jyotiḥ iti na eṣa doṣaḥ sarvatra api gamyamānasya jyotiṣaḥ aparaḥ  divaḥ iti upāsana arthaḥ pradeśa viśeṣa parigrahaḥ  na virudhyate na tu niṣpradeśasya api brahmaṇaḥ pradeśa viśeṣa kalpanā bhāginī asarvatas pṛṣṭeṣu anuttameṣu uttameṣu loka iṣu iti ca ādhāra bahutva śrutiḥ kārye jyotiṣi upapadyatetarām aidam vāva tad yad idam asmin  āntar  puruṣe jyotiḥ iti ca kaukṣeye jyotiḥ aṣi param jyotiḥ adhyasyamānam dṛśyate sārūpya nimittāḥ ca adhyasā bhavanti yathā iti kaukṣeyasya tu jyotiṣaḥ prasiddham abrahma tvam atasya eṣā dṛṣṭiḥ atasya eṣā śrutiḥ iti ca auṣṇya ghoṣa viśiṣṭa tvasya śravaṇāt  atat etad dṛṣṭam ca śrutam cepi upāsīta iti ca śruteḥ acakṣuṣyaḥ śrutaḥ  bhavati ya evam veda iti ca alpa phala śravaṇāt abrahma tvam mahate hi phalāya brahma upāsanam iṣyate na ca anyat api kiñcid sva vākye prāṇa ākāśavat jyotiṣaḥ  asti brahma liṅgam na ca pūrvasmin  api vākye brahma nirdiṣṭam asti agāyatrī vā idam sarvam bhūtam iti chandaḥ nirdeśāt  atha api kathañcid pūrvasmin vākye brahma nirdiṣṭam syāt evam api na tasya iha pratyabhijñānam asti tatra hi atripādasya amṛtam divi iti dyauḥ adhikaraṇa tvena śrūyate atra punar  aparaḥ  divaḥ  jyotiḥ iti dyauḥ maryādā tvena tasmāt prākṛtam jyotiḥ iha grāhyam iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ jyotiḥ iha brahma grāhyam kutas  caraṇa abhidhānāt pāda abhidhānāt iti arthaḥ pūrvasmin hi vākye catuṣpād brahma nirdiṣṭam sya sarvā bhūtāni tripādasya amṛtam divi iti anena mantreṇa tatra yad catuṣpādaḥ  brahmaṇaḥ tri pāda mṛtam dyu saṃbandhi rūpam nirdiṣṭam tad eva iha dyu saṃbandhāt nirdiṣṭam iti pratyabhijñāyate tad parityajya prākṛtam jyotiḥ kalpayataḥ prakṛta hānā prakṛta prakriye prasajyeyātām na kevalam pūrva vākyāt jyotiḥ vākya eva brahma anuvṛttiḥ parasyām api śāṇḍilya vidyayām anuvartiṣyate brahma tasmāt iha jyotiḥ iti brahma pratipattavyam yad tu uktam iti ca etau śabdau kārye jyotiṣi prasiddhau  iti na ayam doṣaḥ prakaraṇāt brahma avagame sati anayoḥ śabdayoḥ aviśeṣaka tvāt  dīpyamāna kārya jyotiḥ upalakṣite brahmaṇi api prayoga saṃbhavāt  ayena sūryaḥ tapati tejasā it dhaḥ iti ca mantra varṇāt  yad vā na ayam jyotiḥ śabdaḥ cakṣuḥ vṛtteḥ eva anugrāhake tejasi vartate anyatra api prayoga darśanāt  avācā eva ayam jyotiṣāḥ te amanaḥ  jyotiḥ juṣatām iti ca tasmāt yad yat kasyacid avabhāsakam tad tajyotiḥ śabdena abhidhīyate tathā sati brahmaṇaḥ  api caitanya rūpasya samasta jagat avabhāsa hetu tvāt upapannaḥ  jyotiḥ śabdaḥ atam eva bhāntam anubhāti sarvam tasya bhāsā sarvam idam vibhāti atad devā jyotiṣām jyotiḥ āyuḥ hepa āsate amṛtam ityādi śrutibhyaḥ ca yad api uktam dyu maryāda tvam sarva gatasya brahmaṇaḥ  na upapadyata iti atra ucyate sarva gatasya api brahmaṇa upāsana arthaḥ pradeśa viśeṣa parigrahaḥ  na virudhyate nanuktam niṣpradeśasya brahmaṇaḥ pradeśa viśeṣa kalpanā na upapadyata iti na ayam doṣaḥ niṣpradeśasya api brahmaṇa upādhi viśeṣa saṃbandhāt pradeśa viśeṣa kalpanā upapatteḥ tathā hi ādityaḥ  cakṣuṣi hṛdaye iti pradeśa viśeṣa saṃbandhāni brahmaṇa upāsanāni śrūyante etena aviśvatas pṛṣṭhā iṣu iti ādhāra bahu tvam upapāditam yad api etad uktam auṣṇya ghoṣa anumite kaukṣeye kārye jyotiṣyadhi asyamāna tvāt param api divaḥ kāryam jyotiḥ eva iti tad api ayuktam parasya api brahṇaṇaḥ  nāma ādi pratīka tvat kaukṣeya jyotiṣpratīka tva upapatteḥ adṛṣṭam ca śrutam ca iti upāsīta iti tu pratīka dvārakam dṛṣṭa tvam śruta tvam ca bhaviṣyati yad api alpa phala śravaṇāt na brahma iti tad api anupapannam nahīyate phalāya brahma āśrayaṇīyam iyate na iti niyama hetuḥ asti yatra hi nirasta sarva viśeṣa saṃbandham param brahma ātma tvena upadiśyate tatra eka rūpam eva phalam mokṣa iti avagamyate yatra tu guṇa viśeṣa saṃbandham pratīka viśeṣa saṃbandham vā brahma upadiśyate tatra saṃsāra gocarāṇi eva uccāvacāni phalāni dṛśyante ityādyāsu śrutiṣu yadi api na sva vākye kiñcid jyotiṣaḥ  brahma liṅgam asti tathā api pūrvasmin vākye dṛśyamānam grahītavyam bhavati tad uktam sūtrakāreṇa iti katham punar vākya antara gatena brahma saṃnidhānena jyotiḥśrutiḥ sva viṣayāt śakyā pracyāvayitum na eṣa doṣaḥ ayadataḥ paraḥ  jyotiḥ iti prathamatara paṭhitena yad śabdena sarva nāmnā dyusaṃbnandhāt pratyabhijñāyamāne pūrva vākya nirdiṣṭe brahmaṇi sva sāmārthyena parāmṛṣṭe satyarthāt jyotiḥ śabdasya api brahma viṣaya tva upapatteḥ tasmāt iha jyotiḥ iti brahma pratipattavyam atha yad uktam pūrvasmin  api vākye na brahma bhihitam iti agāyatrī vā idam sarvam bhūtam yad idam kiñca iti gāyatrī ākhyasya chandasaḥ  abhihita tvāt iti tad parihartavyam katham punar chandobhidhānāt na brahma abhihitam iti śakyate vaktum yāvatā atāvān asya mahimā iti etasyāmṛci catuṣpād brahma darśitam na etad asti agāyatrī vā idam sarvam iti gāyatrīm upakramya tām eva bhūta pṛthivī śarīra hṛdaya vākya pramāṇa bhedaiḥ vyakhyāya asā eṣā catuṣpādā ṣaḍvidhā gāyatrī tad etad ṛca abhyanuktam tāvān asya mahimā iti tasyām eva vyākhyāta rūpāyām gāyatryām udāhṛtaḥ  mantraḥ katham akasmāt brahma catuṣpād abhidadhyāt  yaḥ  api tatra ayat vai tad brahma iti brahma śabdaḥ saḥ  api chandasaḥ prakṛta tvāt chandaḥ viṣaya eva aya etām evam brahma upaniṣadam veda iti atra hi veda upaniṣadam iti vyācakṣate tasmāt chandaḥ bhidhānāt na brahmaṇaḥ prakṛta tvam iticed  na eṣa doṣaḥ atathā cetorpaṇa nigahāt tathā gāyatrī ākhya  chanda udvāreṇa tad anugate brahmaṇi cetasoḥ apaṇam citta samādhānam anena brahmaṇa vākyena nigadyate iti na hi akṣara saṃniveśa mātrāyāḥ  gāyatryāḥ sarva ātmaka tvam saṃbhavati tasmāt yāt gāyatri ākhya vikāre anugatam jagat kāraṇam brahma tad iha sarvam iti ucyate yathā asarvam khalu idam brahma iti kāryam ca kāraṇāt avyatiriktam iti vakṣyāmaḥ iti atra tathā anyatra api vikāra dvāreṇa brahmaṇa upāsanam dṛśyate iti tasmāt asti chandobhidhāne api pūrvasmin vākye catuṣpād brahma nirdiṣṭam tad eva jyotiḥ vākye api parāmṛśyata upāsana antara vidhānāya apara āha sākṣāt eva gāyatrī śabdena brahma pratipādyate saṃkhyā sāmānyāt  yathā gāyatrī catuṣpadā ṣaṣ akṣaraiḥ pādaiḥ tathā brahma catuṣpād  tathā anyatra api chandobhidhāyī śabdoḥ atha antare saṃkhyā sāmānyāt prayujyamānaḥ  dṛśyate tad yathā iti upakramya āha asā eṣā virāḍan  ādi iti asmin pakṣe brahma eva abhihitam iti na chandobhidhānam sarvathā api asti pūrvasmin vākye prakṛtam brahma itas ca evam abhyupagantavyam iti pūrvasmin vākye prakṛtam brahma iti yatas  bhūta ādīn pādān vyapadiśati bhūta pṛthivī śarīra hṛdayāni hi nirdiśi āha iti na hi brahma an āśrayaṇe kevalasya chandasaḥ  bhūta ādayaḥ pādā upapadyante apica brahma an āśrayaṇe na iyam ṛksaṃbodhyeta iti anayā hi ṛcā svarasena brahma eva abhidhīyate apādaḥ  asya sarvā bhūtāni tripādasya amṛtam divi iti sarva ātma tva upapatteḥ puruṣasūkte api iyam ṛc brahma para tayā eva samāmnāyate smṛtiḥ ca brahmaṇa evaṃrūpa tām darśayati iti ayat vai tad brahma iti ca nirdeśa evam sati mukhya artha upapadyate apañca brahma puruṣāḥ iti ca hṛdaya suṣiṣu brahma puruṣa śrutiḥ brahma saṃbandhi tāyām vivakṣitāyām saṃbhavati tasmāt asti pūrvasmin vākye brahma prakṛtam tad eva brahma jyotiḥ vākye dyu saṃbandhāt pratyabhijñāyamānam parāmṛśyata iti sthitam yad api etad uktam pūrvatra iti saptamyā dyauḥ ādhāra tvena upadiṣṭā iti punar  aatha yad atas  paraḥ  divaḥ iti pañcamyā maryādā tvena tasmāt upadeśa bhedān na tasya iha pratyabhijñānam asti tad parihartavyam atra ucyate na ayam doṣaḥ ubhayasmin  api avirodhāt ubhayasmin  api saptamyante pañcamyante ca upadeśe na pratyabhijñānam virudhyate yathā loke vṛkṣa agra saṃbaddhaḥ  api śyena ubhayathā upadiśyamānaḥ  dṛśyate vṛkṣa agre śyenaḥ  vṛkṣa agrāt paratas  śyena iti ca evam divi ā iva sat brahma divaḥ param iti upadiśyate apara āha yathā loke vṛkṣa agreṇa asaṃbaddhaḥ  api śyena ubhayathā upadiśyamānaḥ  dṛśyate vṛkṣa agre śyenaḥ  vṛkṣa agrāt puratas  śyena iti ca evam ca divaḥ param api sat brahma divi iti upadiśyate tasmāt asti pūrva nirdiṣṭasya brahmaṇa iha pratyabhijñānam atas  param eva brahma jyotiḥ śabdam iti siddham pratardana adhikaraṇam sū prāṇa s tathā anugamāt asti kauṣītaki brāhmaṇa upaniṣadi indra pratardana ākhyāyikā iti ārabhya āmnātā tasyām śrūyate smi prajñā ātmā tam mām āyuḥ amṛtam iti upāḥsva iti tathā uttaratra api aatha khalu prāṇa eva prajñā ātmā idam śarīram parigṛhya utthāpayati iti tathā ana vācam vijijñāsīta vaktāram vidyāt ityādi ante ca asa eṣa prāṇa eva prajñā ātma ānandaḥ  ajaraḥ  amṛtaḥ ityādi tatra saṃśayaḥ kim iha prāṇa śabdena vāyu mātram abhidhīyata upa devatā ātmā iti jīvaḥ  athavā param brahma iti nanu aata eva prāṇaḥ iti atra varṇitam prāṇa śabdasya brahma paratvam iha api ca brahma liṅgam asti jaraḥ  amṛtaḥ ityādi katham iha punar  saṃśayaḥ saṃbhavati aneka liṅga darśanāt iti brūmaḥ na kevalam iha brahma liṅgam eva upalabhyate santi hi itara liṅgāni api amām eva vijānīhi iti indrasya vacanam devatā ātma liṅgam idam śarīram parigṛhya utthāpayati iti prāṇa liṅgam ana vācam vijijñāsīta vaktāram vidyāt ityādi jīva liṅgam ata upapannaḥ saṃśayaḥ tatra prasiddheḥ vāyuḥ prāṇa iti prāpta ucyate prāṇa śabdam brahma vijñeyam kutas  tathā anugamāt tathā hi paurvāparyeṇa paryalocyamāne vākye padārthānām samanvayaḥ  brahma pratipādana para upalabhyate upakrame tāvat  avaram vṛṇīṣva iti indreṇa uktaḥ pratardanaḥ paramam puruṣa artham varam upacikṣepa iti tasmai hitatama tvena upadiśyamānaḥ prāṇaḥ katham paramātmā na syāt  na hi anyatra paramātma jñānāt hitatama prāptiḥ asti atam eva viditvā atimṛtyum eti na anyaḥ panthā vidyate ayanāya ityādi śrutibhyaḥ tathā asa yaḥ  mām veda na ha vai tasya kenacana karmaṇā lokaḥ  mīyate na steyena na bhrūṇahatyayā ityādi ca brahma parigrahe ghaṭate brahma vijñānena hi sarva karma kṣayaḥ prasiddhaḥ ityādyāsu śrutiṣu prajñā ātma tvam ca brahma pakṣa eva upapadyate na hi acetanasya vāyoḥ prajñā ātma tvam saṃbhavati tathā upasaṃhāre api aānandaḥ  ajaraḥ  amṛtaḥ iti ānanda tva ādīni na brahmaṇaḥ  anyatra samyak  saṃbhavati asa na sādhunā karmaṇā bhūyān bhavati no eva asādhunā karmaṇā kanīyān eṣa hi eva sādhu karma kārayati tam yamebhyaḥ  lokasya unninīṣate eṣa u bhava asādhu karma kārayati tam yamebhyaḥ  lokebhyaḥ  adhas  ninīṣate iti aeṣa loka adhipatiḥ eṣa lokeśaḥ iti ca sarvam etad parasmaninbrahmaṇi āśrīyamāṇe anugantum śakyate na mukhye prāṇe tasmāt prāṇaḥ  brahma yad uktam prāṇaḥ  brahma iti tad ā ākṣipyate na param brahma prāṇa śabdam kasmāt  vaktuḥ ātma upadeśāt vaktā hi indraḥ  nāma kaścid vigrahavān devatā viśeṣaḥ svam ātmānam pratardanāya ācacakṣe iti upakramya aprāṇaḥ  asmi prajñā ātmā iti ahaṅkāra vādena sa eṣa vaktuḥ ātma tvena upadiśyamānaḥ prāṇaḥ katham brahma syāt  na hi brahmaṇaḥ  vaktṛ tvam saṃbhavati aava āgamanāḥ ityādi śrutibhyaḥ tathā vigraha saṃbandhibhiḥ eva brahmaṇi asaṃbhavadbhiḥ dharmaiḥ ātmānam tuṣṭāva iti evamādibhiḥ prāṇa tvam ca indrasya balava tvāt upapadyate aprāṇaḥ  vai balam iti hi vijñāyate balasya ca indraḥ  devatā prasiddhā ayā ca kācid bala kṛtiḥ indra karma eva ta diti hi vadanti prajñā ātma tvam api apratihata jñāna tvāt devatā ātmanaḥ saṃbhavati apratihata jñānā devatā iti hi vadanti niścite ca evam devatā ātma upadeśe hitatama tva ādi vacanāni yathāsaṃbhavam tad viṣayāṇi eva yojayitavyāni tasmāt uktuḥ indrasya ātma upadeśāt na prāṇaḥ  brahma iti ākṣipya pratisamādhīyate iti adhyātma saṃbandhaḥ pratyagātma saṃbandhasya bhūmā bāhulī asmin  adhyāya upalabhyate ayāvat hi asmin sarīre prāṇaḥ  vasati tāvat āyuḥ iti prāṇasya eva prajñā ātmanaḥ pratyak bhūtasya āyuṣya pradhāna upasaṃhārayoḥ svātantryam darśayati na devatā viśeṣasya parācīnasya tathā astitve ca prāṇānām niḥśreyasam iti adhyātmam eva indriya āśrayam prāṇam darśayati tathā aprāṇa eva prajñā ātmā idam śarīram parigṛhya utthāpayati iti ana vācam vijijñāsīta vaktāram vidyāt iti cepa kramya atat yathā rathasya āreṣu nemiḥ arpitā nābhāvarā arpitā evam eva etā bhūtamātrāḥ prajñāmātrāsu arpitāḥ prajñāmātrāḥ prāṇe arpitāḥ sa eṣa prāṇa eva prajñā ātma ānandaḥ  ajaraḥ  amṛtaḥ iti viṣaya undriya vyavahāra an abhibhūtam pratyak ātmānam eva upasaṃharati asa ma ātmā iti vidyāt iti ca upasaṃhāraḥ pratyagātma parigrahe sādhuḥ na parācīna parigrahe aayam ātmā brahma sarva anabhūḥ iti ca śruti antaram tasmāt adhyātma saṃbandha bāhulyāt brahma upadeśa eva ayam na devatā ātma upadeśaḥ katham tarhi vaktuḥ ātma upadeśaḥ indraḥ  nāma devatā ātmānam svam ātmānam paramātma tvena aham eva param brahma iti ārṣeṇa darśanena yathāśāstram paśyan  upadiśati sma iti yathā ataddhā etad paśyan  ṛṣiḥ vāmadevaḥ pratipede aham manuḥ abhavam sūryaḥ ca iti tadvat  atadyaḥ  yaḥ  devānām pratyabudhyata sa eva tad abhavat iti śruteḥ yad punaruktam amām eva vijānīhi iti uktvā vigraha dharmaiḥ indra ātmānam tuṣṭāva tvāṣṭra vadha ādibhiḥ iti tad parihartavyam atra ucyate na tvāṣṭra vadha ādīnām vijñeya indra stuti artha tvena upanyāsaḥ  yasmāt evaṅkarma aham tasmāt mām vijānīhi iti katham tarhi vijñāna stuti artha tvena yad kāraṇam tvāṣṭra vadha ādīni sāhasāni upanyasya pareṇa vijñāna stutim anusaṃdadhāti ityādinā etad uktam bhavati yadi api adhyātma saṃbandha bhūma darśanāt na parācīnasya devatā ātmana upadeśaḥ tathā api na brahma vākyam bhavitum arhati kutas  jīva liṅgān mukhya prāṇa liṅgāt ca jīvasya tāvat asmin vākye vispaṣṭam liṅgam upalabhyate ana vācam vijijñāsīta vaktāram vidyāt ityādi atra hi vāc ādibhiḥ karaṇaiḥ vyāpṛtasya kārya karaṇa adhyakṣasya jīvasya vijñeya tvam abhidhīyate tathā mukhya prāṇa liṅgam api iti śarīra dhāraṇam ca mukhya prāṇasya dharmaḥ prāṇa saṃvāde vāc ādīn prāṇān prakṛtya iti śravaṇāt  ye tu imam śarīram parigṛhya iti paṭhanti teṣām imam jīvam indriya grāmam vā parigṛhya śarīram utthāpayati iti vyākhyeyam prajñā ātma tvam api jīve tāvat cetana tvāt upapannam mukhye api prāṇe prajñā sādhana prāṇa antara āśraya tvāt upapannam eva jīva mukhya prāṇa parigrahe ca prāṇa prajñā ātmanoḥ saha vṛtti tvena abheda nirdeśaḥ sva rūpeṇa ca bheda nirdeśa iti ubhayayā nirdeśa upapadyate iti brahma parigrahe tu kim kasmad bhidyeta tasmāt ihajīva mukhya prāṇayoḥ antara ubhau vā pratīyeyātām na brahma iti ced  na etad evam upāsā tra evidyāt evam sati trividham upāsanam prasajyeta jīva upāsane mukhya prāṇa upāsanam brahma upāsanam ca iti naca etad ekasmin vākye abhyupagantum yuktam upakrama upasaṃhārābhyām hi vākya eka tvam avagamyate amām eva vijānīhi iti upakramya aprāṇaḥ  asmi prajñā ātmā tam mām āyuḥ amṛtam iti upāḥsva iti uktvā ante asa eṣa prāṇa eva prajñā ātma ānandaḥ  ajaraḥ  amṛtaḥ iti eka rūpau  upakrama upasaṃhārau dṛśyete tatra artha eka tvam yuktam āśrayitum na ca brahma liṅgam anya paratvena pariṇetum śakyam daśānām bhūta mātrāṇām prajñāmātrāṇām ca brahmaṇaḥ  anyatra arpaṇa anupapatteḥ āśrita tāvāt ca anyatra api brahma liṅga vaśāt prāṇa śabdasya brahmaṇi vṛtteḥ iha api ca hitatama upanyāsa ādi brahma liṅga yogāt brahma upadeśa eva ayam iti gamyate yad tu mukhya prāṇa liṅgam darśitam iti tad asat  prāṇa vyāpārasya api paramātmā āyattatvāt paramātmani upacaritum śakya tvāt  ana prāṇena na apānena martyaḥ  jīvati kaścana itareṇa tu jīvanti yasmin  etau  upāśritau iti śruteḥ yad api na vācam vijijñāsīta vaktāram vidyāt  ityādi jīva liṅgam darśitam tad api na brahma pakṣam nivārayati na hi jīvaḥ  nāma atyanta bhinno brahmaṇaḥ atattvam asi aaham brahmā asmi ityādi śrutibhyaḥ buddhi ādi upādhi kṛtam tu viśeṣam āśritya brahmā eva sañjīvaḥ kartā bhoktā ca iti ucyate tasya upādhi kṛta viśeṣa parityāgena svarūpam brahma darśayitum ana vācam vijijñāsīta vaktāram vidyāt ityādinā pratyagātmā abhimukhīkaraṇa artham upadeśaḥ  na virudhyate ayat vācā anabhyuditam yena vāc abhyudyate tad eva brahma tvam viddhi na idam yad idam upāsate ityādi ca śruti antaram vacana ādi kriyā vyāpṛtasya eva ātmanaḥ  brahma tvam darśayati yad punar etad uktam iti prāṇa prajñā ātmanoḥ bheda darśanam brahma vāde na upapadyata iti na eṣa doṣaḥ jñāna kriyā śakti dvaya āśrayayoḥ buddhi prāṇayoḥ pratyagātma upādhi bhūtayoḥ abheda nirdeśa upapatteḥ upādhi dvaya upahitasya tu pratyak ātmanaḥ sva rūpeṇa abheda iti atas  prāṇa eva prajñā ātmā iti ekīkaraṇam aviruddham athavā na upāsātra evidhyāt āśrita tvāt iha tad yogāt iti asya ayamanyor athaḥ na brahma vākyaḥ  api jīva mukhya prāṇa liṅgam virudhyate katham upāsā traividhyāt  trividham iha brahma upāsane vivakṣitam prāṇa dharmeṇa prajñā dharmeṇa svadharmeṇa ca tatra aāyuḥ amṛtam upāḥsvāyuḥ prāṇaḥ iti aidam śarīram parigṛhya utthāpayati iti atasmāt etad eva uktham upāsīta iti ca prāṇa dharmaḥ aatha yathā asyai prajñāyai sarvāṇi bhūtāni ekībhavanti tad vyākhyāsyāmaḥ iti upakramya avāk evā asyā ekam aṅgamadū duhattasya e nāma parastāt prativihitā bhūtamātrā prajñayā vācam samāruhya vācā sarvāṇi nāmāni āpnoti ityādiḥ prajñā dharmaḥ tā vā etā daśa eva bhūtamātrā adhiprajñam daśa prajñāmātrā adhibhūtam yad hi bhūtamātrā na syuḥ na prajñāmātrāḥ syuḥ yad hi prajñāmātrā na syuḥ na bhūtamātrāḥ syuḥ na hi antaratas  rūpam kiñcana siddhyet  no etad nānā atat yathā rathasya āreṣu nemiḥ arpitā nābhāvarā arpitā evam eva etā bhūtamātrāḥ prajñāmātrāsu arpitāḥ prajñāmātrāḥ prāṇe arpitāḥ sa eṣa prāṇa eva prajñā ātmā iti ādiḥ brahma dharmaḥ tasmāt brahma eva etad upādhi dvaya dharmeṇa svadharmeṇa ca ekam upāsanam trividham vivakṣitam anyatra api amanaḥ mayaḥ prāṇa śarīraḥ iti ādau  upādhi dharmeṇa brahmaṇa upāsanam āśritam iha api tad yujyate vākyasya upakrama upasaṃhārābhyām eka artha tva avagamāt prāṇa prajñā brahma liṅga avagamāt ca tasmāt brahma vākyam etad iti siddham iti pādaḥ idam āmnāyate amanaḥ mayaḥ prāṇa śarīraḥ  bhā rūpaḥ ityādi tatra saṃśayaḥ kim iha manaḥ maya tva ādibhiḥ dharmaiḥ śārīra ātma upāsya tvena upadiśyata āhosvit param brahma iti kim tāvat prāptam śārīra iti kutas  tasya hi kārya karaṇa adhipateḥ prasiddhaḥ  manaā ādibhiḥ saṃbandhaḥ  na parasya brahmaṇaḥ aaprāṇaḥ  hyamanāḥ śubhraḥ ityādi śrutibhyaḥ nanu asarvam khalu idam brahma iti sva śabdena eva brahma upāttam katham iha śārīra ātma upāsya āśaṅkyate na eṣa doṣaḥ na idam vākyam brahma upāsanā vidhi param kim tarhi śama vidhi param yad kāraṇam asarvam khalu idam brahma tad jalān iti śānta upāsīta iti āha etad uktam bhavati yasmāt sarvam idam vikāra jātam brahmā eva tad ja tvāt talla tvāt tadana tvāt ca na ca sarvasya eka ātma tve rāga ādayaḥ saṃbhavanti tasmāt śānta upāsīta iti na ca śama vidhi paratve sati anena vākyena brahma upāsanam niyantum śakyate upāsanam tu asa kratum kurvīta iti anena vidhīyate kratuḥ saṃkalpaḥ  dhyānam iti arthaḥ tasya ca viṣaya tvaṃna śrūyate iti jīva liṅgam atas  brūmaḥ  jīva viṣayam etad upāsanam iti asarva karmā sarva kāmaḥ ityādi api śrūyamāṇam paryāyeṇa jīva viṣayam upapadyate aeṣa ma ātma antar hṛdaye aṇīyān vrīheḥ vā yavāt vā iti ca hṛdaya āyatana tvam aṇīyaḥ tvam cāra agra mātrasya jīvasya avakalpate na aparicchinnasya brahmaṇaḥ nanu ajyāyān pṛthivyā ityādi api na paricchinne avakalpata iti atra brūmaḥ na tāvat aṇīyaḥ tvam jyāyaḥ tvam ca ubhayam ekasmin samāśrayitum śakyam virodhāt  anyatara āśrayaṇe ca prathama śruta tvāt aṇīyaḥ tvam yuktam āśrayitum jyāyaḥ tvam tu brahma bhāva apekṣayā bhaviṣyati iti niścite ca jīva viṣaya tve yad ante brahma saṃkīrtanam aetat brahma iti tad api prakṛta parāmarśa artha tvāt jīva viṣayam eva tasmāt manaḥ maya tva ādibhiḥ dharmaiḥ upāsyam kutas  sarvatra prasiddha upadeśāt yad sarveṣu vedānteṣu prasiddham brahma śabdasya ālambanam jagat kāraṇaṃsa iha ca asarvam khalu idam brahma iti vākya upakrame śrute tad eva manaḥ maya tva ādi dharmaiḥ viśiṣṭam upadiśyata iti yuktam evañca prakṛta hānā prakṛta prakriye na bhaviṣyataḥ nanu vākya upakrame śama vidhi vivakṣayā brahma nirdiṣṭam na sva vivakṣaya iti uktam atra ucyate yadi api śama vidhi vivakṣayā brahma nirdiṣṭam tathā api manaḥ maya tva ādiṣu upadiśyamāneṣu tad eva brahma saṃnihitam bhavati jīstu na saṃnihitaḥ  na ca sva śabdena upātta iti vaiṣamyam vaktum iṣṭā vivakṣitāḥ yadi api apauruṣeye vede vaktuḥ abhāva at necca arthaḥ saṃbhavati tathā api upādānena phalena upacaryate loke hi yad śabda abhihitam upādeyam bhavati tad vivakṣitam iti ucyate yad anupādeyam tad avivakṣitam iti tad amavede api upādeya tvena abhihitam vivakṣitam bhavati itaradavivakṣitam upādāna anupādāne tu veda vākya tātparyābhyām avagamyate tad iha ye vivakṣitā guṇā upāsanāyām upādeya tvena upadiṣṭāḥ satya saṃkalpa prabhṛtayaḥ te parasmin brahmaṇi upapadyante satya saṃkalpa tvam hi sṛṣṭi sthiti saṃhāreṣu apratibaddha śakti tvāt paramātmana eva avakalpate paramātma guṇa tvena ca aya ātma apahṛta pāpmā iti atra asatyakāmaḥ satya saṃkalpa iti śrutam ākāśa ātmā ityādinā ākāśavat ātmā asya iti arthaḥ sarva gata tva ādibhiḥ dharṇaiḥ saṃbhavati ākāśena sāmyam brahmaṇaḥ ajyāyān pṛthivyāḥ ityādinā ca etad eva darśayati yadā api ākāśa ātmā yasya iti vyākhyāyacate tad api saṃbhavati sarva jagat kāraṇasya sarva ātmanaḥ  brahma ākāśa ātma tvam ata eva asarva karmā ityādi evam iha upāsyatayā vivakṣitā guṇā brahmaṇi upapadyante yad tu uktam amanaḥ mayaḥ prāṇa śarīraḥ iti jīva liṅgam na tad brahmaṇi upapadyata iti tad api brahmaṇi upapadyata iti brūmaḥ sarva ātma tvāt hi brahmaṇaḥ  jīva saṃbandhīni manaḥ maya tva ādīni brahma saṃbandhīni bhavanti tathā ca brahma viṣaye śruti smṛtī bhavataḥ iti sarvatas pāṇi pādam tad sarvatokṣi śiraḥ mukham sarvatas śrutimat loke sarvam āvṛtya tiṣṭhati iti ca aaprāṇaḥ  hyamanāḥ śubhraḥ iti śrutiḥ śuddha brahma viṣayā iyam tu amanaḥ mayaḥ prāṇa śarīraḥ iti sa guṇa brahma viṣaya iti viśeṣaḥ atas  vivakṣita guṇa upapatteḥ param eva brahma iha upāsya tvena upadiṣṭam iti gamyate pūrveṇa sutreṇa brahmaṇi vivakṣitānām guṇānām upapattiḥ uktā anena tu śārīre teṣām anupapattiḥ ucyate tuśabdaḥ  avadhāraṇa arthaḥ brahma eva uktena nyāyena manaḥ maya tva ādi guṇam na tu śārīraḥ  jīvaḥ  manaḥ maya tva ādi guṇaḥ yad kāraṇam asatya saṃkalpaḥ ākāśa ātmā avākī anādaraḥ jyāyān pṛthivyā iti ca evan jātīyakā guṇā na śārīra āñjasyena upapadyante śārīra iti śarīre bhava iti arthaḥ nanu īśvaraḥ  api śarīre bhavati satyam śarīre bhavati na tu śarīra eva bhavati ajyāyān pṛthivyā jyāyā anantarikṣāt aākāśavat sarva gataḥ ca nityaḥ iti ca vyāpita tva śravaṇāt  jīvaḥ tu śarīra eva bhavati tasya bhoga adhiṣṭhānāt śarīrāt anyatra vṛtti abhāvāt  itas ca na śārīraḥ  manaḥ maya tva ādi guṇaḥ yasmāt karma kartṛ vyapadeśaḥ  bhavati aetamitaḥ pretya abhisaṃbhavitā asmi iti etam iti prakṛtam manaḥ maya tva ādi guṇam upāsyam ātmānam karma tvena prāpya tvena vyapadiśati abhisaṃbhavitā asmi iti śārīram upāsakam kartṛ tvena prāpaka tvena abhisaṃbhavitā asmi iti prāptā asmi iti arthaḥ na ca satyām gatau  ekasya karma kartṛ vyapadeśaḥ  yuktaḥ tathā upāsya upāsaka bhāvaḥ  api bheda adhiṣṭhāna eva tasmāt api na śārīraḥ  manaḥ maya tva ādi viśiṣṭaḥ itas ca śārīrāt anyaḥ  manaḥ maya tva ādi guṇaḥ yasmāt śabda viśeṣaḥ  bhavati samāna prakaraṇe śruti antari iti śārīrasyatnaḥ  yaḥ śabdaḥ  abhidhāyakaḥ saptamī antaḥ  antarātman  iti tasmāt viśiṣṭaḥ  anyaḥ prathama antaḥ puruṣa śabdaḥ  manaḥ maya tva ādi viśiṣṭasya ātmanaḥ  abhidhāyakaḥ tasmāt tayoḥ bhedaḥ  adhigamyate smṛtiḥ ca śārīra paramātmanoḥ bhedam darśayati juna tiṣṭati bhrāmayan sarva bhūtāni yantra ārūḍhāni māyayā ityādyā atra āha kaḥ punar ayam śārīraḥ  nāma paramātmanaḥ  anyaḥ yaḥ pratiṣidhyate aanupapatteḥ tu na śārīraḥ ityādinā śrutiḥ tu to asti draṣṭā śrotā iti evan jātīyakā paramātmanaḥ  anyam ātmānam vārayati tathā smṛtiḥ api iti evan jātīyaka iti atra ucyate satyam etad  para eva ātmā deha indriya manaḥ buddhi upādhibhiḥ paricchidyamānaḥ  bālaiḥ śārīra iti upacaryate yathā ghaṭa karaka ādi upādhi vaśāt aparicchinnam api nabhaḥ paricchinnavat avabhāsate tadvat  tad apekṣayā ca karma kartṛ tva ādi bheda vyavahāraḥ  na virudhyate prāk  atattvam asi iti ātma eka tva upadeśa ghaṇāt  gṛhīte tu ātmā ekatve bandha mokṣa ādi sarva vyavahāra parisamāptiḥ eva syāt  arbhakam alpa mokaḥ  nīḍam aeṣa ma ātma antar hṛdaye iti paricchinna āyatana tvāt  sva śabdena ca aaṇīyān vrīheḥ vā yavāt vā iti aṇīyaḥ tu avyapadeśāt śārīra eva āra agra mātraḥ  jīva iha upadiśyate na karva gataḥ paramātmā iti yad uktam tad parihartavyam atra ucyate na ayam doṣaḥ na tāvat paricchinna deśasya sarva gata tva vyapadeśaḥ katham api upapadyate sarva gatasya tu sarva deśeṣu vidyamāna tvāt paricchinna deśa vyapadeśaḥ  api kayācid apekṣayā saṃbhavati yathā samasta vasudhā adhipatiḥ api hi san  yodhya adhipatiḥ iti vyapadiśyate kayā punar apekṣayā sarva gataḥ sannīśvaroḥ abhakaukā aṇīyān  ca vyapadiśyata iti nicāyya tvāt evam iti brūmaḥ evam aṇīyaḥ tu ādi guṇa gaṇa upeta īśvaraḥ tatra hṛdaya puṇḍarīke nicāyya u draṣṭavya upadiśyate yathā śālagrāme hariḥ tatra asya buddhi vijñānam grāhakam sarva gataḥ  api īśvaraḥ tatra upāsyamānaḥ prasīdati vyomavat ca etad draṣṭavyam yathā sarva gatam api sat vyoma sūcī pāśa ādi apekṣāya arbhaka okaḥ  aṇīyaḥ ca vyapadiśyate evam brahmā api tad evam nicāyya tva apekṣam brahmaṇoḥ abhakaukaḥ tvamaṇīyaḥ tvam ca na pāramārthikam tatra yad aśaṅkyate hṛdaya āyatana tvāt brahmaṇaḥ  hṛdaya āyatanānām ca pratiśarīram bhinna tvāt bhinna āyatanānām ca śuka ādīnām aneka tva sāvayava tva anitya tva ādi doṣa darśanāt brahmaṇaḥ  api tad prasaṅga iti tad api parihṛtam bhavati vyemavat sarva gatasya brahmaṇaḥ sarva prāṇi hṛdaya saṃbandhāt cit rūpa tayā ca śārīrādaviśiṣṭa tvāt  sukha duḥkha ādi saṃbhogaḥ  api aviśiṣṭaḥ prasajyeta eka tvāt ca na hi parasmāt ātmanaḥ  anyaḥ kaścid ātmā saṃsārī vidyate anānyaḥ  atas  asti vijñātā ityādi śrutibhyaḥ tasmāt parasya iva saṃsāra saṃbhoga prāptiḥ iti ced  na vaiśeṣyāt  na tāvat sarva prāṇi hṛdaya saṃbandhāt śarīravat brahṇaḥ saṃbhoga prasaṅgaḥ vaiśeṣyāt  viśeṣaḥ  hi bhavati śārīra parameśvarayoḥ ekaḥ kartā bhoktā dharma adharma sādhanaḥ sukha duḥkha ādimān  ca ekaḥ tad viparītaḥ  apahata pāpma tva ādi guṇaḥ etasmāt anayoḥ viśeṣāt ekasya bhogaḥ  na itarasya yadi ca saṃnidhāna mātreṇa vastu śaktim anāśritya kārya saṃbandhaḥ  abhyupagamyeta ākāśa ādīnām api dāha ādi prasaṅgaḥ sarva gata aneka ātma vādinām api samāvetau codya parihārau yad api eka tvāt brahmaṇa ātma antara abhāvāt śarīrasya bhogena brahṇaḥ  bhoga prasaṅga iti atra vadāmaḥ idam tāvat devānāṃpriyaḥ praṣṭavyaḥ katham ayam tvayā ātma antara abhāvaḥ  adhyavasita iti atatta vamasi aaham brahmā asmi anānyaḥ  atas  asti vijñātā iti ādi śāstrebhya iti ced  yathāśāstram tarhi śāstrīyor athaḥ pratipattavyaḥ  na tatra ardha jaratīyam labhyam śāstram ca tad tvam asi iti apahata pāpma tva ādi viśeṣaṇam brahma śārīrasya ātma tvena upadiśat śārīrasya eva tāvat upabhoktṛ tvam vārayati kutas tad upabhogena brahmaṇa upabhoga prasaṅgaḥ atha agṛhītam śārīrasya brahmaṇā eka tvam tadā mithyājñāna nimittaḥ śārīrasya upabhogaḥ na tena parama artha rūpasya brahmaṇaḥ saṃsparśaḥ na hi bālaiḥ tala malinatā ādibhiḥ vyomni vikalpyamāne tala malita ādi viśiṣṭam eva paramārtha taḥ  vyoma bhavati tad āha na vaiśeṣyāt iti na ekatve api śārīrasya upabhogena brahmaṇa upabhoga prasaṅgaḥ vaiśeṣyāt  viśeṣaḥ  hi bhavati mithyājñāna samyak jñanayoḥ mithyājñāna kalpita upabhogaḥ samyak jñāna dṛṣṭam eka tvam na ca mithyājñāna kalpitena upabhogena samyak jñāna dṛṣṭam vastu saṃspṛśyate tasmāt na upabhoga gandhaḥ  api śakya īśvarasya kalpayitum kaṭhavallīṣu paṭhyate iti atra kaścid odana upasecana sūcitaḥ  attā pratīyate tatra kim agni rattā syāt  uta jīvaḥ athavā paramātmā iti saṃśayaḥ viśeṣān avadhāraṇāt trayāṇām ca agni jīva paramātmanām asmin granthe praśna upanyāsa upalabdheḥ kim tāvat prāptam agniratta iti kutas  aagniḥ anna ādaḥ iti śruti prasiddhibhyām jīvaḥ  vāttā syāt  atayoḥ anyaḥ pippalam svādvatti iti darśanāt  na paramātmā aanaśnannanyaḥ  aabhicākaśīti iti darśanāt iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ atta atra paramātmā bhavitum arhati kutas  carācara grahaṇāt carācaram hi sthāvara jaṅgamam mṛtyupasecanam iha adyātvena pratīyate tādṛśasya ca ādyasya na paramātmanaḥ  anyaḥ kārtsyena āttā saṃbhavati paramātmā tu vikāra jātam saṃharan sarvam attī iti upapadyate nanu iha carācara grahaṇam na upalabhyate katham siddhavat carācara grahaṇam hetu tvena upādīyate na eṣa doṣaḥ mṛtyupasecana tvena sarvasya prāṇi nikāyasya pratīyamāna tvāt  brahma kṣatrayoḥ ca prādhānyāt pradarśana artha tva upapatteḥ yad tu paramātmanaḥ  api nāttṛ tvam saṃbhavati aanaśnannanyaḥ  aabhicākaśīti iti darśanāt iti atra ucyate karma phala bhogasya pratiṣedhakam etad darśanam tasya saṃnihita tvāt  na vikāra saṃhārasya pratiṣedhakam sarva vedānteṣu sṛṣṭi sthiti saṃhāra kāraṇa tvena brahmaṇaḥ prasiddha tvāt  tasmāt parama ātmā ātmā eva īhāt tā bhavitum arhati prakaraṇa āc ca itas ca paramātmā eva īhāt tā bhavitum arhati yad kāraṇam prakaraṇam idam paramatmanaḥ ana jāyate mriyate vā vipaścit ityādi prakṛta grahaṇam ca nyāyyam aka itthā veda yatra saḥ iti ca durvijñāna tvam paramātma liṅgam guhā praviṣṭa adhikaraṇam sū guhām praviṣṭau   ātmānau hi tad darśanāt  kaṭhavallīṣu eva paṭhyate iti tatra saṃśayaḥ kim iha buddhi jīvau nirdiṣṭau  uta jīva paramātmānau  iti yadi buddhi jīvau tatas  buddhi pradhānāt kārya karaṇa saṃghātāt vilakṣaṇaḥ  jīvaḥ pratipāditaḥ  bhavati tad api iha pratipāditavyam ayeyam prete vicikitsā manuṣye asti iti eke na ayam asti iti ca eke etad vidyām anuśiṣṭaḥ tvayā aham varāṇām eṣa varaḥ tṛtīyaḥ iti pṛṣṭa tvāt  atha jīva paramātmānau tatas  jīvāt vilakṣaṇaḥ paramātmā pratipāditaḥ  bhavati tad api iha pratipādayitavyam aanyatra dharmāt anyatra adharmadanyatra asmāt kṛta akṛtāt  anyatra bhūtāt ca bhavyāt ca yad tad paśyasi tadvat iti pṛṣṭa tvāt  atra ahākṣeptā ubhāpi etau pakṣau na saṃbhavataḥ kasmāt  ṛta pānam karma phala upabhogaḥ sukṛtasya loke iti ca dvivacanena dvayoḥ pānam darśayati śrutiḥ atas  buddhi kṣetrajña pakṣaḥ tāvat na saṃbhavati ata eva kṣetrajña paramātma pakṣaḥ  api na saṃbhavati cetane api parama ātmani ṛta pāna asaṃbhavāt aanaḥ  nannanyo aabhicākaśīti iti mantra varṇāt iti atra ucyate na eṣa doṣaḥ chatriṇaḥ  gacchanti iti ekena api chatriṇā bahūnām chatri tva upacāra darśanāt evam ekena api pibatā dvau pibantau  ucyete yad vā jīvaḥ tāvat pibati īśvaraḥ tu pāyayati pāyayan  api pibati iti ucyate pācayitari api praktṛ tva prasiddhi darśanāt  buddhi kṣetrajña parigrahaḥ  api saṃbhavati karaṇe kartṛ tva upacārāt edhāṃsi pacanti iti prayoga darśanāt  nacādhyatma adhikāre anyau kaucidha āvṛtam pibantau saṃbhavataḥ tasmāt buddhi jīvau syātām jīva paramātmānau vā iti saṃśayaḥ kim tāvat prāptam buddhi kṣetrajñau  iti kutas  aguhān praviṣṭau iti viśeṣaṇāt  yadi śarīram guhā yadi vā hṛdayam ubhayathā api buddhi kṣetrajñau guhām praviṣṭau  upapadyete na ca sati saṃbhave sarva gatasya brahmaṇaḥ  viśiṣṭa deśa tvam yuktam kalpayitum asukṛtasya loke iti ca karma gocara anatikramam darśayati paramātmā tu na sukṛtasya vā duṣkṛtasya vā gocare vartate ana karmaṇā vardhate no kanīyān iti śruteḥ achāya ātapau iti ca tetana acetanayoḥ nirdeśa upapadyate chāyā ātapavat paraspara vilakṣaṇa tvāt tasmāt buddhi kṣetrajñā vihocyeyātām iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ vijñāna ātma parama ātmāna avihocyeyātām kasmāt  ātmānau hi tau  ubhau  api cetanau samāna svabhāvau saṃkhyā śravaṇe ca samāna svabhāveṣu eva loke pratītiḥ dṛśyate asya goḥ dvitīyaḥ  anveṣṭavya iti ukte gauḥ eva dvitīyaḥ  anviṣyate na aśvaḥ puruṣaḥ  vā tad iha ṛta pānena liṅgena niścite vijñāna ātmani dvitīya anveṣaṇāyām samāna svabhāvaḥ cetanaḥ paramātmā eva pratīyate nanu uktam guhā hita tva darśanāt na paramātmā pratyetavya iti guhā hita tva darśanāt eva paramātmā apratyetavya iti vadāmaḥ guhā hita tvam tu śruti smṛtiṣu asakṛt paramātmana eva dṛśyate ayaḥ  veda nihitam guhāyām parame vyoman aātmānam anviccha guhām praviṣṭam ityādyāsu sarva gatasya api brahmaṇa upalabdhi arthaḥ  deśa viśeṣa upadeśaḥ  na virudhyata ityet api uktam eva sukṛta loka varti tvam tu chatri tvavat ekasmin  api vartamānam ubhayoḥ aviruddham chāyā tapau  iti api aviruddham chāyā ātapavat paraspara vilakṣaṇa tvāt saṃsāritvā saṃsāri tvayoḥ avidyā kṛta tvāt saṃsāri tvasya pāramārthika tvāt ca asaṃsāri tvasya tasmāt vijñāna ātma paramātamānau guhām praviṣṭau gṛhyete kutas ca vijñāna ātma parama ātmānau gṛhyete viśeṣaṇam ca vijñāna ātma paramātmanoḥ eva bhavati aātmānam rathinam viddhi śarīram ratham eva tu ityādinā pareṇa granthena rathi ratha ādirūpaka kalpanayā vijñānātnām rathinam saṃsāra mokṣayoḥ gantāram kalpayati asaḥ  adhvanaḥ pāram āpnoti tad viṣṇoḥ paramam padam iti ca paramātmānam gantavyam tathā atam durdarśa gūḍham anupraviṣṭham purāṇam adhyātma yoga adhigamena devam matvā dhīraḥ  harṣa śokau jahāti iti pūrvasmin  api granthe mantṛ mantavya tvena etau  eva viśeṣitau prakaraṇam ceda paramātmanaḥ brahma vidaḥ  vadanti iti ca vaktṛ viśeṣa upādanam paramātma parigrahe ghaṭate tasmāt iha jīva paramātmānāvucyeyātām eṣa eva nyāyaḥ advā suparṇā sayujā sakhāyā iti evamādiṣu api tatra api hi adhyātma adhikārāt na prākṛtau suparṇau  ucyete tayoḥ anyaḥ pippalam svāditti iti adana liṅgāt vijñāna ātmā bhavati anaś nannanyo abhicākaśīti iti anaśana cetanābhyām paramātmā anantare ca mantre tau  eva draṣṭṛ draṣṭavya bhāvena viśinaṣṭi nīśayā śocati muhyamānaḥ juṣṭam yadā paśyati anyam īśam asya mahimānam iti vīta śokaḥ iti apara āha iti neya mṛgasya adhikaraṇasya siddhāntam bhajate paiṅgi rahasya brāhmaṇena anyathā vyākhyāta tvāt  atayoḥ anyaḥ pippalam svādi tti iti sattva manaḥ  nannanyo abhicāka śīti iti anaḥ  nannanyo abhipaśyati jñaḥ tau  etau sattva kṣetrajñau iti sattva śabda uti iti anaḥ  nannanyo abhipaśyati yad ucyate tad na sattva kṣetrajña śabdayoḥ antaḥkaraṇa śarīra para tayā prasiddha tvāt  tatra eva ca vyākhyāta tvāt  yam śārīra upadraṣṭā sa kṣetrajñaḥ tau  etau sattva kṣetrajñau iti na api asya adhikaraṇasya pūrva pakṣam bhajate na hi atra śārīraḥ kṣetrajñaḥ kartṛ tva bhoktṛ tva ādinā saṃsāra dharmeṇa upetaḥ  vivakṣyate katham tarhi sarva saṃsāra dharma atītaḥ  brahma bhāvaḥ caitanya mātra svarūpaḥ aanaḥ  nannanyo abhicāka śīti aanaḥ  nannanyo abhicākaśīti jñaḥ iti vacanāt  atattvam asi akṣetra jñam ca api mām viddhi ityādi śruti smṛtibhyaḥ ca tāvatā ca vidyā upasaṃhāra darśana melam eva avakalpate tau  etau sattva kṣetrajñau na ha vā evaṃvidi kiñcana raca ādhvaṃsate ityādi katham punar asmin pakṣe tayoḥ anyaḥ pippalam svādi tti iti sattvam iti acetane sattve bhoktṛ tvā avacanam ti ucyate na iyam śrutiḥ acetanasya sattvasya bhoktṛ tvam vakṣyāmi iti pravṛttā kim tarhi cetanasya kṣetrajñasya abhoktṛ tvam brahma sbhāva tām ca vakṣyāmi iti tad artham sukha ādi vikriyāvati sattve bhoktṛ tvam adhyāropayati idam hi kartṛ tvam bhoktṛ tvam ta sattva kṣetrajñayoḥ ita reti svabhāvau  iveka kṛtam kalpyate paramārthataḥ tu na anyatarasya api saṃbhavati acetana tvāt sattvasya avikriya tvāt ca kṣetrajñasya avidyā pratyupasthāpita svabhāva tvāt ca sattvasya sutarām na saṃbhavati tathā ca śrutiḥ nyat paśyet ityādinā svapna dṛṣṭa hasti ādi vyavahāravat avidyā viṣaya eva kartṛ tva ādi vyavahāram darśayati ayatra tu asya sarvam ātmā eva abhūt tad kena kam paśyet ityādinā ca vivekinaḥ kartṛ tva ādi vyavahara abhāvam darśayati aya eṣaḥ  akṣiṇi puruṣaḥ  dṛśyata eṣa ātmā iti ha uvāca etad amṛtam abhayam etad brahma iti etadi api asmin sarpiḥ vā udakam vā siñcati vartmani eva gacchati ityādi śra yate tatra saṃśayaḥ kim ayam pratibimba ātmakṣi adhikaraṇaḥ  nirdiśyate athavā vijñāna ātmā uta devatā ātma indriyasya adhiṣṭhātāthaveśvara iti kim tāvat prāptam chāyā ātmā puruṣa pratirūpā iti kutas  tasya dṛśyamāna tva prasiddheḥ aya eṣaḥ  akṣiṇi puruṣaḥ  dṛśyate iti ca prasiddavat upadeśāt vijñāna ātmanaḥ  vāyam nirdeśa iti yuktam sa hi cakṣuṣā rūpam paśyan  cakṣuṣi saṃnihitaḥ  bhavati ātma śabdaḥ ca asmin pakṣe anukūlaḥ  bhavati āditya puruṣaḥ  vā cakṣuṣaḥ  anugrāhakaḥ pratīyate araśmibhiḥ eṣaḥ  asmin pratiṣṭhitaḥ iti śruteḥ amṛta tva ādīnām ca devatātnī api kathañcid saṃbhavāt  na īśvaraḥ sthāna viśeṣa nirdeśāt iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ parameśvara eva akṣiṇī abhyantaraḥ puruṣa iha upadiṣṭa iti kasmāt  upapatteḥ upapadyate hi parameśvare guṇa jātam iha upadiśyamānam ātma tvam tāvat mukhyayā vṛttyā parameśvara upapadyate asa ātmā tad tvam asi iti śruteḥ amṛta tva abhaya tve ca tasmin  asakṛt śrutau śrūyete tathā parameśvara anurūpam etad akṣi sthānam yathā hi parameśvaraḥ sarva doṣaiḥ aliptaḥ apahata pāpma tva ādi śravaṇāt tathā akṣi sthānam sarva lepa rahim upadiṣṭam atat yadi api asmin sarpiḥ vā udakam vā siñcati vartmani eva gacchati iti śruteḥ saṃyat vāma tva ādi guṇa upadeśaḥ ca tasmin  avakalpate aetam saṃyat dhāma iti ācakṣate etam hi sarvāṇi vāmāni abhisaṃyanti aeṣa u eva vāma nīreṣa hi sarvāṇi vāmāni nayati eṣa u eva bhāmānīḥ eṣa hi sarveṣu lokeṣu bhāti iti ca ata upapatteḥ antaraḥ parameśvaraḥ katham punar ākaśavat sarva gatasya brahmaṇaḥ  akṣi alpa sthānam upapadyata iti atra ucyate bhavet eṣa anavakḷptiḥ yadi etad eva ekam sthānam asya nirdiṣṭam bhavet  santi hi anyāni api pṛthivī ādīni sthānāni asya nirdiṣṭāni ityādinā teṣu hi cakṣuḥ api nirdiṣṭam iti asthāna ādi vyapadeśāt ityādi grahaṇena etad darśayati na kevalam sthānam eva ekam anucitam brahmaṇaḥ  nirdiśyamānam dṛśyate kim tarhi nāma rūpam iti evan jātīyakam api anāma rūpasya brahmaṇaḥ  anucitam nirdiśyamānam dṛśyate ahiraṇya śmaśruḥ ityādi nirguṇam api sat brahma nāma rūpa gataiḥ guṇaiḥ sa guṇam upāsana artham tatra tatra upadiśyata iti etad api uktam eva sarva gatasya api brahmaṇa upalabdhi artham sthāna viśeṣaḥ  na virudhyate śālagrāma iva viṣṇoḥ iti etad api uktam eva apica na eva atra vivaditavyam kim brahma asmin vākye abhidhīyate na vā iti sukha viśiṣṭa abhidhānam eva brahma tvam siddham sukha viśiṣṭam hi brahma yad vākya upakrame prakrāntam aprāṇaḥ  brahma kam brahma kham brahma iti tad eva iha abhihitam prakṛta parigrahasya nyāyya tvāt  aācāryaḥ tu te gatim vaktā iti ca gati mātra abhidhāna pratijñānāt  katham punar vākya upakrame sukha viśiṣṭam brahma vijñāyata iti ucyate iti etad agnīnām vacanam śrutvā upakosala uvāca iti tatra idam prativacanam iti tatra khaṃśabdaḥ  bhūta ākāśe nirūḍhaḥ  loke yadi tasya viśeṣaṇa tvena kaṃśabdaḥ sukha vācī na upādīyeta tathā sati kevale bhūta ākāśe brahma śabdaḥ  nāma ādiṣu iva pratīka abhiprāyeṇa prayukta iti pratītiḥ syāt  tathā kaṃśabdasya viṣaya indriya saṃparka janite sāmaye sukhe prasiddha tvāt  yadi tasya khaṃśabdaḥ  viśeṣaṇa tvena na upādīyeta laukikam sukham brahma iti pratītiḥ syāt  itaretara viśeṣatau tu kaṅkhaṃśabdau sukha ātmakam brahma gamayataḥ tatra dvitīye brahma śabde anupādīyamāne kam kham brahma iti eva ucyamāne kaṃśabdasya viśeṣaṇa tvena eva upayukta tvāta sukhasya guṇasya adhyeya tvam syāt  tad mā bhūt iti ubhayoḥ kaṅkhaṃśabdayoḥ brahma śabda śiraḥ tvam akam brahma kham brahma iti iṣṭam hi sukhasya api guṇasya guṇavat dhyeya tvam tad evam vākya upakrame sukha viśiṣṭam brahma upadiṣṭam pratyekam ca gārhapatyādayaḥ  agnayaḥ svam svam mahimānam upadiśya aeṣā somya te asmad vidyā ātma vidyā ca iti upasaṃharantaḥ pūrvatra brahma nirdiṣṭam iti jñāpayanti aācāryaḥ tu te gatim vaktā iti ca gati mātra abhidhāna pratijñānam artha antara vivakṣām vārayati ayathā puṣkara palāśā āpaḥ  na śliṣyanta evam evaṃvidi pāpam karma na śliṣyate iti ca akṣi sthānam puruṣam vijānataḥ pāpena anupaghātam bruvan  akṣi sthānasya puruṣasya brahma tvam darśayati tasmāt prakṛtasya eva brahmaṇaḥ  akṣi sthāna tām saṃyat vāma tva ādi guṇa tām ca uktvā arcira ādikān tad vidaḥ  gatim vakṣyāmi iti upakramate kṣiṇi puruṣaḥ  dṛśyata eṣa ātmā iti ha uvāca iti itas ca akṣi sthānaḥ puruṣaḥ parameśvaraḥ yasmāt śruta upaniṣatkasya śruta rahasyavijñānasya brahma vidaḥ  yā gatiḥ devayāna ākhyā prasiddhā śrutau iti smṛtau  api iti sā eva ahākṣi puruṣa vidaḥ  abhidhīyamānā dṛśyate aatha yadu ca eva asmin śavyam kurvanti yadi ca na arciṣam eva abhisaṃbhavanti iti upakramya aādityāt candramasam candramasaḥ  vidyutam tad puruṣaḥ  amānavaḥ sa enān brahma gamayati eva deva pathaḥ  brahma patha etena pratipadyamānā imam mānavam āvarte na āvartante iti tad iha brahma vid viṣayā prasiddhayā gatyā akṣi sthānasya brahma tvam niścīyate yad punaruktam chāyā ātmā vijñāna ātmā devatā ātmā vā syāt akṣi sthāna iti atra ucyate na chāyā ātma adiḥ itara iha grahaṇam arhati kasmāt  anavasthiteḥ na tāvat chāyā ātmanaḥ cakṣuṣi nityam avasthānam saṃbhavati yadā eva hi kaścid puruṣaḥ cakṣuḥ āsīdati tadā cakṣuṣi puruṣa  chāyā dṛśyate apagate tasmin  dṛśyate aya eṣaḥ  akṣiṇi puruṣaḥ iti ca śrutiḥ saṃnidhānāt sva cakṣuṣi dṛśyamānam puruṣam upāsya tvena upadiśati naca upāsanā kāle chāyā karam kañcid puruṣam cakṣuḥ samīpe saṃnidhā apya upāsta iti yuktam kalpayitum aasya eva śarīrasya nāśam anveṣa naśyati iti śrutiḥ chāyā ātmanaḥ  api anavasthita tvam darśayati asaṃbhavāt ca tasmin  amṛta tva ādīnām guṇānām na chāyā ātmani pratītiḥ tathā vijñāna ātmanaḥ  api sādhāraṇe kṛtsna śarīra indriya saṃbandhe sati cakṣuṣi ā iva avasthita tvam vaktum na śakyam brahmaṇaḥ tu vyāpinaḥ  api dṛṣṭa upalabdhi arthaḥ  hṛdaya ādi deśa viśeṣa saṃbandhaḥ samānaḥ ca vijñāna ātmani api amṛta tva ādīnām guṇānām asaṃbandhaḥ yadi api vijñāna ātmā paramātmanaḥ  ananya eva tathā api avidyā kāma karma kṛtam tasmin martya tva madhya ropitam bhayam ca iti amṛta tva abhaya tve na upapadyete saṃyat vāma tva ādayaḥ ca etasmin  ana aiśvaryāt anupapannā eva devatā ātmanaḥ tu araśmibhiḥ eṣaḥ  asmin pratiṣṭhitaḥ iti śruteḥ yadi api cakṣuṣi avasthānam syāt tathā api ātma tvam tāvat na saṃbhavati parāgrūpa tvāt  amṛta tvāt ayaḥ  api na saṃbhavanti utpatti pralaya śravaṇāt  amara tvam api devānām cira kāla avasthāna apekṣam aiśvaryam api parameśvara āyattam na svābhāvikam bhīṣā asmāt vātaḥ pavate bhīṣodeti sūryaḥ bhīṣā asmāt agniḥ ca indraḥ ca mṛtyuḥ dhāvati pañcamaḥ iti mantra varṇāt  tasmāt parameśvara eva ayam akṣi sthānaḥ pratyetavyaḥ asmin  ca pakṣe dṛśyata iti prasiddhavat upādānam śāstra ādi apekṣam vidvat viṣayam prarocana artham iti vyākhyeyam aya imam ca lokam param ca lokam sarvāṇi ca bhūtāni yaḥ  antaraḥ  yamayati iti upakramya śrūyate ityādi atra adhidaivatam adhilokam adhivedam adhiyajñam adhibhūtam adhyātmam ca kaścid antar avasthitaḥ  yamayitā antaryāmī iti śrūyate sa kim adhidaiva ādi abhimānī devatā ātmā kaścid kiṃvā prāpta aṇim ādi aiśvaryaḥ kaścid yogī kiṃvā paramātmā kiṃvā artha antaram kiñci diti apūrva saṃjñā darśana ātma saṃśayaḥ kim tau  annaḥ pratibhāti saṃjñayā aprasiddha tvāt saṃjñinaḥ  api asiddhena artha antareṇa kenacid bhavitavyam iti athavā na anirūpita rūpam artha antaram śakyam asti abhyupagantum antaryāmi śabdaḥ ca antar yamana yogena pravṛttaḥ  na atyantam aprasiddhaḥ tasmāt pṛthivī ādi abhimānī kaścid devaḥ  antaryāmī syāt  tathā ca śrūyate ityādi sa ca kārya kāraṇavat tvāt pṛthivī ādīnantaḥ tiṣṭhanyamaya ti iti yuktam devatā ātmanaḥ  yamayitṛ tvam yoginaḥ  vā kasyacid siddhasya sarva anupraveśena yamayitṛ tvam syāt  na tu paramātmā pratīyeta akārya karaṇa tvāt iti evam prāpta idam ucyate yaḥ  antaryāmya dhidaiva ādiṣu śrūyate sa paramātmā eva syāt na anya iti kutas  tad dharma vyapadeśāt tasya hi paramātmanaḥ  dharmā iha nirdiśyamānā dṛśyante pṛthivī ādi tāvat adhidaivata ādi bheda bhinnam samastam vikāra jātam antar tiṣṭanyamaya ti iti paramātmanaḥ  yamayitṛ tvam dharma upapadyate sarva vikāra kāraṇa tve sati sarva śakti upapatteḥ eṣa ta aātmā antaryāmyamṛtaḥ iti ca ātmatva amṛta tve mukhye paramātmana upapadyete ayam pṛthivī na veda iti ca pṛthivī devatāyāḥ  avijñeyam antaryāmiṇam bruvan devatā ātmanaḥ  anyam antaryāmiṇam darśayati apṛthivī devatā hi aham asmi pṛthivī ityatmānam vijānīyāt tathā aadṛṣṭaḥ  aśrutaḥ ityādi vyapadeśaḥ  rūpa ādi vihīna tvāt param ātmana upapadyata iti yad tva kārya karaṇasya paramātmanaḥ  yamayitṛ tvam na upapadyata iti na eṣa doṣaḥ yān niyacchati tad kārya karaṇaiḥ eva tasya kārya karaṇattva upapatteḥ tasya api anyaḥ  niyantā iti anavasthā doṣaḥ ca na saṃbhavati bheda abhāvāt bhede hi sati anavasthā doṣa upapattiḥ tasmāt parama ātmā eva antaryāmī syāt etad  adṛṣṭa tvāt ayaḥ  dharmāḥ sāṃkhya smṛti kalpitasya pradhānasya api upapadyante rūpa ādi hīna tayā tasya taiḥ abhyupagamāt  aapratarkyam avijñeyam prasuptam iva sarvataḥ iti hi smaranti tasya api niyantṛ tvam sarva vikāra kāraṇa tvāt upapadyate tasmāt pradhānam antaryāmi śabdam syāt  aīkṣateḥ na aśabdam iti atra nirākṛtam api sat pradhānam iha adṛṣṭa tva ādi vyapadeśa saṃbhavena punar āśaṅkyate ata uttaram ucyate na ca smārte pradhānam antaryāmi śabdam bhavitum arhati kasmāta tad dharma abhilāpāt yadi api adṛṣṭa tva ādi vyapadeśaḥ pradhānasyasaṃbhavati tathā api na draṣṭṛ tva ādivya peśaḥ saṃbhavati pradhānasya acetana tvena taiḥ abhyupagamāt  aadṛṣṭaḥ  draṣṭā śrutaḥ śrotāmataḥ  mantā vijñātaḥ  vijñātā iti hi vākya śeṣa iha bhavati ātma tvam api na pradhānasya upapadyate yadi pradhānam ātma tvat raṣṭṛ tva ādi asaṃbhavāt na antaryāmī abhyupagamyate śārīraḥ tarhi antaryāmī bhavatu śārīraḥ  hi cetana tvāt draṣṭā śrotā mantā vijñātā ca bhavati ātmā ca pratyaktvāt  amṛtaḥ ca dharma adharma phala upabhoga upapatteḥ adṛṣṭa tva ādayaḥ ca dharmāḥ śārīre para siddhāḥ darśana ādi kriyāyāḥ kartari pravṛtti virodhāt  ana dṛṣṭeḥ draṣṭāram paśyeḥ ityādi śrutibhyaḥ ca tasya ca kārya karaṇa saṃghātam antaryamayitum śīlam bhoktṛ tvāt tasmāt śārīraḥ  antaryāmī iti ata uttaram paṭhati na iti pūrva sūtrāt anuvartate śārīraḥ ca na antaryāmī iṣyate kasmāt  yadi api draṣṭṛ tvāt ayaḥ  dharmaḥ tasya saṃbhavanti tathā api ghaṭa ākāśavat upādhi paricchinna tvāt na kārtsyena pṛthivī ādiṣu antar avasthātum niyantum ca śaknoti api cobhaye api hi śākhinaḥ kāṇvā mādhyandinānāḥ ca antaryāmiṇaḥ  bhedena enam śārīram pṛthivī ādivat adhiṣṭhāna tvena niyamya tvena ca adhīyate iti kāṇvāḥ aya ātmani tiṣṭhan iti mādhyandināḥ aya ātmani tiṣṭhan iti asminḥ tāvat pāṭhe bhavati ātma śabdaḥ śārīrasya vācakaḥ ayaḥ  vijñāne tiṣṭhan iti asmin  api pāṭhe vijñāna śabdena śārīra ucyate vijñānam ayaḥ  hi śārīraḥ tasmāt śārīradanya īśvaraḥ  antaryāmi iti siddham katham punar ekasmin dehe dvau draṣṭāravupapadyete yaḥ ca ayam īśvaraḥ  antaryāmī yaḥ ca ayam itaraḥ śārīraḥ kā punar iha anupapattiḥ anānyaḥ  atas  asti draṣṭā ityādi śruti vacanam virudhyeta atra hi prakṛtāt antaryāmiṇaḥ  anyam draṣṭāram śrotāram mantāram vijñātāram ca ātmānam pratiṣedhati niyantṛ antara pratiṣedha artham etad vacanam iticet na niyantṛ antara aprasaṅgāt aviśeṣa śravaṇāt ca atra ucyate atra āha na parameśvaraḥ  vaiśvanaraḥ  bhavitum arhati kutas  śabda ādibhyaḥ  antar pratiṣṭhānāt ca śabdaḥ tāvat vaiśvānara śabdaḥ  na parameśvare saṃbhavati artha antare rūḍha tvāt  tathā agni śabdaḥ asa eṣaḥ  agniḥ vaiśvānaraḥ iti ādi śabdāt  ahṛdayam gārhapatyaḥ ityādi agni tretā prakalpanam atat yad buktam prathamam āgacchet tad homīyam ityādinā ca prāṇa āhuti adhikaraṇa tā saṃkīrtanam etebhyaḥ  hetubhyaḥ  jāṭharaḥ  vaiśvānaraḥ pratyetavyaḥ tathā antar pratiṣṭhānam api śrūyate ntar pratiṣṭhitam veda iti tad ca jāṭhare saṃbhavati yad api uktam mūrdhā eva sutejā ityādeḥ viśeṣāt kāraṇāt paramātmā vaiśvānara iti atra brūmaḥ kuto hi eṣa nirṇayaḥ yad ubhayathā api viśeṣa pratibhāne sati parameśvara viṣaya eva viśeṣa āśrayaṇīyaḥ  na jāṭhara viṣaya iti athavā bhūta agneḥ antar bahis ca avatiṣṭhamānasya eṣa nirdeśaḥ  bhaviṣyati tasya api hi dyu loka ādi saṃbandhaḥ  mantra varṇāt avagamyate iti ādau athavā tad śarīrāyā devatāyāḥ  aiśvarya yogāt dyuloka ādi avayava tvam bhaviṣyati tasmāt na parameśvaraḥ  vaiśvānara iti atra ucyate na tathā adṛṣṭi upadeśāt iti na śabda ādibhyaḥ kāraṇebhyaḥ parameśvarasya pratyākhyānam yuktam kutas  tathā jāṭhara aparityāgena dṛṣṭi upadeśāt parameśvara dṛṣṭiḥ hi jāṭhare vaiśvānara iha upadiśyate amanaḥ  brahma iti upāsīta ityādivat  athavā jāṭhara vaiśvānara upādhibhiḥ parameśvara iha draṣṭavya tvena upadiśyate amanaḥ mayaḥ prāṇa śarīraḥ  bhā rūpaḥ ityādivat  yadi ca iha parameśvaraḥ  na vivakṣyeta kevala eva jāṭharaḥ  agniḥ vivakṣyeta tatas  mūrdhā eva sutejā ityādiḥ viśeṣasya asaṃbhava eva syāt  yathā tu devatā bhūta agni vyapāśrayeṇa api ayam viśeṣa upapādayitum na śakyate tathā uttara sūtre vakṣyāmaḥ yadi ca kevala eva jāṭharaḥ  vivakṣyeta puruṣe antar pratiṣṭhita tvam kevalam tasya syāt na tu puruṣa tvam puruṣam api ca enam adhīyate vājasaneyinaḥ gniḥ vaiśvānaraḥ  yad puruṣaḥ sa yaḥ  ha etam evam agnim vaiśvānaram puruṣa vidham puruṣe antar pratiṣṭhitam veda iti parameśvarasya tu sarva ātma tvāt puruṣa tvam puruṣe antar pratiṣṭhita tvam ca ubhayam upapadyate ye tu apuruṣavidham api ca enam adhīyate iti sūtra avayavam paṭhanti teṣām eṣoḥ athaḥ kevala jāṭhara parigrahe puruṣe antar pratiṣṭhita tvam kevalam syāt na puruṣavidha tvam puruṣavidham api ca enam adhīyate vājasaneyinaḥ ntar pratiṣṭhitam veda iti puruṣavidha tvam ca prakaraṇāt yad adhidaivatam dyu mūrdha tva ādi pṛthivī pratiṣṭhita tva antam yad ca adhyātmam prasiddham mūrdha tva ādi cubuka pratiṣṭhita tva antam tad parigṛhyate yad punaruktam bhūtāgneḥ api mantra varṇe dyu loka ādi saṃbandha darśanāt mūrdhā eva sutejā iti ādi avayava kalpanam tasya eva bhaviṣyati iti yad śarīrāyā devatāyāḥ  vaiśvarya yogāt iti tad parihartavyam atra ucyate ata eva uktebhyaḥ  hetubhyaḥ  na devatā vaiśvānaraḥ tathābhūta agniḥ api na vaiśvānaraḥ na hi bhūta agneḥ auṣṇya prakāśa mātra ātmakasya dyu mūrdha tva ādi kalpanā upapadyate vikārasya vikāra antarātma tva asaṃbhavāt tathā devatāyāḥ sati api aiśvarya yoge na dyu mūrdha tva ādi kalpanā saṃbhavati akāraṇa tvāt parameśvara adhīna aiśvarya tvāt ca ātma śabda asaṃbhavaḥ ca sarveṣu eṣu pakṣeṣu sthita eva sākṣāt  api  avirodham jaiminiḥ pūrve jāṭhara agni pratīko jāṭhara agni upādhiko vā parameśvara upāsya iti uktam antar pratiṣṭhita tva ādi anurodhena idānīm tu vinā eva pratīka upādhi kalpanābhyām sākṣāt api parameśvara upāsana parigrahe na kaścid virodha iti jaiminiḥ ācāryaḥ  manyante nanu jāṭhara agni aparigrahe antar pratiṣṭhita tva vacanam śabda dīni ca kāraṇāni virudhyeran  iti atra ucyate antar pratiṣṭhita tva vacanam tāvat na virudhyate na hi iha apuruṣavidham puruṣe antar pratiṣṭhitam veda iti jāṭhara agni abhiprāyeṇa idam ucyate tasya aprakṛta tvāt asaṃśabdita tvāt ca katham tarhi yad prakṛtam mūrdha ādi cubuka anteṣu puruṣa avayaveṣu puruṣa vidhi tvam kalpitam tad abhiprāyeṇa idam ucyate ntar pratiṣṭhitam veda iti yathā vṛkṣe śākhām pratiṣṭhitām paśyati iti tadvat  athavā yaḥ prakṛtaḥ parama ātma adhyātmam adhidaivatam ca puruṣa vidhi tva upādhiḥ tasya yad kevalam sākṣi rūpam tad abhiprāyeṇa idam ucyate ntar pratiṣṭhitam veda iti niścite ca pūrva apara ālocana vaśena paramātma parigrahe tad viṣaya eva vaiśvānara śabdaḥ kenacid yogena vartiṣyate viśvaḥ ca ayam naraḥ ca iti viśveṣām vāyam naraḥ viśve vā narā asya iti viśvānaraḥ paramātmā sarva ātma tvāt  viśvānara eva vaiśvānaraḥ tad hitaḥ  ananya arthaḥ rākṣasa vāyasa ādivat  agni śabdaḥ  api agraṇī tva ādi yoga āśrayaṇena paramātma viṣaya eva bhaviṣyati gārhapatya ādi kalpanam prāṇa āhuti adhikaraṇa tvam ca paramātmanaḥ  api sarva ātma tvāt upapadyate katham punar  parameśvara parigrahe prādeśa mātra śrutiḥ upapadyata iti tām vyākhyātum ārabhate atimātrasya api parameśvarasya prādeśa mātra tvam abhivyakti nimittam syāt  abhivyajyate kila prādeśa mātra parimāṇaḥ parameśvara upāsakānām kṛte pradeśeṣu vā hṛdaya ādiṣu upalabdhi sthāneṣu viśeṣaṇa abhivyajyate atas  parameśvare api prādeśa mātra śrutiḥ abhivyakteḥ upapadyata iti āśmarathya ācāryaḥ  manyate prādeśa mātra hṛdaya pratiṣṭhena vāyam manasā anusmaryate tena prādeśa mātra iti ucyate yathā prastha mitā yavāḥ prasthā iti ucyante tadvat  yadi api ca yaveṣu sva gatam eva parimāṇam prastha saṃbandhāt vyajyate naca iha parameśvara gatam kiñcid parimāṇam asti yad hṛdaya saṃbandhāt vyajyate tathā api prayuktāyāḥ pradeśa mātra śruteḥ saṃbhavati yathā kathañcit anusmaraṇam ālambanam iti ucyate prādeśa mātra tvena vāyama prādeśa mātraḥ  api anusmaraṇīyaḥ prādeśa mātra śruti arthavattāyai evam anusmṛti nimittā parameśvare prādeśa mātraśrutiḥ iti bādariḥ ācāryaḥ  manyate saṃpatti nimittā vā syāt prādeśa mātra śrutiḥ kutas  tathā hi samāna prakaraṇam vājasaneyi brāhmaṇam dyu prabhṛtīn pṛthivī paryantān  trailokya ātmanaḥ  vaiśvānarasya avayavān adhyātma mūrdha prabhṛtiṣu cubuka paryanteṣu deha avayaveṣu saṃpādayat prādeśa mātra saṃpattim parameśvarasya darśayati iti cubukam iti adharam mukhaphalakam ucyate yadi api vājasaneyake dyauḥ atiṣṭhātu guṇa asamāmnāyata ādityaḥ ca su tejaḥ tu aguṇaḥ chāndogye punar dyaiḥ su tejaḥ tu aguṇā samāmnāyata ādityaḥ ca viśvarūpa guṇaḥ tathā api na etāvatā viśeṣeṇa kiñcid hīyate prādeśa mātra śruteḥ aviśeṣāt  sarva śākhā pratyaya tvāt ca saṃpatti nimittām prādeśa mātra śrutim yuktatarām jaimniḥ ācāryaḥ  manyate āmananti ca enam asmin āmananti ca enam parameśvaram asmin mūrdha cubuka antarāle jābālāḥ nto avyakta ātmā saḥ  avimukte pratiṣṭhita iti saḥ  avimuktaḥ kasmin pratiṣṭhita iti varaṇāyām na asyām ca madhye pratiṣṭhita iti kā vai varaṇā kā ca na asīti tatra ca imām eva nāsikām varaṇā na asi iti nirucya yā sarvāṇi indriya kṛtāni pāpāni vārayati iti sā
