varaṇā sarvāṇi indriya kṛtāni pāpāni nāśayati iti sā na asi iti punar āmananti tasmāt upapannā parameśvare prādeśa mātra śrutiḥ abhivimāna śrutiḥ pratyak ātma tva abhiprāyā pratyagātma tayā sarvaiḥ prāṇibhiḥ abhivimīyata iti abhimānaḥ abhigataḥ  vāyam pratyagātma tvāt vimānaḥ ca māna viyogāt iti abhivimānaḥ abhivimimīyate vā sarve jagat kāraṇa tvāt iti abhivimānaḥ tasmāt parameśvaraḥ  vaiśvānara iti siddham iti yadi api prāṇabhṛtaḥ  vijñāna ātmana ātma tvam cetana tvam ca saṃbhavati tathā api upādhi paricchinna jñānasya sarvajña tva ādi asaṃbhave satyasmāt eva atad śabdāt prāṇabhṛt api na dyubhvā ādi āyatana āśrayitavyaḥ naca upādhi paricchinnasya avibhoḥ prāṇabhṛtaḥ  dyubhva ādi āyatana tvam api samyaksaṃbhavati pṛthak yoga karaṇam uttara artham kutas ca na prāṇabhṛt dyabhva ādi āyatana tvena āśritavyaḥ bheda vyapadeśaḥ ca iha bhavati iti jñeya jñātṛ bhāvena tatra prāṇabhṛt tāvat mumukṣu tvāt  jñātā pariśeṣāt ātma śabda vācyam brahma dyubhva ādi āyatanam iti gamyate na prāṇabhṛt  kutas ca na prāṇabhṛt dyubhva ādi āyatana tvena āśrayitavyaḥ prakaraṇam ca idam paramātmanaḥ akasmin  u bhagavaḥ  vijñāte sarvam idam vijñātam bhavati iti eka vijñānena sarva vijñāna apekṣaṇāt parama ātmani hi sarva ātmake vijñāte sarvam idam vijñātam syāt na kevale prāṇabhṛti kutas ca na prāṇa bhṛṣ yubhva ādi āyatana tvena āśrayitavyaḥ dyubhva ādi āyatanam ca prakṛtya advā su praṇā sayujā sakhāyā iti atra sthiti adane nirdiśyete atayoḥ anyaḥ pippalam svādvatti iti karma phala aśanam aanaśnannanyaḥ  abhicāka śīti iti audāsīnyena avasthānam ca tābhyām ca sthiti adanābhyām īśvara kṣetrajñau tatra gṛhyete yadi ca īśvaraḥ  dyubhva ādi āyatana tvena vivakṣitaḥ tatas tasya prakṛtasya īśvarasya kṣetrajñāt pṛthak vacanam avakalpate anyathā hi aprakṛta vacanam ākasmikam asaṃbaddham syāt  nanu tava api kṣetrajñasya īśvarāt pṛthak vacanam ākasmikam eva prasajyeta na tasya avivakṣita tvāt kṣetrajñau hi kartṛ tvena bhoktṛ tvena ca pratiśarīram buddhi ādi upādhi saṃbaddhaḥ  lokata eva prasijaddhaḥ  na asau śrutyā tātparyeṇa vivakṣyate īśvaraḥ tu lokataḥ  aprasiddha tvāt śrutyā tātparyeṇa vivakṣyata iti na tasya ākasmikam vacanam yuktam aguhān praviṣṭau  ātmānau hi iti atra api etad darśitam advā suparṇā iti asyām ṛci īśvara kṣetrajñau  ucyete iti yadā api paiṅgī upaniṣad kṛtena vyākhyānena asyāmṛci sattva kṣetrajñau  ucyete tadā api na virodhaḥ kaścid  katham prāṇabhṛt hi iha ghaṭa ādi  chidravat sattva ādi upādhi abhimāni tvena pratiśarīram gṛhyamāṇaḥ  dyubhva ādi āyatanam na bhavati iti niṣidhyate yaḥ tu sarva śarīreṣu upādhibhiḥ vinā upalakṣyate na bhavati iti niṣidhyate yaḥ tu sarva śarīreṣu upādhibhiḥ vinā upalakṣyate paramātmā eva sa bhavati yathā ghaṭa ādi  chidrāṇi ghaṭa ādibhiḥ upādhibhiḥ vinā upalakṣyamāṇāni mahā ākāśa eva bhavanti tadvat prāṇabhṛtaḥ parasmāt anyatva anupapatteḥ pratiṣedhaḥ  na upapadyate tasmāt sattva ādi upādhi abhimānina eva dyubhva ādi āyatana tva pratiṣedhaḥ tasmāt param eva brahma dyubhva ādi āyatanam tad etad aadṛśya tva ādi guṇa kaḥ  dharma ukteḥ iti anena eva siddham tasya eva hi bhūta yoni vākyasya madhya idam paṭhitam ayasmin dyauḥ pṛthivī ca antarikṣam iti prapañca artham tu punar upanyastam bhūma adhikaraṇam sū bhūmā saṃprasādāt  adhyupadeśāt  idam samāmananti ityādi tatra saṃśayaḥ bhūma iti tāvat bahu tvam abhidhīyate abahoḥ lopaḥ  bhū ca bahoḥ iti bhūma śabdasya bhāva pratyaya antatā smāraṇāt  kimātmakam punar tad bahutvam iti viśeṣa ākāṅkṣāyām aprāṇaḥ  vā āśā bhūyān iti saṃnidhānāt prāṇaḥ  bhūma iti pratibhāti tathā aśrutam hi eva me bhagavat dṛśebhyaḥ tarati śokam ātma vid iti saḥ  aham bhagavaḥ śocāmi tam mā bhagavān śokasya pāram tārayatu iti prakaraṇa utthānāt paramātmā bhūma iti api pratibhāti tatra kasya upādanam nyāyyam kasya vā hānam iti bhavati saṃśayaḥ kim tāvat prāptam prāṇaḥ  bhūma iti kasmāt  bhūyas  praśna prativacana paraṃpara adarśanāt  yathā hi aasti bhagavaḥ  nāmnaḥ  bhūyaḥ iti avāgvāva nāmnaḥ  bhūyasī iti tathā aasti bhagavaḥ  nāmnaḥ  bhūyaḥ iti manaḥ  vāva vācaḥ  bhūyaḥ iti ca nāma ādibhyaḥ  hi ā prāṇāt bhūyaḥ praśna prativacana pravāhaḥ pravṛttaḥ na evam prāṇāt param bhūyas praśna prativacanam dṛśyate asti bhagavaḥ prāṇāt bhūya iti ādaḥ  vāva prāṇāt bhūya iti prāṇam eva tu nāma ādibhya āśāntebhyaḥ  bhūyāsam aprāṇaḥ  vā āśāyā bhūyān ityādinā sa prapañcamuktvā prāṇa darśinaḥ ca ativādi tvam iti abhyanujñāya aeṣa tu vā ativadati yaḥ satyena ativadati iti prāṇa vratam ativādi tvam anukṛṣya aparityajya eva prāṇam satya ādi paramparayā bhūmānam avatārayan prāṇam eva bhūmānam manyanta iti gamyate katham punar  prāṇe bhūmani vyākhyāyamāne ayatra na anyat paśyati iti etad bhūmno lakṣaṇa param vacanam vyākhyāyeta iti ucyate suṣupti avasthāyām prāṇa grasteṣu karaṇeṣu darśana ādi vyavahāra nivṛtti darśanāt saṃbhavati prāṇasya api ayatra na anyat paśyati iti etad lakṣaṇam tathā ca śrutiḥ ana śṛṇoti na paśyati ityādinā sarva karaṇa vyāpāra pratyastamaya rūpām suṣupti avasthām uktvā aprāṇa agnaya eva etasmin pure jāgrati iti tasyām eva avasthāyām pañca vṛtteḥ prāṇasya jāgaraṇam bruvatī prāṇa pradhānām suṣupti avasthām darśayati yad ca etad bhūmnaḥ sukha tvam śrutam iti tad api aviruddham aatra eṣa devaḥ svapnāt na paśyati atha yad etasmin śarīre sukham bhavati iti suṣupti avasthāyām eva sukha śravaṇāt  yad ca ayaḥ  vai bhūmā tad amṛtam iti tad api prāṇasya aviruddham aprāṇaḥ  vā amṛtam iti śruteḥ katham punar  prāṇam bhūmānam manyamānasya tarati śokam ātma vid  iti ātma vividiṣayā prakaraṇasya utthānam upapadyate prāṇa eva iha ātmā vivakṣita iti brūmaḥ tathā hi iti prāṇam eva sarva ātmānam karoti ayathā vā arā nābhau samarpitā evam asmin prāṇe sarvam samarpitam iti ca sarva ātma tvāra nābhi nidarśanābhyām ca saṃbhavati vaipulya ātmikā bhūma rūpa tā prāṇasya tasmāt prāṇaḥ  bhūma iti evam prāptam tatas  idam ucyate paramātmā eva iha bhūmā bhavitum arhati na prāṇaḥ kasmāt  saṃprasādāt adhi upadeśāt saṃprasāda iti suṣuptam sthānam ucyate samyak prasīdati asmin  iti nirvacanāt  bṛhadāraṇyake ca svapna jāgarita sthānābhyām saha pāṭhāt  tasyām ca saṃprasāda avasthāyām prāṇaḥ  jāgarti iti prāṇaḥ  atra saṃprasādaḥ  abhipreyate prāṇāt ūrdhvam bhūmna upadiśyamāna tvāt iti arthaḥ prāṇa eva ced bhūma āsyāt sa eva tasmāt ūrdhvam upadiśyeta ityaśliṣṭam eva etad syāt  na hi nāma eva nāmnaḥ  bhūya iti nāmna ūrdhvam upadiṣṭam kim tarhi nāmnaḥ  anyat artha antaram upadiṣṭam vāc ākhyam iti tathā vāc ādibhyaḥ  api ā prāṇāt artha antaram eva tatra tatra ūrdhvam upadiṣṭam tadvat prāṇāt ūrdhvam upadiśyamānaḥ  bhūmā prāṇāt artha antara bhūtaḥ  bhavitum arhati nanu iha na asti praśnaḥ  asti bhagavaḥ prāṇāt bhūya iti na api prativacanam asti prāṇāt vāva bhūyo asti iti katham prāṇāt adhi bhūma upadiśyate prāṇa viṣayam eva ca ativādi tvām uttaratra anukṛṣyamāṇam paśyāmaḥ iti tasmāt na asti prādadhyupadeśa iti atra ucyate na tāvat prāṇa viṣayasya eva ativādi tvasya etad anukarṣaṇam iti śakyam vaktum viśeṣa vādāt  ayaḥ satyena ativadati iti nanu viśeṣa vādaḥ  api ayam prāṇa viṣaya eva bhaviṣyati katham yathā eṣo agnihotrī yaḥ satyam vadati iti ukte na satyavat anena agnihotri tvam kena tarhi agnihotreṇa eva satya vadanam tvagnihotriṇaḥ  viśeṣa ucyate tathā aeṣa tu vā ativadati yaḥ satyena ativadati iti ukte na satya vadanena ativādi tvam kena tarhi prakṛtena prāṇa vijñānena eva satya vadanam tu prāṇa vidaḥ  viśeṣaḥ  vivakṣyata iti na iti brūmaḥ śruti artha parityāga prasaṅgāt  śrutyā hi atra satya vadanena ativādi tvam pratīyate tivadati iti na atra prāṇa vijñānasya saṃkīrtanam asti prakaraṇāt tu prāṇa vijñānam saṃbadhyeta tatra prakaraṇa anurodhena śrutiḥ parityaktā syāt  prakṛta vyāvṛtti arthaḥ ca tuśabdaḥ  na saṃgacchate aeṣa tu vā ativadati iti asatyam tu eva vijijñāsitavyam iti ca prayatna antara karaṇam artha antara vivakṣām sūcayati tasmāt yathā eka veda praśaṃsāyām prakṛtāyām eṣa tu mahā brāhmaṇaḥ  yaḥ caturaḥ  vedān adhīta iti eka vedebhyor atha antara bhūtaḥ catur vedaḥ praśasyate tādṛś etad draṣṭavyam na ca praśna prativacana rūpayā eva artha antara vivakṣayā bhavitavyam iti niyamaḥ  asti prakṛta saṃbandha asaṃbhava kārita tvāt artha antara vivakṣāyāḥ tatra prāṇāntam anuśāsanam śrutvā tūṣṇībhūtam nāradam svayam eva sanatkumāraḥ  vyutpādayati yad prāṇa vijñānena vikāra anṛta viṣayeṇa ativādi tvam anativādi tvam eva tad  aeṣa tu vā ativadati yaḥ satyena ativadati iti tatra satyam iti param brahmā ucyate parama artha rūpa tvāt asatyam jñānam anantam brahma iti ca śruti antarāt tathā vyutpāditāya nāradāya asaḥ  aham bhagavaḥ satyena ativadāni iti evam pravṛttāya vijñāna ādi sādhana paramparayā bhūmānam upadiśati tatra yad prāṇāt adhi satyam vaktavyam pratijñātam tad eva iha bhūma iti ucyata iti gamyate tasmāt asti prāṇāt adhi bhūmna upadeśa iti atas  prāṇāt anyaḥ paramātmā bhūmā bhavitum arhati evan ca iha ātma vividiṣayā prakaraṇasya utthānam upapannam bhaviṣyati prāṇa eva iha ātmā vivakṣita iti etad api na upapadyate na hi prāṇasya mukhyayā vṛtti ātma tvam asti naca anyatra paramātma jñānāt śoka vinivṛttiḥ asti anānyaḥ panthā vidyate ayanāya iti śruti antarāt atam mā bhagavān śokasya pāram tārayatu iti ca upakramya upasaṃharati iti tama iti śoka ādi kāraṇam avidyā ucyate prāṇānte ca anuśāsane na prāṇasya anyāyat tatocyeta aātmataḥ prāṇaḥ iti ca brāhmaṇam prakaraṇa ante parama ātma vivakṣā bhaviṣyati abhūmā tu prāṇa eva iti ced na asa bhagavaḥ kasmin pratiṣṭhita iti sve mahimni ityādinā bhūmna eva prakaraṇa samāpteḥ anukarṣaṇāt  vaipulya ātmikā ca bhūma rūpa tā sarva kāraṇa tvāt paramātmanaḥ sutarām upapadyate apica ye bhūmni śrūyante dharmāḥ te paramātmani upapadyante ayatra na anyat paśyati na anyat śṛṇoti na anyat vajānāti sa bhūmā iti darśana ādi vyavahāra abhāvam bhūmāni avagamayati parama ātmani ca ayam darśana ādi vyavahāra abhāvaḥ  avagataḥ ayatra tu asya sarvam ātmā eva abhūt tad kena kam paśyet ityādi śruti antarāt yaḥ  api asau suṣupta avasthāyām darśana ādi vyavahāra abhāva uktaḥ saḥ  api ātmana eva asaṅga tva vivakṣayā uktaḥ  na prāṇa svabhāva vivakṣayā paramātma prakaraṇāt  yad api tasyām avasthāyām sukham uktam tad api ātmana eva sukha rūpatva vivakṣayā uktam yata āha sya parama  ānanda etasya eva ānandasya anyāni bhūtāni mātrām upajīvanti iti iha api ayaḥ  vai bhūmā tad sukham na alpe sukham asti bhūmā eva sukham iti sāmaya sukha nirākaraṇena brahmā eva sukham bhūmānam darśayati ayaḥ  vai bhūmā tad amṛtam iti amṛta tvam api iha śrūyamāṇam parama kāraṇam gamayati vikārāṇa am ṛta tvasya āpekṣika tvāt aatas  anyat ārtam iti ca śruti antarāt tathā ca satya tvam sva mahima pratiṣṭhita tvam sarva gata tvam sarvāttma tvam iti ca ete dharmāḥ śrūyamāṇāḥ paramātmani eva upapadyante na anyatra tasmāt bhūma iti siddham akasmin  u khalu ākāśa otaḥ ca protaḥ ca iti sa ha uvāca etad vai tad akṣaram gārgi brāhmaṇā abhivadanti asthūlam anaṇu ityādi śrūyate tatra saṃśayaḥ kim akṣara śabdena varṇa ucyate kiṃvā parameśvara iti tatra akṣara samāmnāya iti ādau  akṣara śabdasya varṇe prasiddha tvāt  prasiddhi atikramasya ca ayukta tvāt  aoṅkāra eva idam sarvam iti ādau ca śruti antare varṇasya api upāsya tvena sarva ātmaka tva avadhāraṇāt varṇa eva akṣara śabda iti evam prāpta ucyate para eva ātma akṣara śabda vācyaḥ kasmāt  ambara anta dhṛteḥ pṛthivī ādeḥ ākāśa antasya vikāra jātasya dhāraṇāt  tatra hi pṛthivī ādeḥ samasta vikāra jātasya kāla traya vibhaktasya aākāśa eva tadā utam ca protam ca iti ākāśe pratiṣṭhita tvam uktvā akasmin  u khalu ākāśa otaḥ ca protaḥ ca iti anena praśnena idam akṣaram avatāritam tathā ca upasaṃhṛtam iti naca iyam ambara anta dhṛtiḥ brahmaṇaḥ  anyatra saṃbhavati yad api aoṅkāra eva idam sarvam iti tad api brahma pratipatti sādhana tvāt stuti artham draṣṭavyam tasmāt na kṣarati aśnute ca iti nitya tva avyāpita tvābhyām akṣaram param eva brahma asyāt etad kāryasya ced kāraṇa adhīna tvam ambara anta dhṛtiḥ abhyupagamyate pradhāna kāraṇa vādinaḥ  api iyam upapadyate katham ambara anta dhṛteḥ brahma tva pratipattiḥ ata uttaram paṭhati sā ca ambara anta dhṛtiḥ parameśvarasya eva karma kasmāt  praśāsanāt  praśāsanam hi iha śrūyate ityādi praśāsanam ca pārameśvaram karma na acetanasya pradhānasya praśāsanam bhavati na hi acetanānām ghaṭa ādi kāraṇānām mṛd ādīnām ghaṭa ādi viṣayam praśāsanam asti anya bhāva vyāvṛtteḥ ca anya bhāva vyāvṛtteḥ ca kāraṇāt brahma eva akṣara śabda vācyam tasya eva ambara anta dhṛtiḥ karma na anyasya kasya cit  kim idam anya bhāva vyāvṛtteḥ iti anyasya bhāvo anya bhāvasi asmāt vyāvṛttiḥ anya bhāva vyāvṛttiḥ iti etad uktam bhavati dhṛteḥ ca hetoḥ parameśvara eva ayam daharaḥ katham adaharaḥ  asmin  antara ākāśaḥ iti hi prakṛti ākāśa aupamya pūrvakam tasmin sarva samādhānam uktvā tām smin  eva ca ātma śabdam prayujya apahata pāpma tva ādi guṇa yogam ca upaduśya tam eva anati vṛtta prakaraṇam nirdiśati iti tatra vidhṛtiḥ iti ātma śabda sāmāna adhikaraṇyāt vidhārayitā ucyate kticaḥ kartari smaraṇāt  yathā udaka saṃtānasya vidhārayitā loke setuḥ kṣetra saṃpadām asaṃbhedāya evam ayam ātma ātmā eṣām adhyātma ādi bheda bhinnānām lokānām varṇa āśrama ādīnām ca vidhāritā setuḥ asaṃbhedāya asaṃkarāya iti evam iha prakṛte dahare vidhāraṇa lakṣaṇam mahimānam darśayati ayam ca mahimā parameśvara eva śruti antarāt upalabhyate aetasya vā akṣarasya praśāsane gārgi sūryācandramasau vidhṛtau tiṣṭhataḥ iti ādeḥ tathā anyatra api niścite parameśvara vākye śrūyate iti evam dhṛteḥ ca hetoḥ parameśvara eva ayam daharaḥ itas ca parameśvara eva adaharaḥ  asmin  antara ākāśaḥ iti ucyate yad kāraṇam ākāśa śabdaḥ parameśvare prasiddhaḥ aākāśaḥ  vai nāma nāma rūpayoḥ nirvahitā asarvāṇi ha vā imāni bhūtāni ākāśāt eva samutpadyante iti ādi prayoga darśanāt jīve tu na kvacid ākāśa śabdaḥ prayujyamānaḥ  dṛśyate bhūtākāśaḥ tu satyām api ākāśa śabda prasiddhau  upamāna upameya bhāva ādi asaṃbhavān na grahītavya iti uktam yadi vākya śeṣa balena dahara iti parameśvaraḥ parigṛhyeta asti itarasya api jīvasya vākya śeṣe parāmarśaḥ smāt śarīrāt samutthāya param jyoti rūpa saṃpadya svena rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyata eṣa ātmā iti ha uvāca iti atra hi saṃprasāda śabdaḥ śruti antare suṣupta avasthāyām dṛṣṭa tvāt tad avasthāvantam jīvam śaknoti upasthāpayitum na artha antaram tathā śarīra vyapāśrayasya iva jīvasya śarīrāt samutthānam saṃbhavati yathā ākāśa vyapāśrayāṇām vāyu ādīnām ākāśāt samutthānam tadvat  yathā ca adṛṣṭaḥ  api loke parameśvara viṣaya ākāśa śabdaḥ parameśvara dharma samabhivyāhārāt aākāśaḥ  vai nāma nāma rūpayoḥ nirvahitā iti evamādau parameśvara viṣayaḥ  abhyupagata evam jīva viṣayaḥ  api bhaviṣyati tasmāt itara parāmarśāt adaharaḥ  asmin  antara ākāśa iti atra sa eva jīva ucyate iti ced  na etad evam syāt  kasmāt  asaṃbhavāt  na hi jīvaḥ  buddhi ādi upādhi pariccheda abhimānī san  ākāśena upamīyeta naca upādhi dharmān abhimanyamānasya apahata pāpma tvāt ayaḥ  dharmāḥ saṃbhavanti prapañcitam ca etad prathama sūtre atireka āśaṅkā parihāra āya atra tu punar upanyastam paṭhiṣyati ca upariṣṭāt  aanya arthaḥ ca parāmarśaḥ iti itara parāmarśa ādyā jīvāśaṅkā jātā sa asaṃbhavāt nirākṛtā atha idānīm mṛtasya iva amṛta sekāt punar  samutthānam jīvāśaṅkāyāḥ kriyate uttarasmāt prajāpatyāt vākyāt  tatra hi aya ātma apahata pāpmā iti apahata pāpma tva ādi guṇakam ātmānam anveṣṭavyam vijijñāsitavyam ca pratijñāya aya eṣaḥ  akṣiṇi puruṣaḥ  dṛśyata eṣa ātmā iti bruvan  akṣi stham draṣṭāram jīvam ātmānam nirdiśati aetam tu eva te bhūyo anuvyākhyāsyāmi iti ca tam eva punar  punar  parāmṛśya aya eṣa svapne mahīyamānaḥ carati eṣa ātmā iti atad yatra etad suptaḥ samastaḥ saṃprasannaḥ svapnam na vijānāti eṣa ātmā iti ca jīvam eva avasthā antara gatam vyācaṣṭe tasya eva cāpahata pāpma tva ādi darśayati iti na aham khalu ayam evam saṃprati ātmānam jānātyayam aham asmi iti no eva imāni bhūtāni iti ca suṣupta avasthāyām doṣam upalabhya aetam tu eva te bhūyo anuvyākhyāsyāmi no eva anyatra etasmāt  iti ca upakramya śarīra saṃbandha nindā pūrvakam aeṣa saṃprasādaḥ  asmāt śarīrāt samutthāya param jyotiḥ upasaṃpadya svena rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyate sa uttamaḥ puruṣaḥ iti jīvam eva śarīrāt samutthitam uttama puruṣam darśayati tasmāt asti saṃbhavaḥ  jīve pārameśvarāṇām dharmāṇām atas  adaharaḥ  asmin  antara ākāśaḥ iti jīva eva ukta iti ced kaścid brūyāt  tam prati brūyāt  iti tuśabdaḥ pūrva pakṣa vyāvṛtti arthaḥ na uttarasmāt api vākyāt iha jīvasya āśaṅkā saṃbhavati iti arthaḥ kasmāt  yatas tatra api āvirbhūta svarūpaḥ  jīvaḥ  vivakṣyate āvirbhūtam svarūpam asya iti āvirbhūta svarūpaḥ bhūta pūrva gatyā jīva vacanam etad uktam bhavati kṣiṇi iti akṣi lakṣitam draṣṭāram nirdiśya udaśa rāva brāhmaṇena enam śarīra ātma tāyā vyutthāpya aetam tu eva te iti punar punar tam eva vyākhyāyeya tvena ākṛṣya svapna suṣupta upanyāsa krameṇa aparam jyotiḥ upasaṃpadya svena rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyate iti yad asya pāramārthikam svarūpam param brahma tad rūpa tayā enam jīvam vyācaṣṭe na jaivena rūpeṇa yad param jyoti rūpa saṃpattavyam śrutam tad param brahma tad ca apahata pāpma tva ādi dharmakam tad eva ca jīvasya pāramārthikam svarūpam atattvam asi ityādi śāstrebhyaḥ na itarat upādhi kalpitam yāvat eva hi sthāṇau  iva puruṣa buddhim dvaita lakṣaṇām avidyām nivartayan kūṭastha nitya dṛś svarūpam ātmānam aham brahma asmi iti na pratipadyate tāvat jīvasya jīva tvam yadā tu deha indriya manaḥ buddhi saṃghātāt vyutthāpya śrutyā pratibodhyate na asi tvam deha indriya manaḥ buddhi saṃghātaḥ na asi saṃsārī kim tarhi tad yad satyam sa ātmā caitanya mātra svarūpaḥ tattvam asi iti tadā kūca stha nitya dṛś svarūpam ātmānam pratibuda dhyā asmāt śarīra ādi abhimānāt samuttiṣṭhan sa eva kūṭastha nitya dṛś svarūpa ātmā bhavati asa yaḥ  ha vai tad paramam brahma veda brahmā eva bhavati ityādi śrutibhyaḥ tad eva ca asya pāramārthikam svarūpam yena śarīrāt samutthāya svena rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyate katham punar  svam ca rūpam svena eva niṣpadyata iti saṃbhavati kūṭastha nityasya suvarṇa ādīnām tu dravya antara saṃparkāt abhibhūta svarūpāṇām anabhivyakta asādhāraṇa viśeṣāṇām kṣāra prakṣepa ādibhiḥ śodhyamānānām sva rūpeṇa abhiniṣpattiḥ syāt  tathā nakṣatra ādīnām ahani abhibhūta prakāśānām abhibhāvaka viyoge rātrau sva rūpeṇa abhiniṣpattiḥ syāt  na tu tathā ātma caitanya jyotiṣaḥ  nityasya kenacid abhibhavaḥ saṃbhavati asaṃsargi tvāt vyomna iva dṛṣṭa virodhāt ca dṛṣṭi śruti mati vijñātayo hi jīvasya svarūpam tad ca śarīrāt asamutthitasya api jīvasya sadā niṣpannam eva dṛśyate sarvaḥ  hi jīvaḥ paśyan śṛṇvan manvānaḥ  vijānan vyavaharati anyathā vyavahāra anupapatteḥ tad ced śarīrāt samutthitasya niṣpadyeta prāk samutthānāt dṛṣṭaḥ  vyavahāraḥ  virudhyeta atas  kimātmakam idam śarīrāt samutthānam kimātmikā vā svarūpeṇa abhiniṣpattiḥ iti atra ucyate prāk viveka vijñāna utpatteḥ śarīra indriya manaḥ buddhi viṣaya vedanā upādhibhiḥ avi viktam iva jīvasya dṛṣṭi ādi jyotiḥ svarūpam bhavati yathā śuddhasya sphaṭikasya svācchyam śauklyam ca svarūpam prāk viveka grahaṇāt rakta nīla ādi upādhibhiḥ avi viktam iva bhavati pramāṇa janita viveka grahaṇāt tu parācīnaḥ sphaṭikaḥ svācchyena śauklyena ca svena rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyata iti ucyate prāk api tathā eva san tathā deha ādi upādhi aviviktasya eva sataḥ  jīvasya śruti kṛtam viveka vijñānam śarīrāt samutthānam viveka vijñāna phalam sva rūpeṇa abhiniṣpattiḥ kevala ātma svarūpa avagatiḥ tathā vivekauviveka mātreṇa eva ātmanaḥ  aśarīra tvam sa śarīra tvam ca mantra varṇāt  aaśarīram śarīra iṣu iti aśarīra sthaḥ  api kaunteya na karoti na lipyate iti ca sa śarīra tva aśarīra tva viśeṣa abhāva smaraṇāt  tasmāt viveka vijñāna abhāvāt anāvirbhūta svarūpaḥ san viveka vijñānāt āvirbhūta svarūpa iti ucyate natvā anyādṛśau  āvirbhāva an āvirbhāvau svarūpasya saṃbhavataḥ sva rūpa tvāt eva evam mithyājñāna kṛta eva jīva parameśvarayoḥ bhedaḥ  na vastu kṛtaḥ vyomavat asaṅga tva aviśeṣāt kutaścid evam pratipattavyam yatas  aya eṣaḥ  akṣiṇi puruṣaḥ  dṛśyate iti upadiśya aetat amṛtam abhayam etad brahma iti upadiśati yaḥ  akṣiṇi prasiddhaḥ  draṣṭā draṣṭṛ tvena vibhāvyate saḥ  amṛta abhaya lakṣaṇāt brahmaṇaḥ  anyaḥ ced syāt tatas  amṛta abhaya brahma sāmānā adh ikaraṇyam na syāt  na api praticchāyā ātmā ayam akṣi lakṣitaḥ  nirdiśyate prajāpateḥ mṛṣau  ādi tva prasaṅgāt  tathā dvitīye api paryāye aya eṣaḥ svapne mahīyamānaḥ carati iti na prathama paryāya nirdiṣṭāt akṣi puruṣāt draṣṭuḥ anyaḥ  nirdiṣṭaḥ aetam tu eva te bhūyo anuvyākhyāsyāmi iti upakramāt  kiñca aham adya svapne hastinam adrākṣam na idānīm tam paśyāmi iti dṛṣṭam eva pratibuddhaḥ pratyācaṣṭe draṣṭāram tu tam eva pratyabhijānāti ya eva aham svapnam adrākṣam sa eva aham jāgaritam paśyami iti tathā tṛtīye api paryāye anahi khalu ayam evam saṃprati ātmānam jānātyayam aham asmi iti no eva imāni bhūtāni iti suṣupta avasthāyām viśeṣa vijñāna abhāvam eva darśayati na vijñātāram pratiṣedhati yad tu tatra avināśam eva apītaḥ  bhavati iti tad api viśeṣa vijñāna vināśa abhiprāyam eva na vijñātṛ vināśa abhiprāyam anahi vijñātuḥ vijñāteḥ viparilopaḥ  vidyate avināśi tvāt iti śruti antarāt tathā caturthe api paryāye aetam tu eva te bhūyo anuvyākhyāsyāmi no eva anyatra etasmāt iti upakramya amaghavat martyam vā idam śarīram ityādinā prapañcena śarīrāt upādhi saṃbandha pratyākhyānena saṃprasāda śabda uditam jīvam asvena rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyate iti brahma svarūpa āpannam darśayan  parasmāt brahmaṇaḥ  amṛta abhaya svarūpāt anyam jīvam darśayati kecid tu paramātma vivakṣāyām aetam tu eva te iti jīvākarṣaṇam anyāyyam manyamānā etam eva vākya upakrama sūcitam apahata pāpma tva ādi guṇakam ātmānam te bhūyo anuvyākhyāsyāmi iti kalpayanti teṣām etam iti saṃnihitā avalambinī sarvanāma śrutiḥ viprakṛṣyeta bhūyas śrutiḥ ca uparudhyeta paryāya antara abhihitasya paryāya antare anabhidhīyamāna tvāt  aetam tu eva te iti ca pratijñāya prāc caturthāt paryāyāt anyam anyam vyācakṣāṇasya prajāpateḥ pratāraka tvam prasajyeta tasmāt yad avidyā pratyupasthāpita pārama arthikam jaivam rūpam kartṛ bhoktṛ rāga dveṣa ādi doṣa kaluṣitam aneka anartha yogi tad vilayanena tad viparītam apahata pāpma tva ādi guṇakam pārameśvaram svarūpam vidyayā pratipādyate sarpa ādi vilayanena iva rajju ādīn apare tu vādinaḥ pāramārthikam eva jaivam rūpam iti manyante asmadīyāḥ ca kecid  teṣām sarveṣām ātmā ekatva samyak darśana pratipakṣa bhūtānām pratibodhāya idam śārīrakam ārabdham eka eva parameśvaraḥ kūṭastha nityaḥ  vijñāna dhātuḥ avidyayā māyayā māyā vivat anekadhā vibhāvyate na anyaḥ  vijñāna dhātuḥ asti iti yad tu idam parameśvara vākye jīvam āśaṅkhya pratiṣedhati sūtra kāraḥ ityādinā tatra ayam abhiprāyaḥ nitya śuddha buddha mukta svabhāve kūṭastha nitye ekasmin  asaṅge parama ātmani tad viparītam jaivam rūpam vyomni iva tala mala ādi parikalpitam tad ātmā ekatva pratipādana paraiḥ vākyaiḥ nyāya upetaiḥ dvaita vāda pratiṣedhaiḥ ca apaneṣyāmi iti paramātmanaḥ  jīvāt anya tvam draḍhayati jīvasya tu na parasmāt anya tvam pratipipādayiṣati kim tu anuvadati eva avidyā kalpitam loka prasiddham jīva bhedam evam hi svābhāvika kartṛ tva bhoktṛ tva anuvādena pravṛttāḥ karma vidhayaḥ  na virudhyanta iti manyate pratipādyam tu śāstra artham ātmā eka tvam eva darśayati ityādinā avarṇiḥ ca asmābhiḥ vidvat bhedena karma vidhi virodha parihāraḥ yad api uktam adaharaḥ  asmin  antara ākāśaḥ iti ākāśasya alpa tvam śrūyamāṇam parameśvare na upapadyate jīvasya tvārāgra upanimitasya alpa tvam avakalpata iti tasya parihāraḥ  vaktavyaḥ uktaḥ  hi asya parihāraḥ parameśvarasya āpekṣikam alpa tvam avakalpata iti aarbhakaukaḥ tvāt tad vyapadeśāt ca na iti ced na nicāyya tvāt evam vyomavat ca iti atra sa eva iha parihāraḥ  anusaṃdhātavya iti sūcayati śrutyā eva ca idam alpa tvam pratyuktam prasiddhena ākāśena upamimānayā ayāvān vā ayam ākāśaḥ tā  ān eṣaḥ  antar hṛdaya ākāśaḥ iti anukṛti adhikaraṇam sū anukṛteḥ  tasya ca ana tatra sūryaḥ  bhāti na candra tārakam na imā vidyutaḥ  bhānti kuto ayama agniḥ tam eva bhāntam anubhāti sarvam tasya bhāsā sarvam idam vibhāti iti samāmananti yatra yam bhāntam anubhāti sarvam yasya ca bhāsā sarvam idam vibhāti sa kim tejaḥ dhātuḥ kaścid uta prājña ātmā iti vicikitsāyām tejaḥ dhātuḥ iti tāvat prāptam kutas  tejaḥ dhātūnām eva surī ādīnām bhāna pratiṣedhāt  tejaḥ svabhāvakam hi candra tāraka ādi tejaḥ svabhāvaka eva suryaḥ  bhāsamāne ahani na bhāsata iti prasiddham tathā saha sūryeṇa sarvam idam candra tāraka ādi yasmin  bhāsate saḥ  api tejaḥ svabhāva eva kaścid iti avagamyate anubhānam api tejaḥ svabhāvaka eva u apapadyate samāna svabhāvakeṣu anukāra darśanāt  gacchantam anugacchati itivat  tasmāt tejaḥ dhātuḥ kaścid iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ prājña eva ātmā bhavitum arhati kasmāt  anukṛteḥ anukaraṇam anukṛtiḥ yad etad  atam eva bhāntam anubhāti sarvam iti anubhānam tad prājña parigrahe avakalpate abhārūpaḥ satya saṃkalpaḥ iti hi prājñam ātmānam āmananti na tu tejaḥ dhātum kañcid sūryāt ayaḥ  anubhānti iti prasiddham sama tvāt ca tejaḥ dhātūnām sūrya ādīnām na tejaḥ dhātum anyam pratyapekṣā asti yam bhāntam anubhāyuḥ na hi pradīpaḥ pradīpa antaram anubhāti yad api uktam samāna svabhāvakeṣu anukāraḥ  dṛśyata iti na ayam ekāntaḥ  niyamaḥ bhinna svabhāvakeṣu api hi anukāraḥ  dṛśyate yathā su taptaḥ  ayaḥ piṇḍaḥ  agni anukṛtiḥ agnim dahantam anudahati bhaumam vā rajaḥ  vāyum vahantam anuvahanti iti anukṛteḥ iti anubhāna m asūsucat tasya ca iti caturtham pādam asya ślokasya sūcayati atasya bhāsā sarvam idam vibhāti iti tadhetukam bhānam sūryādeḥ ucyamānam prājñam ātmānam gamayati atad devā jyotiṣām jyotiḥ āyuḥ hepa āsate amṛtam iti hi prājñam ātmānam āmananti tejaḥ ntareṇa surī ādi tejaḥ  vibhāti iti aprasiddham viruddham ca tejaḥ ntareṇa tejontarasya pratidhātāt  athavā na sūrya ādīnam eva śloka paripaṭhitānām idam tad hetukam vibhānam ucyate kim tarhi asarvam idam iti aviśeṣa śruteḥ sarvasya eva asya nāma rūpa kriyā kāraka phala jātasya yā abhivyaktiḥ sā brahma jyotiḥ sattā nimittā yathā sūrya ādi jyotiḥ sattā nimittā sarvasya rūpa jātasya abhivyaktiḥ tadvat  ana tatra sūryaḥ  bhāti iti ca tatra śabdam āharan prakṛta grahaṇam darśayati prakṛtam ca brahma ayasmin dyauḥ pṛthivī ca antarikṣamotam ityādinā anantaram ca ahiraṇmaye pare kośe virajam brahma niṣphalam tad śubhram jyotiṣām jyotiḥ tad yad ātma vidaḥ  viduḥ iti katham tad jyotiṣām jyotiḥ ityata idam utthitam iti yad api uktam sūrya ādīnām tejasām bhāna pratiṣedhaḥ tejaḥ dhātau  evanyasmin  avakalpate sūrya iva itareṣām iti tatra tu sa eva tejaḥ dhātuḥ anyaḥ  na saṃbhavati iti upapāditam brahmaṇi api ca eṣām bhāna pratiṣedhaḥ  avakalpate yatas  yad upalabhante tad sarvam brahmaṇā eva jyotiṣā upalabhyate brahma tu na anyena jyotiṣā upalabhyate svayam jyotiḥ svarūpa tvāt yena sūrya ādayaḥ tasmin bhāyuḥ brahma hi ānyat vyanakti na tu brahma anyena vyajyate aātmanā eva ayam jyotiṣāḥ te aāgṛhyaḥ  na hi gṛhyate ityādi śrutibhyaḥ apicedṛś rūpa tvam prājñasya eva etmanaḥ smaryate bhagavadgītāsu iti ayat āditya gatam tejaḥ  jagat bhāsayate akhilam yad candramasi yad ca agnau tad tejaḥ  viddhi māmakam iti ca pramita adhikaraṇam sū śabdāt  eva pramitaḥ aaṅguṣṭa mātraḥ puruṣaḥ madhya ātmani tiṣṭhati iti śrūyate tathā aṅguṣṭa mātraḥ puruṣaḥ  jyotiḥ iva ādhūmakaḥ īśānaḥ  bhūta bhavyasya sa eva adya sa u śva etad vai tad iti ca tatra yaḥ  ayam aṅguṣṭha mātraḥ puruṣaḥ śrūyate sa kim vijñāna ātmā kiṃvā paramātmā iti saṃśayaḥ tatra parimāṇa upadeśāt tāvat vijñāna ātmā iti prāptam na hi ananta āyāma vistārasya paramātmanaḥ  aṅguṣṭha parimāṇam upapadyate vijñāna ātma nanaḥ tu upādhimat tvāt saṃbhavati kayācid kalpanayā aṅguṣṭha mātra tvam smṛteḥ ca iti na hi parameśvaraḥ  balāt yamena niṣkraṣṭum śakyaḥ tena tatra saṃsāri aṅguṣṭha mātraḥ  niścitaḥ sa eva iha api iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ paramātmā eva ayam aṅguṣṭha mātra parimitaḥ puruṣaḥ  bhavitum arhati kasmāt  śabdāt  aīśānaḥ  bhūta bhavyasya iti na hi anyaḥ parameśvarāt bhūta bhavyasya niraṅ kuśam īśitā aetat vai tad iti ca prakṛtam pṛṣṭam iha anusaṃdadhāti etad vai tad yad pṛṣṭam brahma iti arthaḥ pṛṣṭam ca iha brahma aanyatra dharmāt anyatra adharmāt anyatra asmāt kṛta akṛtāt  anyatra bhūtāt ca bhavyāt ca yad tad paśyasi tadvat iti śabdāt eva iti abhidhāna śruteḥ eva īśāna iti parameśvaraḥ  ayam gamyata iti arthaḥ katham punar  sarva gatasya paramātmanaḥ parimāṇa upadeśa iti atra brūmaḥ sarva gatasya api paramātmanaḥ  hṛdaye avasthānam apekṣya aṅguṣṭha mātra tvam idam ucyate ākāśasya iva vaṃśa parva apekṣa mara tri mātra tvam na hi añjasā atimātrasya paramātmanaḥ  aṅguṣṭha mātra tvam upapadyate na ca anyaḥ paramātmana iha grahaṇam arhati īśāna śabda ādibhya iti uktam nanu pratiprāṇi bhedam hṛdayānām anavasthita tvāt apekṣam api aṅguṣṭha mātra tvam na upapadyata iti ata uttaram ucyate manuṣya adhikāra tvāt iti śāstram hi aviśeṣa pravṛttam api manuṣyān eva adhikaroti śakta tvāt arthi tvāt aparyudasta tvāt upanayana ādi śāstrāt ca iti varṇitam etad adhikāra lakṣaṇe manuṣyāṇām ca niyata parimāṇaḥ kāyaḥ aucityena niyata parimāṇam eva ca eṣām aṅguṣṭha mātram hṛdayam atas  manuṣya adhikāra tvāt śāstrasya manuṣya hṛdaya avasthāna apekṣam aṅguṣṭha mātra tvam upapannam paramātmanaḥ yad api uktam parimāṇa upadeśāt smṛteḥ ca saṃsārya iva ayam aṅguṣṭa mātraḥ pratyetavya iti tad pratyucyate ityādivat saṃsāriṇa eva sataḥ  aṅguṣṭha mātrasya brahma tvam idam upadiśyata iti dvi rūpā hi vedānta vākyānām pravṛttiḥ kvacid paramātma svarūpa nirūpaṇa parā kvacid vijñāna ātmanaḥ paramātmā eka tva upadeśa parā tad atra vijñāna ātmanaḥ paramātmanā eka tvam upadiśyate na aṅguṣṭha mātra tvam kasyacid  etam eva artham pareṇa sphuṭīkariṣyati ntarātmā sadā janānām hṛdaye saṃniviṣṭaḥ tam svāt śarīrāt pravṛhet muñjā di veṣikām dhairyeṇa tam vidyāt śukram amṛtam iti aṅguṣṭha mātra śrutiḥ manuṣya hṛdaya apekṣayā manuṣya adhikāra tvāt śāstrasya iti uktam tad prasaṅgena idam ucyate bāḍham manuṣya adhikāra iti śāstram na tu manuṣyān eva iti iha brahma jñāne niyamaḥ  asti teṣām manuṣyāṇām upariṣṭa ādye deva ādayaḥ tān api adhikaroti śāstram iti bādarāyaṇa ācāryaḥ  manyante kasmāt  saṃbhavāt  saṃbhavati hi teṣām api arthi tva ādi adhikāra kāraṇam tatra arthi tvam tāvat mokṣa viṣayam deva ādīnām api saṃbhavati vikāra viṣaya vibhūti anitya tva ālocana ādi nimittam tathā sāmarthyam api teṣām saṃbhavati mantra artha vāda itihāsa purāṇa lokebhyaḥ  vigrahavat tva ādi avagamāt na ca teṣām kaścid pratiṣedhaḥ  asti naca upanayana śāstreṇa eṣām adhikāraḥ  nivartyeta upanayanasya veda adhyayana artha tvāt teṣām ca svayaṃpratibhāta veda tvāt  api cā eṣām vidyā grahaṇa artham brahmacarya ādi darśayati abhṛguḥ vai vāruṇiḥ varuṇam pitaram upasasāra adhīhi bhagavaḥ  brahma ityādi yad api karmasu anadhikāra kāraṇam uktam iti ana ṛṣīṇām ārṣeya antara abhāvāt iti na tad vidyāsu asti na hi indra ādīnām vidyā svadha kriyamāṇānām indra ādi uddeśena kiñcid kṛtyam asti na ca bhṛgu ādīnām bhṛgu ādi sagotra tayā tasmāt deva ādīnām api vidyāsu adhikāraḥ kena vāryate deva ādi adhikāre api aṅguṣṭa mātra śrutiḥ sva aṅguṣṭha apekṣayā na virudhyate syāt etad  yadi vigrahavat tva ādi abhyupagamena deva ādīnām vidyāsu adhikāraḥ  varṇyeta vigrahavat tvāt ṛtvigādindrā ādīnām api sva rūpa saṃnidhānena karma aṅga bhāvaḥ  abhyupagamyeta tadā ca virodhaḥ karmaṇi syāt  na hi indra ādīnām sva rūpa saṃnidhānena yāge aṅga bhāvaḥ  dṛśyate na ca saṃbhavati bahuṣu yāgeṣu yugapad ekasya indrasya svarūpa saṃnidhāna tā anupapatteḥ iti ced  na ayam asti virodhaḥ kasmāt  aneka pratipatteḥ ekasya api devatā ātmanaḥ  yugapad aneka svarūpa pratipattiḥ saṃbhavati katham etad avagamyate darśanāt  tathā hi iti upakramya atrayaḥ ca trī ca śatā trayaḥ ca trī ca sahasrā iti nirucya akatama te iti asyām pṛcchāyām amahimāna eva eṣām ete trayastriṃśat tvā iva devāḥ iti nirbruvatī śrutiḥ ekaikasya devatā ātmanaḥ  yugapad aneka rūpa tām darśayati tathā trayastriṃśataḥ  api ṣaṭ ādi antarbhāva krameṇa akatama ekaḥ  deva iti prāṇaḥ iti prāṇa eka rūpa tām devānām darśayantī tasya ekasya prāṇasya yugapad aneka rūpa tām darśayati tathā smṛtiḥ api iti evan jātīyakā prāpta aṇim ādi aiśvaryāṇām yoginām api yugapad aneka śarīra yogam darśayati kim u vaktavyam ājāna siddhānām devānām aneka rūpa pratipatti saṃbhavāt ca ekaikā devatā bahubhī rūpaiḥ ātmānam pravibhajya bahuṣu yāgeṣu yugapad aṅga bhāvam gacchati iti paraiḥ ca na dṛśyate antardhāna ādi kriyā yogāt iti upapadyate aneka pratipatteḥ darśana ādityasya aparā vyākhyā vigrahavatām api karma aṅga bhāva codanāsu anekā pratipattiḥ dṛśyate kvacid eko api vigrahavān anekatra yugapad aṅga bhāvam na gacchati yathā bahubhiḥ bhojayadbhiḥ na ekaḥ  brāhmaṇaḥ  yugapad bhojyate kvacid ca eko api vigrahavān anekatra yugapad aṅga bhāvam gacchati yathā bahubhiḥ namaskurvāṇaiḥ ekaḥ  brāhmaṇaḥ  yugapad nam askriyate tadvat iha uddeśa parityāga ātmaka tvāt yāgasya vigrahavatīm api ekām devatām uddiśya bahavaḥ svam svam dravyam yugapad parityakṣyanti iti vigrahavat tve api devatānām na kiñcid karmaṇi virudhyate mā nāma vigrahavat tve deva ādīnām abhyupagamyamāne karmaṇi kaścid virodhaḥ prasañji śabde tu virodhaḥ prasajyeta katham autpattikam hi śabdasya arthena saṃbandham āśritya aanapekṣa tvāt iti vedasya prāmāṇyam sthāpitam idānīm tu vigrahavatī devatā abhyupagamyamānā yadi api aiśvarya yogāt yugapad aneka karma saṃbandhīni havīṃṣi bhuñjīta tathā api vigraha yogāt asmad ādivat janana maraṇavatī sā iti nityasya śabdasya nityena arthena nitye saṃbandhepratīyamāne yad vaidike śabde prāmāṇyam sthitam tasya virodhaḥ syāt iti ced  na ayam api asti virodhaḥ kasmāt  atas  prabhavāt  ata eva hi vaidikāt śabdā deva ādikam jagat prabhavati nanu janma ādyasya yatas  iti atra brahma prabhava tvam jagataḥ  avadhāritam katham iha śabda prabhava tvam ucyate apica yadi nāma vaidikāt śabda āt asya prabhavaḥ  abhyupagataḥ katham etāvatā virodhaḥ śabde parihṛtaḥ yāvatā vasavaḥ  rudrā ādityā viśvedevā maruta iti eter atha anityā eva utpattimat tvāt tad anitya tve ca tad vācinām vaidikānām vasu ādi śabdānām anitya tvam kena nivāryate prasiddham hi loke devadattasya putra utpanne yajñadatta iti tasya nāma kriyata iti tasmāt virodha eva śabda iti ced  na gavā ādi śabda artha saṃbandha nitya tva darśanāt na hi gavā ādi vyaktīnām utpattimat tve tad ākṛtīnīm api utpattimat tvam syāt  dravya guṇa karmaṇām hi vyaktaya eva utpadyante na ākṛtayaḥ ākṛtibhiḥ ca śabdānām saṃbandhaḥ  na vyaktibhiḥ vyaktīnām ānantyāt saṃbandha grahaṇa anupapatteḥ vyaktiṣu utpadyamānāsu api ākṛtīnām nitya tvāt ca gavā ādi śabdeṣu kaścid virodhaḥ  dṛśyate tathā deva ādi vyakti prabhava abhyupagame api ākṛti nitya tvāt na kaścid vasu ādi śabdeṣu virodha iti draṣṭavyam ākṛti viśeṣaḥ tu deva ādīnām mantra artha vāda ādibhyaḥ  vigrahavat tva ādi avagamāt avagantavyaḥ sthāna viśeṣa saṃbandha nimittāḥ ca indra ādi śabdāḥ senāpatya ādi śabdavat tatas ca yaḥ  yaḥ tad tad sthānam adhirohati sa sa indra ādi śabdaiḥ abhidhīyata iti na doṣaḥ  bhavati nacedam śabda prabhava tvam brahma prabhava tvavat upādāna kāraṇa abhiprāyeṇa ucyate katham tarhi sthite vācaka ātmanā nitye śabde nitya artha saṃbandhini śabda vyavahāra yogya artha vyakti niṣpattiḥ atas  prabhava iti ucyate katham punar avagamyate śabdāt prabhavati jagat iti pratyakṣa anumānābhyām pratyakṣam śrutiḥ prāmāṇyam pratyanapekṣa tvāt  anumānam smṛtiḥ prāmāṇyam prati sa apekṣa tvāt  te hi śabda pūrvaḥ  sṛṣṭim darśayataḥ aete iti vai prajāpatiḥ devān asṛjatā asṛgram iti manuṣyān indava iti pitṛn  tiraḥ pavitram iti grahānāśava iti stotram viśvāni iti śastram abhisaubhaga iti anyāḥ prajāḥ iti śrutiḥ tathā anyatra api asa manasā vācam mithunam samabhavat ityādinā tatra tatra śabda pūrvikā sṛṣṭiḥ śrāvyate smṛtiḥ api iti utsargaḥ  api ayam vācaḥ saṃpradāya pravartana ātmakaḥ  draṣṭavyaḥ anādi nidhanāyā anyādṛśasya utsargasya asaṃbhavāt tathā anāma rūpam ca bhūtānām karmaṇām ca pravartanam veda śabdebhyaḥ  eva ādau nirmame sa maheśvaraḥ iti sarveṣām tu sa nāmāni karmāṇi ca pṛthak pṛthak  veda śabdebhyaḥ  eva ādau pṛthak saṃsthāḥ ca nirmame iti ca apica cikīrṣitam artham anutiṣṭhan  tasya vācakam śabdam pūrvam smṛtvā paścāt tam artham anuṣṭhati iti sarveṣām naḥ pratyakṣam etad  tathā prajāpateḥ api sraṣṭuḥ sṛṣṭeḥ pūrvam vaidikāḥ śabdā manasi prādurbabhūvuḥ paścāt tad anugatānarthān sasarja iti gamyate tathā ca śrutiḥ iti evamādikā bhūḥ ādi śabdebhya eva manasi prādurbhūtebhyaḥ  bhūḥ ādi lokān sṛṣṭān darśayati kimātmakam punar  śabdam abhipretya idam śabda prabhava tvam ucyate sphoṭam iti āha varṇa pakṣe hi teṣām utpanna pradhvaṃsi tvāt nityebhyaḥ śabdebhyaḥ  deva ādi vyaktīnām prabhava iti anupapannam syāt  utpanna dhvaṃsinaḥ ca varṇāḥ pratyuccāraṇam anyathā ca anyathā ca pratīyamāna tvāt  tathā hi adṛśyamānaḥ  api puruṣa viśeṣaḥ  adhyayana dhvani śravaṇāt eva viśeṣataḥ  nirdhāryate devadattaḥ  ayam adhīte yajñadattaḥ  ayam adhīte iti nacāyam varṇa viṣayaḥ  anyathātva pratyayo mithyājñānam bādhaka pratyaya abhāvāt na ca varṇebhyor atha avagatiḥ yuktā na hi ekaikaḥ  varṇor atham pratyāyayet  vyabhicārāt  na ca varṇa samudāya pratyayo asti kramavat tvāt varṇānām pūrva pūrva varṇa anubhava janita saṃskāra sahitaḥ  antyaḥ  varṇor atham pratyāyayiṣyati iti yadi ucyeta tad na saṃbandha grahaṇa apekṣaḥ  hi śabdaḥ svayam pratīyamānoḥ atham pratyāyayet dhūma ādivat  na ca pūrva pūrva varṇa anubhava janita saṃskāra sahitasya antya varṇasya pratītiḥ asti apratyakṣa tvāt saṃskārāṇām kārya pratyāyitaiḥ saṃskāraiḥ sahitaḥ  antyaḥ  varṇa ūrtham pratyāyayiṣyati iti ced  na saṃskāra kāryasya api smaraṇasya krama varti tvāt tasmāt sphoṭa eva śabdaḥ sa ca eca eka varṇa pratyaya āhita saṃskāra bīje antya varṇa pratyaya janita pari pāke pratyayinī eka pratyaya viṣaya tayā jhaṭiti pratyavabhāsate nacāyam eka pratyayo varṇa viṣayā smṛtiḥ varṇānām aneka tvāt eka pratyaya viṣaya tva anupapatteḥ tasya ca pratyuccāraṇam pratyabhijñāyamāna tvāt nitya tvam bheda pratyayasya varṇa viṣaya tvāt tasmāt nityāt śabda sphoṭa rūpāt abhidhāyakāt kriyā kāraka phala lakṣaṇam jagat abhidheya bhūtam prabhavati iti varṇā eva tu na śabdaḥ iti bhagavān upavarṣaḥ nanu utpanna pradhvaṃsi tvam varṇāt muktam tad na ta eva iti pratyabhijñānāt  sādṛśyāt pratbhijñānam keśa ādiṣu iva iti ced  na pratyabhijñānasya pramāṇa antareṇa bādha anupapatteḥ pratyabhijñānam ākṛti nimittam iti ced  na vyakti pratyabhijñānāt  yadi hi pratyuccāraṇam gavā ādi vyaktivat anyā anyā varṇa vyaktayaḥ pratīyeran  tata ākṛti nimittam pratyabhijñānam syāt  na tu etad asti varṇa vyaktaya eva hi pratyuccāraṇam pratyabhijñāyante dvirgo śabda uccārita iti hi pratipattiḥ na tu dvau go śabdau  iti nanu varṇā api uccāraṇa bhedena bhinnaḥ pratīyante deva datta yajñadattayoḥ adhyayana dhvani śravaṇāt eva bheda pratīteḥ iti uktam atra abhidhīyate sati varṇa viṣaye niścite pratyabhijñāne saṃyoga vibhāga abhivyaṅgya tvāt varṇānām abhivyañjaka vaicitrya nimittaḥ  ayam varṇa viṣayaḥ  vicitraḥ pratyayo na svarūpa nimittaḥ apica varṇa vyakti bheda vādinā api pratyabhijñāna siddhaye varṇa ākṛtayaḥ kalpayitavyāḥ tāsu ca para upādhikaḥ  bheda pratyaya iti abhyupagantavyam tad varam varṇa vyaktiṣu eva para upādhikaḥ  bheda pratyayaḥ svarūpa nimittam ca pratyabhijñānam iti kalpanā lāghavam eṣa eva ca varṇa viṣayasya bheda pratyayasya bādhakaḥ pratyayo yad pratyabhijñānam katham hi ekasmin kālam bahūnām uccārayatām eka eva sanga kāraḥ  yugapad aneka rūpaḥ syāt  udāttaḥ ca anudāttaḥ ca svaritaḥ ca sa anunāsikaḥ ca niranunāsikaḥ ca iti athavā dhvani kṛtaḥ  ayam pratyaya bhedaḥ  na varṇa kṛta iti adoṣaḥ kaḥ punar ayam dhvaniḥ nāma yaḥ  dūrāt ākarṇayataḥ  varṇa vivekam apratipadyamānasya karṇa patham avatarati pratyāsīdataḥ ca paṭum aṭu tva ādi bhedam varṇeṣu āsañjayati tad nibandhanāḥ ca udāttādayaḥ  viśeṣā na varṇa svarūpa nibandhanāḥ varṇānām pratyuccārāṇam pratyabhijñāyamāna tvāt  evañca sati sa ālambanā udātta ādi pratyayā bhaviṣyanti itaradhā hi varṇānām pratyabhijñāyamānānām nirbheda tvāt saṃyoga vibhāga kṛtā udātta ādi viśeṣāḥ kalperan saṃyoga vibhāgānām ca apratyakṣa tvāt ca tad āśrayā viśeṣā varṇeṣu adhyavasitum śakyanta iti atas  nirālambanā eva eta udātta ādi pratyayāḥ syuḥ apica na eva etad abhiniveṣṭavyam udātta ādi bhedena varṇānām pratyabhijñāyamānānām bhedaḥ  bhavet iti na hi anyasya bhedena anyasya abhidyamānasya bhedaḥ  bhavitum arhati na hi vyakti bhedena jātim bhinnām manyante varṇebhyaḥ ca artha pratīteḥ saṃbhavāt sphoṭa kalpanānarthikā na kalpayāmi aham sphoṭam pratyakṣam eva tu enam avagacchāmi ekaika varṇa grahaṇa āhita saṃskārāyām buddhau jhaṭiti pratyava ūbhāsanāt iti ced  na asyāḥ  api buddheḥ varṇa viṣaya tvāt ekaika varṇa grahaṇa uttara kālā hi iyam ekā buddhiḥ gauḥ iti samasta varṇa viṣayā na artha antara viṣayā katham etad avagamyate yatas  asyām api buddhau gakāra ādayaḥ  varṇā anuvartante na tu dakāra ādayaḥ yadi hi asyāḥ  buddheḥ gakāra ādibhyor atha antaram sphoṭaḥ  viṣayaḥ syāt tatas  dakāra ādaya iva gakāra ādayaḥ  api asyā buddheḥ vyāvarteran na tu tathā asti tasmāt iyam ekabuddhiḥ varṇa viṣayā eva smṛtiḥ nanu aneka tvāt varṇānām na eka buddhi viṣayatā upapadyata iti uktam tad pratibrūmaḥ saṃbhavati anekasya api ekabuddhi viṣaya tvam paṅ ktiḥ vanam senā daśa śatam sahasram iti ādi darśanāt  yā tu gauḥ iti ekaḥ  ayam śabda iti buddhiḥ sā bahuṣu eva varṇeṣu eka artha avaccheda nibandhana aupacārikī vanasena ādi buddhivat eva atra āha yadi varṇā eva sāmastyena eka buddhi viṣaya tām āpadyamānāḥ padam syuḥ tatas  jārā rājā kapiḥ pikaḥ ityādiṣu pada viśeṣa pratipattiḥ na syāt  ta eva hi varṇā itaratra ca itaratra ca pratyavabhāsanta iti atra vadāmaḥ sati api samasta varṇa pratyavamarśe yathā krama anurodhinya eva pipīlikāḥ paṅ ktibuddhim ārohanti evam krama anurodhana eva varṇāḥ pada buddhim ārokṣyanti tatra varṇānām aviśeṣe api krama viśeṣa kṛtā pada viśeṣa pratipattiḥ na virudhyate vṛddha vyavahāre ca ime varṇāḥ krama ādi anugṛhītā gṛhīta artha viśeṣa saṃbandhāḥ santaḥ sva vyavahāraḥ  api ekaika varṇa grahaṇa anantaram samasta pratyavamarśinyām buddhau tādṛśā eva pratyavabhāsamānāḥ tam tam artham avyabhicāreṇa pratyāyayiṣyanti iti varṇa vādinaḥ  laghīyasī kalpanā sphoṭa vādinaḥ tu dṛṣṭa hāniḥ adṛṣṭa kalpanā ca varṇāḥ ca ime krameṇa gṛhyamāṇāḥ sphoṭam vyañjayanti sa sphoṭor atham vyanakti iti garīyasī kalpanā syāt  atha api nāma pratyuccāraṇam anye anye varṇāḥ syuḥ tathā api pratyabhijñā ālambana bhāvena varṇa sāmānyānām avaśya abhyupagantavya tva ādyā varṇeṣu artha pratipādana prakriyā racitā sā sāmānyeṣu saṃcārayitavyā tatas ca nityebhyaḥ śabdebhyaḥ  deva ādi vyaktīnām prabhava iti aviruddham svatantrasya kartuḥ asmaraṇa ādibhiḥ sthite vedasya nitya tve deva ādi vyakti prabhava abhyupagamena tasya virodham āśaṅkya aatas  prabhavāt iti parihṛtya idānīm tad eva veda nitya tvam sthitam draḍhayati ata eva ca nitya tvam iti ata eva niyata ākṛteḥ deva ādeḥ jagataḥ  veda śabda prabhava tvāt veda śabde nitya tvam api pratyetavyam tathā ca mantra varṇaḥ yuga ante antarhitān vedān sa itihāsān mahā ṛṣayaḥ lebhire tapasā pūrvam anujñātāḥ svayaṃbhuvā iti atha api syāt  yadi paśu ādi vyaktivat deva ādi vyaktayo api saṃtatyā eva utpadyeran nirudhya īran  ca tatas  abhidhāna abhidheya abhidhātṛ vyavahāra avi  chedāt saṃbandha nitya tvena virodhaḥ śabde parihriyeta yadā tu khalu sakalam trailokyam parityakta nāma rūpam nirlepam pralīyate prabhavati ca abhinavam iti śruti smṛti vādā vadanti tadā katham avirodha iti tatra idam abhidhīyate samāna nāma rūpa tvāt iti tadā api saṃsārasya anādi tvam tāvat abhyupagantavyam pratipādayiṣyati ca ācāryaḥ saṃsārasya anādi tvam ca iti anādau ca saṃsāre yathā svāpa prabodhayoḥ pralaya prabhava śravaṇe api pūrva prabodhavat ukta prabodhe api vyavahārān na kaścid virodhaḥ evam kalpa antara prabhava pralayayoḥ iti draṣṭavyam svāpa prabodhayoḥ ca pralaya prabhavau śrūyete pi manuṣya ādi stamba paryanteṣu jñāna aiśvarya ādi pratibandhaḥ pareṇa pareṇa bhūyān bhavan dṛśyate tathā manuṣya ādi stamba paryanteṣu hiraṇyagarbha paryanteṣu jñāna aiśvarya ādi abhivyaktiḥ api pareṇa pareṇa bhūyasī bhavati iti etad śruti smṛti vādeṣu asakṛt anuśrūyamāṇam na śakyam vaditum tatas ca atīta kalpa anuṣṭhita prakṛṣṭa jñāna karmaṇām īśvarāṇām hiraṇyagarbha ādīnām vartamāna kalpa ādau prādurbhavatām parameśra anugṛhītānām supta pratibuddha tva kalpa antara vyavahāra anusaṃdhāna upapattiḥ tathā ca śrutiḥ iti smaranti ca śaunaka ādayaḥ amadhu  chandaḥ prabhṛtibhiḥ ṛṣibhiḥ darśitayyaḥ  dṛṣṭāḥ iti prativedam ca evam eva kāṇḍarṣyādayaḥ smaryante śrutiḥ api ṛṣi jñāna pūrvakam eva mantreṇa anuṣṭhānam darśayati iti upakramya tasmāt etāni mantre mantre vidyāt iti prāṇinām ca sukha prāptaye dharmaḥ  vidhīyate duḥkha parihārāya ca adharmaḥ pratiṣidhyate dṛṣṭa ānuśravika sukha duḥkha viṣayau ca rāga dveṣau bhavataḥ  na vilakṣaṇa viṣayau  iti ato dharma adharma phala bhūta uttarā sṛṣṭiḥ niṣpadyamānā pūrva sṛṣṭi sadṛśi ā iva niṣpadyate smṛtiḥ ca bhavati iti pralīyamānam api ca idam jagat śakti aśeṣam eva pralīyate śakti mūlam eva ca prabhavati itarathā kasmika tva prasaṃṅāt  naca aneka ākārāḥ śaktayaḥ śakyāḥ kalpayitum tatas ca vicchidya vicchidyā api udbhavatām bhūḥ ādi loka pravāhāṇām deva tiryak manuṣya lakṣaṇānām ca prāṇi nikāya pravāhāṇām varṇa āśrama dharma phala vyavasthānām ca anādau saṃsāre niyata tvam indriya viṣaya saṃbandha niyata tvavat pratyetavyam nahi indriya viṣaya saṃbandha ādeḥ vyavahārasya pratisargam anyathātvam ṣaṣṭha indriya viṣaya kalpam śakyam utprekṣitum atas ca sarva kalpānām tulya vyavahāra tvāt kalpa anta vyavahāra anusaṃdhāna kṣama tvāt ca īśvarāṇām samāna nāma rūpā eva pratisargam viśeṣāḥ prādurbhavanti samāna nāma rūpa tvāt ca avṛttau  api mahā sarga mahāpralaya kṣaṇāyām jagataḥ  abhyupagamyamānāyām na kaścid śabda prāmāṇya ādi virodhaḥ samāna nāma rūpa tām ca śruti smṛtī darśayataḥ iti yathā pūrvasmin kalpe sūryācandramaḥ prabhṛti jagat kḷptam tathā asmin  api kalpe parameśvaraḥ  akalpayat iti arthaḥ tathā aagniḥ vā akāmayata anna ādaḥ  devān āṃsyām iti sa etam agnaye kṛttikābhyaḥ puroḍāśam aṣṭākapālam niravapat iti nakṣatra iṣṭi vidhau yaḥ  agniḥ niravapadi asmai vā agnaye niravapattayoḥ samāna nāma rūpa tām darśayati iti evan jātīyakā śrutiḥ iha udāhartavyā smṛtiḥ api tītāḥ tulyaḥ te sāṃprataiḥ iha devāḥ  devaiḥ atātaiḥ hi rūpaiḥ nāmabhiḥ eva ca iti eva jātīyakā draṣṭavyā iha deva ādīnām api brahma vidyāyām asti adhikāra iti yad pratijñātam tad paryāvartyate deva ādīnām anadhikāram jaiminiḥ ācāryaḥ  manyante kasmāt  madhu ādiṣu asaṃbhavāt  brahma vidyāyām adhikāra abhyupagame hi vidyā tvā aviśeṣāt madhu ādi vidyāsu api adhikāraḥ  abhyupagamyeta na ca evam saṃbhavati katham aasau vā ādityaḥ  deva madhu iti atra manuṣyā ādityam madhu adhyāsena upasīran deva ādiṣu hi upāsakeṣi abhyupagamyamāneṣu ādityaḥ kam anyam ādityam upāsīta punar ca āditya vyapāśrayāṇi pañca rohita ādīni amṛtāni upakramya vasavaḥ  rudrā ādityā marutaḥ sādhyāḥ ca pañca deva gaṇāḥ krameṇa tad tatam ṛtam upajīvanti iti upadiśya asa ya etad evam amṛtam veda vasūnām eva eko bhūtvā agninā eva mukhena etad eva amṛtam dṛṣṭvā tṛpyati ityādinā vasu ādi upajīvyāni amṛtāni vijānatām vasu ādi mahima prāptim darśayati vasu ādayaḥ tu kānanyān vasu ādīn amṛta upajīvinaḥ  vijānīyuḥ kam vā anyam vasu ādi mahimānam prepseyuḥ atathā agniḥ pādaḥ  vāyuḥ pāda ādityaḥ pādaḥ  diśaḥ pādaḥ avāyuḥ vāva saṃvargaḥ aa aādityaḥ  brahma iti ādeśaḥ ityādiṣu devatā ātma upāsaneṣu na teṣām eva devatā ātmānam adhikāraḥ saṃbhavati tathā aimau  eva gotama bharadvājā vayam eva gotamaḥ  ayam bharadvājaḥ ityādiḥ vipi ṛṣi saṃbandheṣu upāsaneṣu na teṣām eva ṛṣīṇām adhikāraḥ saṃbhavati kutas ca deva ādīnām adhikāraḥ yad idam jyotiḥ maṇḍalam dyusthānam ahorātrābhyām bambhra majja gat avabhāsayati tasmin  ādityādayaḥ  devatā vacanāḥ śabdāḥ prayujyante loka prasiddharvākī aśeṣa prasiddheḥ ca na ca jyotiḥ maṇḍalasya hṛdaya ādinā vigraheṣu cetanayā arthi tva ādinā vā yogaḥ  avagantum śakyate mṛta ādivat acetanatva avagamāt etena agni ādayaḥ  vyākhyātāḥ syāt etad  mantra artha vāda itihāsa purāṇa lokebhyaḥ  deva ādānām vigrahavat tva ādi avagamāt ayam adoṣa iti na iti ucyate na hi tāvat lokaḥ  nāma kiñcid svatantram pramāṇam asti pratyakṣa ādibhya eva hi avicārita viśeṣebhyaḥ pramāṇebhyaḥ prasiddhi anarthaḥ  lokāt prasidhyati iti ucyate na ca atra pratyakṣa ādīnām anyatamam pramāṇam asti itihāsa purāṇam api pauruṣeya tvāt pramāṇa antara mūlam ākāṅkṣati artha vādā api vidhinā eka vākya tvāt stuti arthāḥ santaḥ  na pārtha garthyena deva ādīnām vigraha ādi sadbhāve kāraṇa bhāvam pratipadyante mantrā api śruti ādi viniyuktāḥ prayoga samavāyinaḥ  abhidhāna arthā na kasyacid arthasya pramāṇam iti ācakṣate tasmāt abhāvaḥ  deva ādīnām adhikārasya tuśabdaḥ pūrva pakṣam vyavartayati bādarāyaṇaḥ tu ācāryaḥ  bhāvam adhikārasya deva ādīnām api manyante yadi api madhu ādi vidyāsu devatā ādi vyāmiśrāsu āsaṃbhavaḥ  adhikārasya tathā api asti hi śuddhāyām brahma vidyāyām saṃbhavaḥ arthi tva sāmarthya pratiṣedha ādi apekṣa tvāt adhikārasya na ca kvacid asaṃbhava iti etāvatā yatra saṃbhavaḥ tatra api adhikāraḥ  apodyeta manuṣyāṇām api na sarveṣām brāhmaṇa ādīnām sarveṣu rājasūya ādiṣu adhikāraḥ saṃbhavati tatra yaḥ  nyāyaḥ saḥ  atra api bhaviṣyati brahma vidyām ca prakṛtya bhavati darśanam śrautam deva ādi adhikārasya sūcakam iti ate ha ūcuḥ hanta tam ātmānam anvicchāmaḥ  yam ātmānam anviṣya sarvān  ca lokān āpnoti sarvān  ca kāmān iti aindraḥ  ha vai devānām abhipravrāja virocana asurāṇām ityādi ca samārtam api gandharva yājñavalkya saṃvāda ādi yad api uktam jyotiṣi bhāvāt ca iti atra brūmaḥ jyotiḥ ādi viṣayā api ādityādayaḥ  devatā vacanāḥ śabdāḥ cetanāvantam aiśvarya ādi upetam tam tam devatā ātmānam samarpayanti mantra artha vāda ādiṣu tathā vyavahārāt  asti hi aiśvarya yogāt devatānām jyotiḥ ādya ātmabhiḥ ca avasthātum yatheṣṭam ca tam tam vigraham grahītum sāmarthyam tathā hi śrūyate subrahmaṇya artha vāde medhātitheḥ meṣa iti amedha atithim ha kāṇvāyanam indraḥ  meṣaḥ  bhūtvā jahāra iti smaryate ca iti mṛd ādiṣu api cetanā adhiṣṭhitāraḥ  abhyupagamyante mṛd abravīt āpobruvan  iti ādi darśanāt  jyotiḥ ādeḥ tu bhūtadhātoḥ āt itya ādiṣu acetana tvam abhyupagamyate cetanāḥ tu adhiṣṭhitāraḥ  devatā ātmanaḥ  mantra artha vāda ādi vyavahārāt iti uktam yad api uktam mantra artha vādayoḥ anyāya artha tvāt na devatā vigraha ādi prakāśana sāmarthyam iti atra brūmaḥ pratyaya apratyayau hi sadbhāva asadbhāvayoḥ kāraṇam na anyartha tvam ananyā artha tvam vā tathā hi anya artham api prasthitaḥ pathi patitam tṛṇa parṇa ādi asti iti eva pratipadyate atra āha viṣama upanyāsaḥ tatra hi tṛṇa parṇa ādi viṣayam pratyakṣam pravṛttam asti yena tad astitvam pratipadyate atra punar vidhi uddeśa eka vākya bhāvena stuti arther athavādena pārtha garthyena vṛttānta viṣayā pravṛttiḥ śakyā adhyavasātum na hi ana surām pibet iti nañvati vākye pada traya saṃbandhāt surā pāna pratiṣedha eva ekor atho avagamyate na punar  surām pibet iti pada dvaya saṃbandhāt surā pāna vidhiḥ api iti atra ucyate viṣama upanyāsaḥ yuktam yad surā pāna pratiṣedhe pada anvayasya eka tvāt avāntara vākya arthasya agrahaṇam vidhi uddeśa artha vādayoḥ tu arthavāda sthāni padāni pṛthak anvaya vṛttānta viṣayam pratipadya anantaram kaimarthya vaśena kāmam vidheḥ stāvaka tvam pratipadyante yathā hi iti atra vidhi uddeśa vartinām vāyavī ādi padānām vidhinā saṃbandhaḥ na evam avāyuḥ vai kṣepiṣṭhā devatā vāyum eva svena bhāgadheyena upadhāvati sa eva enam bhūtim gamayati iti eṣām artha vāda gatānām padānām na hi bhavati vāyuḥ vā ālabheta iti kṣepiṣṭhā devatā vā ālabheta ityādi vāyu svabhāva saṃkīrtanena tu avāntaram anvayam pratipadya evam viśiṣṭa daivatyam idam karma iti vidhim stuvanti tad yatra saḥ  avāntara vākya arthaḥ pramāṇa antara gocaraḥ  bhavati tatra tad anuvādenartha vādaḥ pravartate yatra pramāṇa antara viruddhaḥ tatra guṇa vādena yatra tu tad ubhayam na asti tatra kim pramāṇa antara abhāvāt guṇa vādaḥ syāt āhosvid pramāṇa antara avirodhāt vidyamāna vāda iti pratīti śaraṇaiḥ vidyamāna vāda āśrayaṇīyaḥ  na guṇa vādaḥ etena mantraḥ  vyākhyātaḥ apica vidhibhiḥ eva indra ādi daivatyāni havīṃṣi codayadbhiḥ apekṣitam indra ādīnām svarūpam na hi sva rūpa rahitā indra ādayaḥ cetasi āropayitum śakyante na ca cetasi anārūḍhāyai tasyai tasyai devatāyai haviḥ pradātum śakyate śrāvayati ca iti na ca śabda mātram artha svarūpam saṃbhavati śabda arthayoḥ bhedāt  tatra yādṛśam mantra artha vādayoḥ indra ādīnām sva rūpam avagatam na tad tādṛśam śabda pramāṇakena pratyākhyatum yuktam itihāsa purāṇam api vyākhyātena mārgeṇa saṃbhavat mantra artha vāda mūla tvāt prabhavati devatā vigraha ādi sādhayitim pratyakṣa ādi mūlam api saṃbhavati bhavati hi asmākam apratyakṣam api cirantanānām pratyakṣam tathā ca vyāsādayaḥ  deva ādibhiḥ pratyakṣam vyavaharanti iti smaryate yaḥ tu brūyāt idānī ntanānām iva pūrveṣām api na asti deva ādibhiḥ vyavahartum sāmarthyam iti sa jagat vaicitryam pratiṣedhet  idānīm iva ca na anyat api sārvabhaumaḥ kṣatriyaḥ  asti iti brūyāt  tatas ca rājasūya ādi codana uparundhyāt idānīm iva ca kāla antare api avyavasthita prāyān varṇa āśrama dharmān pratijānīta tatas ca vyavasthā vidhāyi śāstram anarthakam syāt  tasmāt dharma utkarṣa vaśāt cirantanā deva ādibhiḥ pratyakṣam vyavajahnuḥ iti śliṣyate apica smaranti ityādi yogaḥ  api aṇima ādyaiśvarī arprāpti phalaḥ smaryamāṇaḥ  na śakyate sāhasa mātreṇa pratyākhyātum śrutiḥ ca yoga māhātmyam prakhyāpayati nilakhe samutthite pañca ātmake yoga guṇe pravṛtte na tasya rogaḥ  na jarā na mṛtyuḥ prāptasya yoga agni mayam śarīram aa iti ṛṣīṇām api mantra brāhmaṇa darśinām sāmarthyam na asmadīyena sāmarthyena upamātum yuktam tasmāt sa mūlam itihāsa purāṇam loka prasiddhiḥ api na sati saṃbhave nirālamba nādhyavasātum yuktā tasmāt upapannaḥ  mantra ādibhyaḥ  deva ādīnām vigrahavat tva ādi avagamaḥ tatas ca arthi tva ādi saṃbhavāt upapannaḥ  deva ādīnām api brahma vidyāyām adhikāraḥ krama mukti darśanāni api evam eva upapadyante yathā manuṣya adhikāra niyamam apodya deva ādīnām api vidyāsu adhikāra uktaḥ tathā eva dvijāti adhikāra niyama apavādena śūdrasya api adhikāraḥ syāt iti etām āśaṅkām nivartayitum idam adhikaraṇam ārabhyate tatra śūdrasya api adhikāraḥ syāt asti tāvat prāptam arthi tva sāmarthyayoḥ saṃbhavāt  atasmāt śūdraḥ yajñe anavakḷptaḥ itivat  aśūdraḥ  vidyāyām anavakḷptaḥ iti ca niṣedha aśravaṇāt yad ca karmasu anadhikāra kāraṇam śūdrasya anagni tvam na tad vidyāsu avikārasya apavādakam liṅgam na hi āhavanīya ādi rahitena vidyā veditum na śakyate bhavati ca liṅgam śūdra adhikārasya upoddhalakam saṃvarga vidyāyām hi jānaśrutim pautrāyaṇam śuśrūṣum śūdra śabdena parāmṛśati iti vidura prabhṛtayaḥ ca śūdra yoni prabhavā api viśiṣṭa vijñāna saṃpannāḥ smaryante tasmāt adhikriyate śūdraḥ  vidyāsu iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ na śūdrasya adhikāraḥ veda adhyayana abhāvāt adhīta vedaḥ  hi vidita veda arthaḥ  veda artheṣu adhikriyate na ca śūdrasya veda adhyayanam asti upanayana pūrvaka tvāt veda adhyayanasya upanayanasya ca varṇa traya viṣaya tvāt yad tu arthi tvam na tad asati sāmarthye adhikāra kāraṇam bhavati sāmarthyam api na lokikam kevalam adhikāra kāraṇam bhavati śāstrīyer athe śāstrīyasya sāmarthyasya apekṣita tvāt śāstrīyasya ca sāmarthyasya adhyayana nirākaraṇena nirākṛta tvāt  yad ca idam aśūdraḥ  yajñe anavakḷptaḥ iti tad nyāya pūrvaka tvāt vidyāyām api anavakḷpta tvam dyotayati nyāyasya sādhāraṇa tvāt  yad punar  saṃvarga vidyāyām śūdra śabda śravaṇam liṅgam manyase na tad liṅgam nyāya abhāvāt  nyāya ukte hi liṅga darśanam dyotakam bhavati na ca atra nyāyaḥ  asti kāmam ca ayam śūdra śabdaḥ saṃvarga vidyāyām eva ekasyām śūdram adhikuryāt  tad viṣaya tvāt na sarvāsu vidyāsu arthavāda sthāt tu na kvacid api ayam śūdram adhikaṛtum utsahate śakyate ca ayam śūdra śabdaḥ  adhikṛta vaṣayaḥ  yojayitum katham iti ucyate iti asmāt haṃsa vākyāt ātmanaḥ  anādaram śrutavataḥ  jānaśruteḥ pautrāyaṇasya śugutpede tām ṛṣī raikvaḥ śūdra śabdena anena sūcayaṃbabhūva ātmanaḥ parokṣa jña tā khyāpanāya iti gamyate jāti śūdrasya anadhikārāt katham punar  śūdra śabdena śugutpannā sūcyata iti ucyate tadā dravaṇāt  śucam abhidudrāva śucā vā abhidudruve śucā vā raikvam abhidudrāva iti śūdraḥ avayava artha saṃbhavāt rūḍha arthasya ca asaṃbhavāt  dṛśyate ca ayam arthaḥ  asyām ākhyāyikāyām itas ca na jāti śūdraḥ  jānaśrutiḥ yad kāraṇam prakaraṇa nirūpaṇena kṣatriya tvam asya uttaratra caitrarathena abhipratāriṇā kṣatriyeṇa samabhivyāhārāt gamyate uttaratra hi saṃvarga vidyā vākya śeṣe caitrarathiḥ abhipratārī kṣatriyaḥ saṃkīrtyate iti caitrarathi tvam ca abhipratāriṇaḥ kāpeya yogāt avagantavyam kāpeya yogaḥ  hi citrarathasya avagataḥ aetena vai citraratham kāpeyā ayājayan iti samāna anvayānām ca prāyeṇa samāna anvayā yājakā bhavanti atasmāt caitrarathiḥ nāmakaḥ kṣatra patiḥ ajāyata iti ca kṣatrapati tva avagamāt kṣatriya tvam asya avagantavyam tena kṣatriyeṇa abhipratāriṇā saha samānāyām vidyayāyām saṃkīrtanam jānaśruteḥ api kṣatriya tvam sūcayati samānānām eva hi prāyeṇa samabhivyāhārā bhavanti kṣattṛ preṣaṇa ādi aiśvarya yogāt ca jānaśruteḥ kṣatriya tva avagatiḥ atas  na śūdrasya adhikāraḥ itas ca na śūdrasya adhikāraḥ yad vidyā pradeśeṣu upanayana ādayaḥ saṃskārāḥ parāmṛśyante adhīhi bhagava iti ha upasasāda brahma parā brahma niṣṭhāḥ param brahma anveṣamāṇā eṣa ha vai tad sarvam vakṣyati iti te ha samidh pāṇayaḥ  bhagavantam pippalādam upasannāḥ iti ca tān ha anupanīya eva iti api pradarśitā eva upanayana prāptiḥ bhavati śūdrasya saṃskāra abhāvaḥ  abhilapyate aśūdraḥ caturthaḥ  varṇa eka jātiḥ iti eka jāti tva smaraṇāt  ana śūdraḥ  pātakam kiñcid na ca saṃskāram arhati ityādibhiḥ ca itas ca na śūdrasya adhikāraḥ yad satya vacanena śūdra tva abhāve nirdhārite jābālam gautama upanetum anuśāsitum ca pravavṛte anaitat brāhmaṇaḥ  vivaktum arhati samidham somya āhara upa tvā neṣye na satyādagāḥ iti śruti liṅgāt  itas ca na śūdrasya adhikāraḥ yad asya smṛteḥ śravaṇa adhyayana artha pratiṣedhaḥ  bhavati veda śravaṇa pratiṣedhaḥ  veda adhyayana pratiṣedhaḥ tad artha jñāna anuṣṭhānayoḥ ca pratiṣedhaḥ śūdrasya smaryate śravaṇa pratiṣedhaḥ tāvat  aatha asya vedam upaśṛṇvataḥ trapujatubhyām śrotra pratipūraṇam iti apadyu ha vā etad śmaśānam yad śūdraḥ tasmāt śūdra samīpe na adhyetavyam iti ca ata eva adhyayana pratiṣedhaḥ yasya hi samīpe api na adhyetavyam bhavati sa katham aśrutam adhīyīta bhavati ca veda uccāraṇe jihvāt chedaḥ  dhāraṇe śarīra bheda iti ata eva ca arthāt artha jñāna anuṣṭhānayoḥ pratiṣedhaḥ  bhavati ana śūdrasya matim dadyāt iti advijātīnām adhyayanam ijyā dānam iti ca yeṣām punar  pūrva kṛta saṃskāra vaśāt viduḥ dharma vyādha prabhṛtīnām jñāna utpattiḥ teṣām na śakyate phala prāptiḥ pratiṣeddhum jñānasya aikāntika phala tvāt aśrāvayet caturaḥ  varṇān iti ca itihāsa purāṇa adhigame cāturvarṇyasya adhikāra smaraṇāt veda pūrvakaḥ tu na asti adhikāraḥ śūdrāṇām iti sthitam avasitaḥ prāsaṅgikaḥ  adhikāra vicāraḥ prakṛtām eva idānīm vākya artha vicāraṇām pravartayiṣyāmaḥ ayat idam kiñca jagat sarvam prāṇa ejati niḥsṛtam mahat bhayam vajram udyatam ya etad viduḥ amṛtāḥ te bhavanti iti etad vākyam aejṛ kampane iti dhātvartha anugamāt lakṣitam asmin vākye sarvam idam jagat prāṇa āśrayam spandate mahat ca kiñcid bhaya kāraṇam vajra śabditam udyatam tad vijñānāt ca amṛta tva prāptiḥ iti śrūyate tatra kaḥ  asau prāṇaḥ kim tad bhayānakam vajram iti apratipatteḥ vicāre kriyamāṇe prāptam tāvat prasiddheḥ pañcavṛttiḥ vāyuḥ prāṇa iti prasiddheḥ eva ca aśaniḥ vajram syāt  vāyoḥ ca idam māhātmyam saṃkīrtyate katham sarvam idam jagat pañca vṛttau vāyau prāṇa śabdite pratiṣṭhāya ejati vāyu nimittam eva ca mahat bhayānakam vajram udyamyate vāyau hi parjanya bhāvena vivartamāne vidyut stanayitru vṛṣṭi aśanayo vivartanta iti ācakṣate vāyu vijñānāt eva ca idam amṛta tvam tathā hi śruti antaram iti tasmāt vāyuḥ ayam iha pratipattavya iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ brahma eva idam iha pratipattavyam kutas  pūrva uttara ālocanāt  pūrva uttarayoḥ hi grantha bhāgayoḥ brahma evanirdiśyamānam upalabhāmahe iha eva katham akasmāt antarāle vāyum nirdiśyamānam pratipadyemahi pūrvatra tāvat  atat eva śukram tad brahma tad eva amṛtam ucyate tasmin  lokāḥ śritāḥ sarve tad u na atyeti kaścana iti brahma nirdiṣṭam tad eva iha api saṃnidhānāt  jagat sarvam prāṇa ejati iti ca loka āśrayavat tva pratyabhijñānāt nirdiṣṭam iti gamyate prāṇa śabdaḥ  api ayam prayuktaḥ aprāṇasya prāṇam iti darśanāt  ejayitṛ tvam api idam paramātmana eva upapadyate na vāyu mātrasya tathā ca uktam iti uttaratra api abhayāt asya agniḥ tapati bhayāt tapati sūryaḥ bhayāt indraḥ ca vāyuḥ ca mṛtyuḥ dhāvati pañcamaḥ iti brahmā eva nirdekṣyate na vāyuḥ sa vāyukasya jagataḥ  bhaya hetutva abhidhānāt tad eva iha api saṃnidhānāt mahat bhayam vajram udyatam iti ca bhaya hetu tva pratyabhijñānāt nirdiṣṭam iti gamyate vajra śabdaḥ  api ayam bhaya hetu tva sāmānyāt prayuktaḥ yathā hi vajram udyatam mama eva śirasi nipatet yadi aham asya śāsanam na kuryām iti anena bhayena jano niyamena rāja ādi śāsane pravartata evam idam agni vāyu sūrya ādikam jagat asmāt eva brahmaṇaḥ  bibhyat niyamena sva vyāpāre pravartata iti bhayānakam vajra upamitam brahma tathā ca brahma viṣayam śruti antaram iti amṛta tva phala śravaṇāt api brahma eva idam iti gamyate brahma jñānāt hi amṛta tva prāptiḥ atam eva viditvā atimṛtyum eti na anyaḥ panthā vidyate ayanāya iti mantra varṇāt  yad tu vāyu vijñānāt kvacid amṛta tvam abhihitam tad āpekṣikam tatra eva prakaṇa antara karaṇena paramātmānam abhidhāya aanto anyat ārtam iti vāyu ādeḥ ārta tva abhidhānāt prakaraṇāt api atra paramātma niścayaḥ anyatra dharmāt anyatra adharmāt anyatra asmad kṛta akṛtāt  anyatra bhūtāt ca bhavyāt ca yad tad paśyasi tad vada iti paramātmanaḥ pṛṣṭa tvāt  aeṣa saṃprasādaḥ  asmāt śarīrāt samutthāya param jyotiḥ upasaṃpadya svena rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyate iti śrūyate tatra saṃśayyate kim jyotiḥ śabdam cakṣuḥ viṣayatama upaham tejaḥ kiṃvā param brahma iti kim tāvat prāptam prasiddham eva tejaḥ  jyotiḥ śabdam iti kutas  tatra jyotiḥ śabdasya rūḍha tvāt  ajyotiḥḥ caraṇa abhidhānāt iti atra hi prakaraṇa ajyotiḥ śabdaḥ sva artham parityajya brahmaṇi vartate naca iha tadvat kiñcit sva artha parityāge kāraṇam dṛśyate tathā ca nāḍīkhaṇḍe iti mumukṣoḥ āditya prāptiḥ abhihitā tasmāt prasiddham eva tejaḥ  jyotiḥ śabdam iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ param eva brahma jyotiḥ śabdam kasmāt  darśanāt  tasya hi iha prakaraṇe vaktavya tvena anuvṛttiḥ dṛśyate ya ātma apahata pāpmā iti apahata pāpma tva ādi guṇakasya ātmanaḥ prakaraṇa ādau  anveṣṭavya tvena vijijñāsitavya tvena ca pratijñānāt  aetam tu eva te bhūyo anuvyākhyāsyāmi iti ca anusaṃdhānāt  aaśarīram vāvasantam na priya apriye spṛśataḥ iti ca aśarīra tāyai jyotiḥ saṃpatteḥ asya abhidhānāt brahma bhāvāt ca anyatra aśarīra tā anupapatteḥ aparam jyotiḥ asa uttamaḥ puruṣaḥ iti ca viśeṣaṇāt  yad tu uktam mumukṣoḥ āditya prāptiḥ abhihitā iti na asau  ātyantikaḥ  mokṣaḥ  gati utkrānti saṃbandhāt na hi ātyantike mokṣe gati utkrāntī sta iti vakṣyāmaḥ aākāśaḥ  vai nāma nāma rūpayoḥ nirvahitā te yad antarā tad brahma tad amṛtam sa ātmā iti śrūyate tad kim ākāśa sabdam param brahma kiṃvā prasiddham eva bhūtākāśam iti vicāre bhūta parigrahaḥ  yuktaḥ ākāśa śabdasya tasmin rūḍha tvāt nāma rūpa nirvahaṇasya ca avakāśa ādāna dvāreṇa tasmin yojayitum śakya tvāt  sraṣṭṛ tva ādeḥ ca spaṣṭasya brahma liṅgasya aśravaṇāt iti evam prāpta idam ucyate param eva brahma iha ākāśa śabdam bhavitum arhati kasmāt  artha antara tva ādi vyapadeśāt ate yad antarā tad brahma iti hi nāma rūpābhyām artha antara bhūtam ākāśam vyapadiśati na ca brahmaṇaḥ  anyat nāma rūpābhyām artha antaram saṃbhavati sarvasya vikāra jātasya nāma rūpābhyām eva vyākṛta tvāt  nāma rūpayoḥ api nirvahaṇam niraṅ kuśam na brahmaṇaḥ  anyatra saṃbhavati aanena jīvena ātmanā anupraviśya nāma rūpe vyākaravāṇi ityādi brahma kartṛ tva śravaṇāt nanu jīvasya api pratyakṣam nāma rūpa viṣayam nirvoḍhu tvam asti bāḍham asti abhedaḥ tu iha vivakṣitaḥ nāma rūpa nirvahaṇa abhidhānāt eva ca sraṣṭṛ tva ādi brahma liṅgam abhihitam bhavati atat brahma tad amṛtam sa ātmā iti ca brahma vādasya liṅgāni aākāśaḥ tad liṅgāt iti asya eva ayam prapañcaḥ vyapadeśāt iti anuvartate bṛhadāraṇyake ṣaṣṭe prapāṭhake akatama ātmā iti yaḥ  ayam vijñāna mayaḥ prāṇeṣu hṛdi antar jyotiḥ puruṣaḥ iti upakramya bhūyānātma viṣayaḥ prapañcaḥ kṛtaḥ tad kim saṃsāri svarūpa mātra anvākhyāna param vākya mutā saṃsāri svarūpa pratipādana param iti saṃśayaḥ kim tāvat prāptam saṃsāri svarūpa mātra viṣayam eva iti kutas  upakrama upasaṃhārābhyām upakrame ayaḥ  ayam vijñāna mayaḥ prāṇa iṣu iti śārīra liṅgāt  upasaṃhāre ca sa vā eṣa mahān aja ātmā yaḥ  ayam vijñāna mayaḥ prāṇa iṣu iti tad aparityāgāt  madhye api buddha anta ādi avastha upanyāsena tasya eva prapañcanāt iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ parameśvara upadeśa parameva idam vākyam na śārīra mātra anvākhyāna param kasmāt  suṣuptau  utkrāntau ca śarīrāt bhedena parameśvarasya vyapadeśāt  suṣuptau tāvat  aayam puruṣaḥ prājñena ātmanā saṃpariṣvaktaḥ  na bāhyam kiñcana veda na antaram iti śārīrāt bhedena parameśvaram vyapadiśati tatra puruṣaḥ śārīraḥ syāt tasya veditṛ tvāt bāhya abhyantara vedana prasaṅge sati tad pratiṣedha saṃbhavāt prājñaḥ parameśvaraḥ sarvajña tva lakṣaṇayā prajñayā nityam aviyogāt  tathā utkrāntau  api aayam śārīra ātmā prājñena ātmanā anvārūḍha utsarjanyāti iti jīvāt bhedena parameśvaram vyapadiśati tatra api śārīraḥ  jīvaḥ syāt śarīra svāmi tvāt  prājñaḥ tu sa eva parameśvaraḥ tasmāt suṣupti utkrāntyoḥ bhedena vyapadeśāt parameśvara eva atra vivakṣata iti gamyate yad uktam ādi anta madhyeṣu śārīra liṅgāt tatparatvam asya vākyasya iti atra brūmaḥ upakrametāvat  ayaḥ  ayam vijñāna mayaḥ prāṇeṣu iti na saṃsāri svarūpam vivakṣitam kim tarhi anūdya saṃsāri svarūpam pareṇa brahmaṇā asya ekatām vivakṣati yatas  adhyāyati iva lelāyati iva iti evamādi uttara grantha pravṛttiḥ saṃsāri dharma nirākaraṇa parā lakṣyate tathā upasaṃhāre api yathā upakramam eva upasaṃharati yam vijñāna mayaḥ prāṇa iṣu iti yaḥ  ayam vijñāna mayaḥ prāṇeṣu saṃsārī lakṣyate sa vā eṣa mahān aja ātmā parameśvara eva asmābhiḥ pratipādita iti arthaḥ yaḥ tu madhye buddha anta ādi avastha upanyāsāt saṃsāri svarūpa vivakṣām manyante na prācīm api diśam prasthāpitaḥ pratīcīm api diśam pratiṣṭheta yatas  na buddha anta ādi avastha upanyāsena avasthāvat tvam saṃsāri tvam vā vivakṣati kim tarhi avasthā rahita tva saṃsāri tvam ca katham etad avagamyate yad  aata ūrdhve vimokṣāya eva brūhi iti pade pade pṛcchati yad ca aananvāgataḥ tena bhavati asaṅgaḥ  hi ayam puruṣaḥ iti pade pade prativakti aananvāgatam puṇyena ananvāgatam pāpena tīrṇaḥ  hi tadā sarvān śokān hṛdayasya bhavati iti ca tasmāt asaṃsāri svarūpa pratipādana param eva etad vākyam iti avagantavyam itas ca asaṃsāri svarūpa pratipādana param eva etad vākyam iti avagantavyam yad asmin vākye pati ādayaḥ śabdā asaṃsāri svarūpa pratipādana parāḥ saṃsāri svabhāva pratiṣedhanāḥ ca bhavanti asarvasya vaśī sarvasya īśānaḥ sarvasya adhipatiḥ iti evan jātīyakā asaṃsāri svabhāva pratipādana parāḥ asa na sādhunā karmaṇā bhūyāt naḥ  eva asādhunā kanīyān iti evan jātīyakāḥ saṃsāri svabhāva pratiṣedhanāḥ tasmāt asaṃsārī parameśvara iha ukta iti avagamyate iti śrīmat śaṅkara bhagavat pāda kṛtau śārīrakamī māṃsa ābhāṣye prathama adhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ brahma jijñāsām pratijñāya brahmaṇaḥ  lakṣaṇam uktam iti tad lakṣaṇam pradhānasya api samānam iti āśaṅkya tad aśabda tvena nirākṛtam iti gatismānyam ca vedānta vākyānām brahma kāraṇa vādam prati vidyate na pradhāna kāraṇa vādam prati iti prapañcitam gatena granthena idam tu idānīm avaśiṣṭam āśaṅkṣyate yad uktam pradhānasya aśabda tvam tad asiddham kāsuci  chāsvāsu pradhāna samarpaṇa ābhāsānām śabdanām śrūyamāṇa tvāt  atas  pradhānasya kāraṇa tvam veda siddham eva mahadbhiḥ parama ṛṣibhiḥ kapila prabhṛtibhiḥ parigṛhītam iti prasajyate tad yāvat teṣām śabdānām anya para tvam na pratipādyate tāvat sarvajñam brahma jagataḥ kāraṇam iti pratipāditam api ākulībhavet atas teṣām anya paratvam darśayitum paraḥ saṃdarbhaḥ pravartate ānumānikam api anumāna nirūpitam api pradhānam ekeṣām śākhinām śabdavat upalabhyate kāṭhake hi paṭhyate iti tatra ya eva yad nāmānaḥ  yad kramāt ca mahat avyakta puruṣāḥ smṛti prasiddhāḥ ta eva iha pratyabhijñāyante tatra avyaktam iti smṛti prasiddheḥ śabda ādi hīna tvāt ca na vyaktam avyaktam iti vyutpatti saṃbhavāt  smṛti prasiddham pradhānam abhidhīyate tasya śabdavat tvāt aśabda tvam anupapannam tad eva ca jagataḥ kāraṇam śruti smṛti nyāya prasiddhibhya iti ced  na etad evam na hi etad kāṭakam vākyam smṛti nyāya prasiddhayoḥ mahat avyaktayoḥ astitva param na hi atra yādṛśam smṛti prasiddham svatantram kāraṇam triguṇam pradhānam tādṛśam pratyabhijñāyate śabda mātram hi atra avyaktam itipratyabhijñāyate sa ca śabdaḥ  na vyaktam avyaktam iti yaugika tvāt anyasmin  api sūkṣme su durlakṣye ca prayujyate nacāyam kasmiṃścid rūḍhaḥ yā tu pradhāna vādinām rūḍhiḥ sā teṣām eva pāribhāṣikī satī na veda artha nirūpaṇe kāraṇa bhāvam pratipadyate na ca krama mātra sāmānyāt samāna artha pratipattiḥ bhavati asati tad rūpa pratyabhijñāne na hi aśva sthāne gām paśyan  aśvo ayam iti amūḍhaḥ  adhyavasyati prakaraṇa nirūpaṇāyām ca atra na para parikalpitam pradhānam pratīyate śarīra rūpa kavinyasgṛhīteḥ śarīram hi atra ratha rūpaka vinyastam avyakta śabdena parigṛhyate kutas  prakaraṇāt pariśeṣāt ca tathā hi anantarātītaḥ  grantha ātma śarīra vādinām rathi ratha ādirūpaka kḷptim darśayati iti taiḥ ca indriya ādibhiḥ asaṃyataiḥ saṃsāram adhigacchati saṃyataiḥ tvadhvanaḥ pāram tad viṣṇoḥ paramam padam āpnoti darśayitvā kim tad adhvanaḥ pāram viṣṇoḥ paramam padam iti asyām ākāṅkṣāyām tebhya eva prakṛtebhyaḥ  indriya ādibhyaḥ paratvena paramātmānam adhvanaḥ pāram viṣṇoḥ paramam padam darśayati iti tatra ya eva indriya ādayaḥ pūrvasyām ratha rūpaka kalpanāyām aśva ādi bhāvena prakṛtāḥ te  eva iha parigṛhyante prakṛta hānā prakṛta prakriyā parihārāya tatra indriya manaḥ buddhayaḥ tāvat pūrvatra iha ca samāna śabdā eva arthā ye śabda ādayaḥ  viṣayā indriya haya gocara tvena nirdiṣṭāḥ teṣām ca indriyebhyaḥ paratvam aindriyāṇām graha tvam viṣayāṇām atigraha tvam iti śruti prasiddheḥ viṣayebhyaḥ ca manasaḥ para tvam manaḥ mūla tvāt viṣaya indriya vyavahārasya manasaḥ tu parā buddhiḥ buddhim hi āruhya bhogya jātam bhoktāram upasarpati buddheḥ ātmā mahān paraḥ yaḥ sa aātmānam rathinam viddhi iti rathi tvena upakṣiptaḥ kutas  ātma śabdāt  bhoktuḥ ca bhoga upakaraṇāt paratva upapatteḥ mahat tvam ca asya svāmi tvāt upapannam athavā amanaḥ  mahānta matiḥ brahmā pūrbuddhiḥ khyatiḥ īśvaraḥ prajñā saṃvid citiḥ ca eva smṛtiḥ ca paripaṭhyate iti smṛteḥ ayaḥ  brahmāṇam vidadhāti pūrvam yaḥ  vai vedān  ca prahiṇoti tasmai iti ca śruteḥ yā prathama jasya hiraṇyagarbhasya buddhiḥ sā sarvāsām buddhīnām parā pratiṣṭhā sā iha mahān ātmā iti ucyate sā ca pūrvatra buddhi grahaṇena eva gṛhītā satī hirugīha upadiśyate tasyāḥ  api asmādīya abhyaḥ  buddhibhyaḥ paratva upapatteḥ etasmin  tu pakṣe paramātma viṣayeṇa eva pareṇa puruṣa grahaṇena rathina ātmanaḥ  grahaṇam draṣṭavyam paramārthataḥ paramātma vijñāna ātmanoḥ bheda abhāvāt tad evam śarīram eva ekam pariśiṣyate itarāṇi indriya ādīni prakṛtāni eva parama pada didarśayiṣayā samanukrāman pariśiṣyamāṇena iha antyena avyakta śabdena pariśiṣyamāṇam prakṛtam śarīram darśayati iti gamyate śarīra indriya manaḥ buddhi viṣaya vedanā saṃyuktasya hi avidyāvataḥ  bhoktuḥ śarīra ādīnām ratha ādi rūpaka kalpanayā saṃsāra mokṣa gati nirūpaṇena pratyagātma brahma avagatiḥ iha vivakṣitā tathā ca aeṣa sarveṣu bhūteṣu gūḍha ātmā na prakāśate dṛśyate tu agryayā buddhyā sūkṣmayā sūkṣma darśibhiḥ iti vaiṣṇavasya parama padasya duravagam atvam uktvā tad avagama artham yogam darśayati iti etad uktam bhavati vācam manasi saṃyacchet  vāc ādi bāhya indriya vyāpāram utsṛjya manaḥ mātreṇa avatiṣṭheta manaḥ  api viṣaya vikalpa abhimikham vikalpa doṣa darśanena jñāna śabda uditāyām buddhau  adhyavasāya svabhāvāyām dhārayet  tām api buddhim mahati ātmani bhoktari agryāyām vā buddhau sūkṣma tā āpāt anena niyacchet  mahāntam tu ātmānam śānta ātmani prakaraṇavati parasmin puruṣe parasyām kāṣṭhāyām pratiṣṭhāpayet iti ca tad evam pūrva apara ālocanāyām na asti atra para parikalpitasya pradhānasya avakāśaḥ uktam etad prakaraṇa parīśeṣābhyām śarīram avyakta śabdaḥ na pradhānam iti idam idānīm āśaṅkyate katham avyakta śabda arha tvam śarīrasya yāvatā sthūla tvāt spṛṣṭataram idam śarīram vyakta śabda arham aspaṣṭa vacanaḥ tu avyakta śabda iti ata uttaram ucyate sūkṣmam tu iha kāraṇa ātmanā śarīram vivakṣyate sūkṣmasya avyakta śabda arha tvāt yadi api sthūlam idam śarīram na svayam avyakta śabdam arhati tathā api tasya tu ārambhakam bhūta sūkṣmam avyakta śabdam arhati prakṛti śabdaḥ ca vikāre dṛṣṭaḥ yathā agobhiḥ śrīṇīta matsaram iti śrutiḥ ca iti idam eva vyākṛta nāma rūpa vibhinnam jagat prāc avasthāyām parityakta vyākṛta nāma rūpam bīja śakti avastham avyakta śabda yogam darśayati atra āha yadi jagat idam anabhivyakta nāma rūpam bīja ātmakam prāc avastham avyakta śabda arham abhyupagamyeta tad ātmanā ca śarīrasya api avyakta śabda arha tvam pratijñāyeta sa eva tarhi pradhāna kāraṇa vāda evam satyāpadyeta asya eva jagataḥ prāc avasthāyāḥ pradhāna tvena abhyupagamāt iti atra ucyate yadi vayam svatantrām kāñcid prāc avasthām jagataḥ kāraṇa tvena abhyupagacchema prasañjyema tadā pradhāna kāraṇa vādam parameśvara adhīnā tu iyam asmābhiḥ prāk avasthā jagataḥ  abhyupagamyate na svatantrā sā ca avaśya abhyupagantavyā arathavatī hi sā na hi tayā vinā parameśvarasya sraṣṭṛ tvam siddhayati śakti rahitasya tasya pravṛtti anupapatteḥ muktānām ca punar anutpattiḥ kutas  vidyayā tasyāḥ  bīja śakteḥ dāhāt  avidyā ātmikā hi bīja śaktiḥ avyakta śabda nirdeśyā parameśvara āśrayā māyā mayī mahā suptiḥ yasyām svarūpa pratibodha rahitāḥ śerate saṃsāriṇaḥ  jīvāḥ tad etad avyaktam kvacid ākāśa śabda nirdiṣṭam iti śruteḥ kvacid akṣara śabda uditam iti śruteḥ kvacid māyā iti sūcitam iti mantra varṇāt  avyaktā hi sā māyā tattva anya tva nirūpaṇasya aśakya tvāt tad idam amahataḥ param avyaktam iti uktam avyakta prabhava tvāt mahataḥ yadā hairaṇyagarbhī buddhiḥ mahān yadā tu jīvaḥ  mahān  tadā api avyakta adhīna tvāt jīva bhāvasya mahataḥ param avyaktam iti uktam avidyā hi avyaktam avidyāvat tvena eva jīvasya sarvaḥ saṃvyavahāraḥ saṃtataḥ  vartate mahataḥ para tvam abheda upacārāt tad vikāre śarīre parikalpyate sati api śarīravat indriya ādīnām tad vikāra tva aviśeṣe śarīrasya eva abheda upacārāt avyakta śabdena grahaṇam indriya ādīnām sva śabdaiḥ eva gṛhīta tvāt pariśiṣṭa tvāt ca śarīrasya anye tu varṇayanti dvividham hi śarīram sthūlam sūkṣmam ca sthūlam yad idam upalabhyate sūkṣmam yad uttaratra vakṣyate iti tad ca ubhayam api śarīram aviśeṣāt pūrvatra ratha tvena saṃkīrtitam iha tu sūkṣmam avyakta śabdena parigṛhyate sūkṣmasya avyakta śabda arha tvāt tad adhīna tvāt ca bandha mokṣa vyavahārasya jīvāt tasya paratvam yathārtha adhīna tvāt indriya vyāpārasya indriyebhyaḥ para tvam arthānām iti taiḥ tu etad vaktavyam aviśeṣeṇa śarīra dvayasya pūrvatra ratha tvena saṃkīrtita tvāt samānayoḥ prakṛta pariśiṣṭa tvayoḥ katham sūkṣmam eva śarīram iha gṛhyate na punar  sthūlam api iti āmnātasya artham pratipattum prabhavāmaḥ  na āmnā atam paryanuyoktum āmnātam ca avyakta padam sūkṣmam eva pratipādayitum śaknoti na itarat vyakta tvāt tasya iti ced  na eka vākyata adhīna tvāt artha pratipatteḥ na hi ime pūrva uttare āmnāte eka vākyatām anāpadya kañcid artham pratipādayataḥ para kṛta hāna aprakṛta prakriyā prasaṅgāt  naca ākāṅkṣām antareṇa eka vākyatā pratipattiḥ asti tatra avaśiṣṭāyām śarīra dvayasya grāhya tva ākāṅkṣāyām yathākāṅkṣam saṃbandhe anabhyupagamyamāna eka vākyatā eva bādhitā bhavati kuta āmnātasya artha pratipattiḥ na ca evam mantavyam duḥśodha tvāt sūkṣmasya eva śarīrasya iha grahaṇam sthūlasya tu dṛṣṭa bībhatsa tayā su śodha tvāt agrahaṇam iti yatas  na eva iha śodhanam kasyacid vivakṣyate na hi atra śodhana vidhāyi kiñcid ākhyātam asti anantara nirdiṣṭa tvāt tu kim tad viṣṇoḥ paramam padam iti idam iha vivakṣyate tathā ahi idam asmāt param idam asmāt param iti uktvā apuruṣān na param kiñcit iti āha sarvathā api tvā anumānika nirakaraṇa upapatteḥ tathā nāma astu na naḥ kiñcicchidyate jñeya tvena ca sāṃkhyaiḥ pradhānam smaryate guṇa puruṣa antara jñānāt kaivalyam itivadbhiḥ na hi guṇa svarūpam ajñā tvā guṇebhyaḥ puruṣasya antaram śakyam jñātum iti kvacid ca vibhūti viśeṣa prāptaye pradhānam jñeyam iti smaranti nacet agiha avyaktam jñeya tvena ucyate pada mātram hi avyakta śabdaḥ na iha avyaktam jñātavyam upāsitavyam ca iti vākyam asti naca anupadiṣṭa padārtha jñānam puruṣa artham iti śakyam pratipattum tasmāt api na avyakta śabdena pradhānam abhidhīyate asmākam tu ratha rūpaka kḷpta śarīra ādi anusaraṇena viṣṇoḥ eva paramam padam darśayitum ayam upanyāsa iti anavadyam vadati iti ced  na prājñaḥ  hi prakaraṇāt  atra āha sāṃkhyaḥ jñeya tva avacanāt  iti asiddham katham śrūyate hi uttaratra avyakta śabda uditasya pradhānasya jñeya tva vacanam iti atra hi yādṛśam śabda ādi hīnam pradhānam mahataḥ param smṛtau nirūpitam tādṛśam eva nicāyya tvena nirdiṣṭam tasmāt pradhānam eva idam tad eva ca avyakta śabda nirdiṣṭam iti atra brūmaḥ na iha pradhānam nicāyya tvena nirdiṣṭam prājñaḥ  hi iha paramātmā nicāyya tveta nirdiṣṭam iti gamyate kutas  prakaraṇāt  prājñasya hi prakaraṇam vitatam vartate apuruṣān na param kiñcid sā kāṣṭhā sā parā gatiḥ ityādi nirdeśāt aeṣa sarveṣu bhūteṣu gūḍhotmā na prakāśate iti ca durjñāta tva vacanena tasya eva jñeya tva ākāṅkṣaṇāt  ayacchet vāc manasī prājñaḥ iti ca tad jñānāya eva vāc ādi saṃyamasya vihita tvāt  mṛtyu mukha pramokṣaṇa phala tvāt ca na hi pradhāna mātram nicāyya mṛtyu mukhāt pramucyata iti sāṃkhyaiḥ iṣyate cetana ātma vijñānāt hi mṛtyu mukhāt pramucyate iti teṣām abhyupagamaḥ sarveṣu vedānteṣu prājñasya eva ātmanaḥ  aśabda ādi dharma tvam abhilapyate tasmāt na pradhānasya atra jñeya tvam avyakta śabda nirdiṣṭa tvam vā itas ca na pradhānasya avyakta śabda vācya tvam jñeya tvam vā yasmāntrayāṇām eva padārthān magni jīva paramātmanām asmin granthe kaṭhavallīṣu vara pradhāna sāmarthyāt vakta vyatā upanyāsaḥ  dṛśyate tad viṣaya eva ca praśnaḥ na atas  anyasya praśna upanyāsaḥ  vā asti tatra tāvat  asa tvam agnim svargya madhyeṣi mṛtyo prabrūhi tam śraddadhānāya mahyam iti agni viṣayaḥ praśnaḥ ayeyam prete vicikitsā manuṣye asti iti eke na ayam asti iti ca eke etad vidyām anuśiṣṭaḥ tvayā aham varāṇām eṣa varaḥ tṛtīyaḥ iti jīva viṣayaḥ praśnaḥ aanyatra dharmāt antra adharmāni atra asmad kṛta akṛtāt  anyatra bhūtāt ca bhavyāt ca yad tad paśyasi tad vada iti paramātma viṣayaḥ prativacanam api aloka ādimam agnim tam uvāca tasmai yā iṣṭakāyāvatīrvā yathā vā iti agni viṣayam ahanta ta idam pravakṣyāmi guhyam brahma sanātanam yathā ca maraṇam prāpya ātmā bhavati gautama yonim anye prapadyante śarīra tvāya dehinaḥ sthāṇum anye anusaṃyanti yathākarma yathāśrutam iti vyavahitam jīva viṣayam ana jāyate mriyate vā vipaścit ityādi bahu prapañcam paramātma viṣayam na evam pradhāna viṣayaḥ praśnaḥ  asti apṛṣṭa tvāt ca anupanyasanīya tvam tasya iti atra āha yaḥ  ayam ātma viṣayaḥ praśnaḥ  yā iyam prete vicikitsā manuṣye asti iti kim sa eva ayam aanyatra dharmāt anyatra adharmāt iti punar anukṛṣyate kiṃvā tatas  anyaḥ  ayam apūrvaḥ praśna utthāpyata iti kicātaḥ sa eva ayam praśnaḥ punar anukṛṣyata iti yadi ucyeta dvayoḥ ātma viṣayayoḥ praśnayoḥ eka tā āpatteḥ agni viṣaya ātma viṣayaḥ ca dvau  eva praśnau  iti ato na vaktavyam trayāṇām praśna upanyāsau  iti atha anyaḥ  ayam apūrvaḥ praśnaḥ utthāpyata iti ucyeta tatas  yathā eva vara pradāna vyatirekeṇa praśna kalpanāyām adoṣa evam praśna vyatirekeṇa api pradhāna upanyāsa kalpanā āyāma doṣaḥ syāt iti atra ucyate na evam vayam iha vara pradāna vyatirekeṇa praśnam kañcid kalpayāmaḥ  vākya upakrama sāmarthyāt  vara pradāna upakramā hi mṛtyu naciketaḥ saṃvāda rūpā vākya pravṛttiḥ āsamāpteḥ kaṭhavat līnām lakṣyate mṛtyuḥ kila nāciketase pitrā prahitāya trīn varān pradadau naciketāḥ kila teṣām prathamena vareṇa saumanasyam vavre dvitīyena agni vidyām tṛtīyena ātma vidyām ayeyam prete iti avarāṇām eva varaḥ tṛtīyaḥ iti liṅgāt  tatra yadi anyatra dharmāt iti anyo ayam apūrvaḥ praśna utthāpyeta tatas  vara pradāna vyatirekeṇa api praśna kalpanāt vākyam bādhyetha nanu praṣṭhavya bhedāt apūrvaḥ  ayam praśnaḥ  bhavitum arhati pūrvo hi praśnaḥ  jīva viṣayaḥ yoyam prete vicikitsā manuṣye asti na asti iti vicikitsā abhidhānāt jīvaḥ ca dharma ādi gocara tvāt na anyatra dharmāt iti praśnam arhati prājñaḥ tu dharma ādi atīta tvāt anyatra anyatra dharmāt iti praśnam arhati praśna  chāyā ca na samānā lakṣyate pūrvasya astitva nāstitva viṣaya tvāt uttarasya dharma ādi atīta vastu viṣaya tvāt tasmāt pratyabhijñāna abhāvāt praśna bhedaḥ na pūrvasya eva uttaratra anukarṣaṇam iti ced  na jīva prājñayoḥ eka tva abhyupagamāt bhavet praṣṭavya bhedāt praśna bhedaḥ  yadi anyaḥ  jīvaḥ prājñāt syāt  na tu anya tvam asti tad tvam asi iti ādi śruti antarebhyaḥ iha ca anyatra dharma ādityasya praśnasya prativacanam ana jāyate mriyate vā vipaścit iti janma maraṇa pratiṣedhena pratipādyamānam śārīra parameśvarayoḥ abhedam darśayati sati hi prasaṅge pratiṣedhaḥ  bhāgī bhavati prasaṅgaḥ ca janma maraṇayoḥ śarīra saṃsparśāt śārīrasya bhavati na parameśvarasya tathā yad eva iha tad amutra yad amutra tad anu iha mṛtyoḥ sa mṛtyum āpnoti ya iha na anā iva paśyati iti jīva prājña bheda dṛṣṭim apavat ati tathā jīva vīṣayasya
