astitva nāstitva praśnasya anantaram aanyam varam naciketa u vṛṇīṣva iti ārabhya mṛtyunā taiḥ taiḥ kāmaiḥ pralobhyamānaḥ  api naciketā yadā na cacāla tadā enam mṛtyuḥ abhyudaya nīḥ śreyasa vibhāga pradarśanena vidyā avidyā vibhāga pradarśanena ca avidyā abhīpsinam naciketasam manye na tvā kāmā bahavaḥ  alolupanta iti praśasya praśnam api tadīyam praśaṃsanyat uvāca iti tena api jīva prājñayoḥ abheda eva iha vivakṣata iti gamyate yad praśna nimittām ca praśaṃsām mahatīm mṛtyoḥ pratyapadyata naciketā yadi tam vihāya praśaṃsā anantaram anyam eva praśnam upakṣipet asthāna eva sā sarvā praśaṃsā prasāritā syāt  tasmāt  ayeyam prete iti asya eva praśnasya etad anukarṣaṇam aanyatra dharmāt iti yad tu praśna  chāyā vailakṣaṇyam uktam tad adūṣaṇam tadīyasya eva viśeṣasya punar  pṛcchyamāna tvāt  pūrvatra hi deha ādi vyatiriktasya ātmanaḥ  astitvam pṛṣṭam uttaratra tu tasya eva asaṃsāri tvam pṛcchyata iti yāvat hi avidyā na nivartate tāvat dharma ādi gocara tvam jīvasya jīva tvam ca na nivartate tad nivṛttau tu prājña eva tad tvam asi iti śrutyā pratyāyyate naca avidyāvat tve tad apagame ca vastunaḥ kaścid viśeṣaḥ  asti yathā kaścid saṃtamase patitām kāñcid rajju m ahim manyamānaḥ  bhītaḥ  vepamānaḥ palāyate tam ca aparaḥ  brūyāt mā bhaṣīḥ na aya mahī rajjuḥ eva iti sa ca tad upaśrutya ahi kṛtam bhayam utsṛjet vepathum palāyanam ca na tu ahi buddhi kāle tad apagama kāle ca vastunaḥ kaścid viśeṣaḥ syāt  tathā eva etad api draṣṭavyam tatas ca ana jāyate mriyate vā iti evamādi api bhavati astitva praśnasya prativacanam sūtram tu avidyā kalpita jīva prājña bheda apekṣayā yojayitavyam ekatve api hi ātma viṣayasya praśnasya prāyaṇa avasthāyām deha vyatirikta astitva mātra vicikitsānāt kartṛ tva ādi saṃsāra svabhāvān apohanāt ca pūrvasya paryāyasya jīva viṣaya tvam utprekṣyate uttarasya tu dharma ādi atyaya saṃkīrtanāt prājña viṣaya tvam iti tatas ca yukta agni jīva param ātma kalpanā pradhāna kalpanāyām tu na vara pradānam na praśnaḥ  na prativacanam iti vaiṣamyam yathā mahat śabdaḥ sāṃkhyaiḥ sattā mātre api prathama je prayukte na tam eva vaidike api prayoge abhidhatte abuddheḥ ātmā mahān paraḥ amahāntam vibhum ā ātmānam aveda aham etam puruṣam mahāntam iti evam ādau  ātma śabda prayoga ādibhyaḥ  hetubhyaḥ tathā avyakta śabdaḥ  api na vaidike prayoge pradhānam abhidhātum arhati atas ca na asya anumānikasya śabdavat tvam camasa adhikaraṇam sū camasavat aviśeṣāt  punar api pradhāna vādya śabda tvam pradhānasya asiddham iti āha kasmāt  mantra varṇāt  nuśete jahāti enām bhukta bhogām ajaḥ  anyaḥ iti atra hi mantre lohita śukla kṛṣṇa śabdai rajaḥ sattvata māṃsi abhidhīyante lohitam rajaḥ  rañjana ātmaka tvāt  śuklam sattvam prakāśa ātmaka tvāt  kṛṣṇam tama āvaraṇāt katvāt  teṣām sāmya avasthā avayava dharmaiḥ vyapadiśyate lohita śukla kṛṣṇam iti na jāyata iti ca ajā syāt  amūla prakṛtiḥ avikṛtiḥ iti abhyupagamāt  nanu ajā śabdaḥ chāgāyām rūḍhaḥ bāḍham sā tu rūḍhiḥ iha na āśrayitum śakyā vidyā prakaraṇāt  sā ca vahnīḥ prajāḥ traiguṇya anvitā janayati tām prakṛtim aja ekaḥ puruṣaḥ  juṣamāṇaḥ prīyamāṇaḥ sevamānaḥ  vā anuśete tām eva avidyāya ātma tvena upagamya sukhī duḥkhī mūḍhaḥ  aham iti aviveka tayā saṃsarati anyaḥ punar ajaḥ puruṣe utpanna viveka jñānaḥ  viraktaḥ  jahāti enām prakṛtim bhukta bhogām kṛta bhoga apavargām parityajati mucyata iti arthaḥ tasmāt śruti mūlā eva pradhāna ādi kalpanām iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ na anena mantreṇa śrutimat tva sāṃkhya vādasya śakyam āśrayitum na hi ayam mantraḥ svātantryeṇa kañcid api vādam samarthayitum utsahate sarvatra api yayā kayācid kalpanayā jātu ādi saṃpādana upapatteḥ sāṃkhya vāda eva iha abhipreta iti viśeṣa avadhāraṇa kāraṇa abhāvāt camasavat  yathā hi arvāc balaḥ camasa ūrdhva budhnaḥ iti asmina mantre svātantryeṇa ayam nāma asau camaso abhipreta iti na śakyate nirūpayitum sarvatra api yathā kathañcit arvāk bila tva ādi kalpanā upapatteḥ evam iha api aviśeṣaḥ  ajām ekām iti asya mantrasya na asmin mantre pradhānam eva aja abhipreta iti śakyate niyantum tatra tu aidam tad śira eṣa hi arvāc bilaḥ camasa ūrdhva budhnaḥ iti vākya śeṣāt camasa viśeṣa pratipattiḥ bhavati iha punar  kā iyam ajā pratipattavyā iti atra brūmaḥ parameśvarāt utpannā jyotiḥ pramukhā tejaḥ banna lakṣaṇā caturvidhasya bhūta grāmasya prakṛti bhūtā iyam ajā pratipattavyā tuśabdaḥ  avadhāṇa arthaḥ bhūta traya lakṣaṇā eva iyam ajā vijñeyā na guṇatraya lakṣaṇā kasmāt  tathā hi eke śākhinaḥ tejaḥ bannānām parameśvarāt utpattim āmnāya teṣām eva rohita ādi rūpa tām āmananti iti tāni eva iha tejaḥ bannāni pratyabhijñāyante rohita ādi śabda sāmānyāt rohita ādīnām ca śabdānām rūpa viśeṣeṣu mukhya tvāt bhākta tvāt ca guṇa viṣaya tvasya asaṃdigdhena ca saṃdigdhasya nigamanam nyāyyam manyante tathā iha api abrahma vādinaḥ  vadanti kiṅkāraṇam brahma iti upakramya ate dyāna yoga anugatā apaśyan deva ātma śaktim sva guṇaiḥ nigūḍhām iti pārameśvaryāḥ śakteḥ samasta jagat vidhāyinyā vākya upakrame avagamāt  vākya śeṣe api amāyām tu prakṛti vidyāt māyinam tu maheśvaram iti ayaḥ  yonim yonim adhitiṣṭhati ekaḥ iti ca tasyāḥ  eva avagamāt na svatantrā kācid prakṛtiḥ pradhānam nāma jāmantreṇa āmnā āyata iti śakyate vaktum prakaraṇāt tu sā eva daivī śaktiḥ avyākṛta nāma rūpā nāma rūpayoḥ prāc avasthānena api mantreṇa āmnāyata iti ucyate tasyāḥ ca sva vikāra viṣayeṇa trairūpyeṇa trairūpyam uktam katham punar tejaḥ ban  ātmanā trairūpyeṇa trirūpā jā pratipattum śakyate yāvatā na tāvat tejaḥ banneṣu ajā ākṛtiḥ asti na ca tejaḥ bannānām jāti śravaṇāt ajāti nimittaḥ  api ajā śabdaḥ saṃbhavati iti ata uttaram paṭhati na ayam aja ākṛti nimittaḥ  ajā śabdaḥ na api yaugikaḥ kim tarhi kalpanā upadeśaḥ  ayam ajā rūpaka kḷptiḥ tejaḥ banna lakṣaṇāyāḥ carācara yoneḥ upadiśyate yathā hi loke yadṛcchayā kācid ajā rohita śukla kṛṣṇaṇa varṇā syāt bahubarkarā sarūpa barkarā ca tām ca kaścid ajaḥ  juṣamāṇaḥ  anuśayīta kaścid ca enām bhukta bhogām juhyāt  evam iyam api tejaḥ banna lakṣaṇā bhūta prakṛtiḥ tri varṇā bahu sarūpam carācara lakṣaṇam vikāra jātam janayati aviduṣā ca kṣetrajñena upabhujyate viduṣā ta parityajata iti naca idam āśaṅkitavyam ekaḥ kṣetrajñaḥ  anuśete anyaḥ  jahāti iti atas  kṣetrajña bhedaḥ pāramārthikaḥ pareṣa ām iṣṭaḥ prāpnoti iti na hīyam kṣetrajña bheda pratipipādayiṣā kintu bandha mokṣa vyavasthā pratipipādayiṣā tu eṣā prasiddham tu bhedam anudya bandha mokṣa vyavasthā pratipādyate bheda stu upādhi nimittaḥ  mithyājñāna kalpitaḥ  na pāramārthikaḥ aekaḥ  devaḥ sarva bhūteṣu gūḍhaḥ sarva vyāpī sarva bhūta antarātmā ityādi śrutibhyaḥ madhu ādivat  yathā aādityasya ām adhunaḥ  madhu tvam avācāḥ ca adhena ūrdhenu tvam adyuloka ādīnām ca anagnīnām agni tvam iti evan jātīyakam kalpyate evam idamanajāyā ajā tvam kalpyata iti arthaḥ tasmāt avirodhaḥ tejaḥ banneṣu ajā śabda prayogasya evam parigṛhīte api ajā mantre punar anyasmāt mantrāt sāṃkhyaḥ pratyavatiṣṭhate ayasmin pañca pañcajanā ākāśaḥ ca pratiṣṭhitaḥ tam eva manya ātmānam vidvān brahmā amṛtaḥ  amṛtam iti asmin mantre pañca pañcajanā iti pañca saṃkhyā viṣayā aparā pañca saṃkhyā śrūyate pañca dvaya śabda darśanāt  ta ete pañca pañcakāḥ pañcaviṃśatiḥ saṃpadyante tathā pañcaviṃśati saṃkhyayā yāvantaḥ saṃkhyeyā ākāṅkṣyantelatāvanti ā iva ca tattvāni sāṃkhyaiḥ saṃkhyāyante iti tayā śruti prasiddhayā pañcaviṃśati saṃkhyayā teṣām smṛti prasiddhānām pañcaviṃśati tattvānām upasaṃgrahāt prāptam punar  śrutimat tvam eva pradhāna ādīnām tatas  brūmaḥ na saṃkhyā upasaṃgrahāt api pradhāna ādīnām śrutimat tvam pratyāśā kartavyā kasmāt  nānā bhāvāt nānā hi etāni pañcaviṃśatiḥ tattvāni na eṣām pañcaśas  pañcaśas  sādhāraṇaḥ  dharmaḥ  asti yena pañcaviṃśateḥ antarāle parāḥ pañca pañca saṃkhyā niveśeran na hi eka nibandhanam antareṇa nānā bhūteṣu dvi tva ādikāḥ saṃkhyā niviśante atha ucyeta pañcaviṃśati saṃkhyā eva iyam avayava dvāreṇa lakṣyate yathā apañca sapta ca varṣāṇi na vavarṣa śatakratuḥ iti dvādaśa vārṣikīm anāvṛṣṭim kathayanti tadvat iti tad api na upapadyate ayam eva asmin pakṣe doṣaḥ  yad lakṣaṇa āśrayaṇīyā syāt  paraḥ ca atra pañca śabdaḥ  jana śabdena samastaḥ pañcajanā iti pāribhāṣikeṇa svareṇa eka pada tva niścayāt prayoga antare ca apañcānām tvā pañcajanānām iti aikapadya eka svarya eka vibhaktika tva avagamāt samastasya na vīpsā pañca pañca iti na ca pacaka dvaya grahaṇam pañca pañca iti na ca pañca saṃkhyāyā ekasyāḥ pañca saṃkhyayā parayā viśeṣaṇam pañca pañcakā iti upasarjanasya viśeṣaṇena asaṃyogāt nanu āpanna pañca saṃkhyakā janā eva punar  pañca saṃkhyayā viśeṣyamāṇāḥ pañcaviṃśatiḥ pratyeṣyante yathā pañca pañca pūlya iti pañcavaṃśati pūlāḥ pratīyante tadvat  na iti brūmaḥ yuktam yad pañca pūlī śabdasya samāhāra abhiprāya tvāt kati iti satyām bheda ākāṅkṣāyām pañca pañca pūlya iti viśeṣaṇam iha tu pañca pañca janā iti ādita eva bheda upādānāt kati iti asatyām bheda ākāṅkṣāyām na pañca pañcajanā iti viśeṣaṇam bhavet  bhavat api idam viśeṣaṇam pañca saṃkhyāyā eva bhavet  tatra ca uktaḥ  doṣaḥ tasmāt pañca pañcajanā iti na pañcaviṃśati tattva abhiprāyam atirekāt ca na pañcaviṃśati tattva abhiprāyam atirekāt ca na pañcaviṃśati tattva abhiprāyam atirekaḥ  hi bhavati ātma ākāśābhyām pañcaviṃśati saṃkhyāyāḥ ātmā tāvat iha pratiṣṭhām pratyādhāra tvena nirdiṣṭaḥ yasmin  iti saptami sūcitasya aatam eva manya ātmānam iti ātma tvena anukarṣaṇāt  ātmā ca cetanaḥ puruṣaḥ sa ca pañcaviṃśatau  antargata eva iti na tasya eva ādhāra tvam ādheya tvam ca yujyate artha antara parigrahe ca tattva saṃkhyā atirekaḥ siddhānta viruddhaḥ prasajyeta tathā aākāśaḥ ca pratiṣṭhitaḥ iti ākāśasya api pañcaviṃśata vantargatasya na pṛthak upādānam nyāyyam artha antara parigrahe ca uktam dūṣaṇam katham ca saṃkhyā mātra śravaṇe satya śrutānām pañcaviṃśati tattvānām upasaṃgrahaḥ pratīyate jana śabdasya tatveṣu arūḍha tvāt  artha antara upasaṃgrahe api saṃkhyā upapatteḥ katham tarhi pañca pañcajanā iti ucyate iti viśeṣaṇa smaraṇāt saṃjñāyām eva pañca śabdasya jana śabdena samāsaḥ tatas ca rūḍha tva abhiprāyeṇa eva kecid pañcajanā nāma vivakṣyante na sāṃkhya tattva abhiprāyeṇa te kati iti asyām ākāṅkṣāyām punar  pañca iti prayujyate pañcajanā nāma ye kecid te ca pañca eva iti arthaḥ saptarṣayaḥ sapta iti yathā ke punar te pañcajanā nāma iti tad ucyate ayasmin apañca pañcajanāḥ iti ata uttarasmin mantre brahma svarūpa nirūpaṇāya prāṇa ādayaḥ pañca nirdiṣṭāḥ iti te atra vākya śeṣa gatāḥ saṃnidhānāt pañcajanā vivakṣyante katham punar  prāṇa ādiṣu jana śabda prayogaḥ tattveṣu vā katham jana śabda prayogaḥ samāne tu prasiddhi atikrame vākya śeṣa vaśāt prāṇa ādaya eva gpahītavyā bhavanti jana saṃbandhāt ca prāṇa ādayaḥ  jana śabda bhājaḥ  bhavanti jana vacanaḥ ca puruṣa śabdaḥ prāṇeṣu prayuktaḥ ate vā ete pañca brahma puruṣāḥ iti atra aprāṇaḥ  ha pitā prāṇaḥ  ha mātā ityādi ca brāhmaṇam samāsa balāt ca masudāyasya rūḍha tvam aviruddham katham punar asati prathamprayoge rūḍhiḥ śakya āśrayitum śakyā udbhidādivat iti āha prasiddha artha saṃnidhāne hi aprasiddhārthaḥ śabdaḥ prayujyamānaḥ samabhivyāhārāt tad viṣayaḥ  niyamyate yathā audbhidā yajeta ayūpam chinatti avedim karoti iti tathā ayam api pañcajana śabdaḥ samāsa anvā ākhyānāt avagata saṃjñā bhāvaḥ saṃjñya ākāṅkṣī vākya śeṣa samabhivyāhṛteṣu prāṇa ādiṣu vartiṣyate kaiścid tu devāḥ pitaraḥ  gandharvā asurā rakṣāṃsi ca pañca pañcajanā vyākhyātāḥ anyaiḥ ca catvāraḥ  varṇā niṣāda pañcamāḥ parigṛhītāḥ kvacid ca ayat pāñcajanyayā viśā iti prajā paraḥ prayogaḥ pañcajana śabdasya dṛśyate tad parigpahe api iha na kaścid varodhaḥ ācāryaḥ tu na pañca viśateḥ tad tvānam iha pratītiḥ asti iti evaṃpara tayā aprāṇāt ayaḥ  vāki śeṣāt iti jagāda bhaveyuḥ tāvat prāṇa ādayaḥ pañcajanā mādhyandinānām ye annam prāṇa ādiṣvāmananti kāṇvānām tu katham prāṇa ādayaḥ pañcajanā bhaveyuḥ ye annam prāṇa ādiṣu nāmananti iti ata uttaram paṭhati asatī api kāṇvānām anne jyotiṣā teṣām pañca saṃkhyā pūryeta te api hi ayasmin pañca pañcajanāḥ iti atas  pūrvasmin mantre brahma svarūpa nirūpaṇāya eva jyotiḥ adhīyate iti katham punar ubhayeṣām api tulyavat idam jyotiḥ paṭhyamānam samāna mantra gatayā pañca saṃkhyayā keṣāñcid grṛhyate keṣāñcinna iti apekṣā bhedāt iti āha mādhyandinānām hi samāna mantra paṭhita prāṇa ādi pañcajana lābhāt na asmin mantra antara paṭhite jyotiṣu apekṣā bhavati tad alābhāt tu kāṇvānām bhavati apekṣā apekṣā bhedāt ca samāne api mantre jyotiṣaḥ  grahaṇa agrahaṇe yathā samāne api atirātre vacana bhedāt ṣoḍaṣino grahaṇa agrahaṇe tadvat  tad evam na tāvat śruti prasiddhiḥ kācid pradhāna viṣaya asti smṛti nyāya prasiddhī tu parihariṣyete pratipāditam brahmaṇaḥ  lakṣaṇam pratipāditam ca brahma viṣayam gati sāmānyam vedānta vākyānām pratipāditam ca pradhānasya aśabda tvam tatra idam aparamāśaṅkate na janma ādi karaṇa tvam brahmaṇaḥ  brahma viṣayam vā gati sāmānyam vedānta vākyānām pratipattum śakyam kasmāt  vigāna darśanāt  prativeda antam hi anyā anyā sṛṣṭiḥ upalabhyate krama ādi vaicitryāt  tathā hi kvacid  aātmana ākāśaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ iti ākāśa ādika asṛṣṭarāmnāyate kvacid teja ādikā sṛjata iti kvacid prāṇa ādikā iti kvacid akrameṇa eva lokānām utpattiḥ āmnāyate sa imān  lokān asṛjata ambho marīcīḥ maramāpaḥ iti tathā kvacid asat pūrvikā sṛṣṭiḥ paṭhyate iti asat eva idam agra āsīt tad sadā āsīt tad samabhavat iti ca kvacid asat vāda nirākaraṇena sat pūrvikā prakriyā pratijñāyate iti upakramya akutaḥ tu khalu somya evam syāt iti ha uvāca katham asataḥ sat jāyeta iti sattvā iva somya idam agra āsīt iti kvacid svayaṅkartṛkā eva vyākriyā jagataḥ  nigadyate iti evam anekadhā vipratipattiḥ vastuni ca vikalpasya anupapatteḥ na vedānta vākyānām jagat kāraṇa avadhāraṇa para tā nyāyyā smṛti nyāya prasiddhāyām tu kāraṇa antara parigrahaḥ  nyāyya iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ sati api prativeda antam sṛjyamāneṣu ākāśa ādiṣu krama ādi dvārake vigāne na sraṣṭari kiñcid vigānam asti kutas  yathā vyapadiṣṭa ukteḥ yathābhūtaḥ  hi ekasmin veda ante sarvajñaḥ sarva īśvaraḥ sarva ātmā ekaḥ  advitīyaḥ kāraṇa tvena vyapadiṣṭaḥ tathābhūta eva vedānta antareṣu api vyapadiśyate tad yathā iti atra tāvat jñāna śabdena pareṇa ca tad viṣayeṇa kāmayitṛ tva vacanena cetanam brahma nya rūpayat apara prayojya tvena īśvaram kāraṇam abravīt  tad viṣayeṇa eva pareṇa ātma śabdena śarīra ādi kośa paraṃparayā ca antaranupraveśanena sarveṣām antar  pratyak ātmānam niradhārayat  abahu syā prajāyeya iti ca ātma viṣayeṇa bahu bhavana anuśaṃsanena sṛjyamānānām vikārāṇām sraṣṭuḥ abhedam abhāṣata tathā aidam sarvam asṛjata yad idam kiñca iti samasta jagat sṛṣṭi nirdeśena prākhsṛṣṭeḥ advitīyam sraṣṭāram ācaṣṭe tad atra yad lakṣaṇam brahma kāraṇa tvena vijñātam tad lakṣaṇam eva anyatra api vijñāyate atadaikṣata bahu syām prajāyeya iti tad tejaḥ  asṛjata iti tathā aātmā vā idam eka eva agra āsīt na anya kiñcana miṣat  sa īkṣata lokān nu sṛjai iti ca evan jātīyakasya kāraṇa svarūpa nirūpaṇa parasya vākya jātasya prativeda antam avigīta artha tvāt kārya viṣayam tu vigānam dṛśyate kvacid ākāśa ādikā sṛṣṭiḥ kvacid teja ādikā iti evan jātīyakam na ca kārya viṣayeṇa vigānena kāraṇam api brahma sarva vedānteṣu avigītam adhigamyamānam avivakṣitam bhavitum arhati iti śakyate vaktum atiprasaṅgāt  samādhasyati ca ācāryaḥ kārya viṣayam api vigānam ana viyat aśruteḥ iti ārabhya bhavet api kāryasya vigīta tvam apratipādya tvāt na hi ayam sṛṣṭi ādi prapañcaḥ pratipādayiṣitaḥ na hi tad pratibaddhaḥ kvacid puruṣa arthaḥ  dṛśyate śrūyate vā na ca kalpayitum śakyate upakrama upasaṃhārābhyām tatra tatra brahma viṣayaiḥ vākyaiḥ sākam eka vākyatāyāḥ  gamyamāna tvāt  darśayati ca sṛṣṭi ādi prapañcasya brahma pratipatti artha tām iti mṛd ādi dṛṣṭāntaiḥ ca kāryasya kāraṇena abhedam vaditum sṛṣṭi ādi prapañcaḥ śrāvyata iti gamyate tathā ca saṃpradāya vidaḥ  vadanti vatārāya na asti bhedaḥ kathañcana iti brahma pratipatti pratibaddham tu phalam śrūyate atarati śokam ātma vit atam eva viditvā atimṛtyum eti aa iti pratyakṣa avagamam ca idam phalam atattvam asi iti asaṃsārya ātma tva pratipattau satyām saṃsārya ātma tva vyāvṛtteḥ yad punar  kāraṇa viṣayam vigānam darśitam ityādi tad parihartavyam atra ucyate aasat vā idam agra āsīt iti na atra asat nirātmakam kāraṇa tvena śrāvyate yatas  aasan  eva sa bhavati asat brahma iti veda ced  asti brahma iti ced veda santam enam tatas  viduḥ iti asadvāda apavādena astitva lakṣaṇam brahma anna maya ādi kośa paramparayā pratyak ātmānam nirdhārya asaḥ  akāmayata iti tam eva prakṛtam samākṛṣya sa prapañcām sṛṣṭim tasmāt śrāvayitvā atat satyam iti ācakṣate iti ca upasaṃhṛtya atat api eṣa ślokaḥ  bhavati iti tasmin  eva prakṛter athe ślokam imam udāharati iti yadi tu asannirātmakam asmin śloke abhipreyeta tatas  anya samākarṣaṇe anyasya udāharaṇāt asaṃbaddham vākyam āpadyeta tasmāt nāma rūpa vyākṛta vastu viṣayaḥ prāyeṇa sat śabdaḥ prasiddha iti tad vyākaraṇa abhāva apekṣayā prāk utpatteḥ sat eva brahma asat ivāsīt iti upacaryate eṣā eva aasat eva idam agra āsīt iti atra api yojanā atat sadāsīt iti samākarṣaṇāt  atyanta abhāva abhyupagame hi tad sadā āsīt iti kim samākṛṣyeta ataddhā eka āhuḥ asat eva idam agra āsīt iti atra api na śruti antara abhiprāyeṇa ayam ekīyam ata upanyāsaḥ kriyāyām iva vastuni vikalpasya asaṃbhavāt tasmāt śruti parigṛhīta sat pakṣa dārḍhyāya eva ayam manda mati parikalpitasya asat pakṣasya upanyasya nirāsa iti draṣṭavyam atadhedam tarhi avyākṛtam āsīt iti atra api na niradhyakṣasya jagataḥ  vyākaraṇam kathyate asa eṣa iha praviṣṭa ānakha agrebhyaḥ iti adhyakṣasya vyākṛta kārya anupraveśi tvena samākarṣāt  niradhyakṣe vyākaraṇa abhyupagame hi anantareṇa prakṛta avalambanā sa iti anena sarva nāmnā kaḥ kārya anupraveśi tvena samākṛṣyeta cetanasya ca āyām ātmanaḥ śarīre anupraveśaḥ śrūyate praviṣṭasya cetana tva śravaṇāt  apaśyan  cakṣuḥ śṛṇvan śrotram manvānaḥ  manaḥ iti apica yādṛśam idamadya tve nāma rūpābhyām vyākriyamāṇam jagat sādhyakṣam vyākriyata evamādi sarge api iti gamyate dṛṣṭa viparīta kalpanā anupapatteḥ śruti antaram api aanena jīvena ātmanā anupraviśya nāma rūpe vyākaravāṇi iti sa adhi akṣām ā iva jagataḥ  vyākriyām darśayati vyākriyata iti api karma kartari lakāraḥ sati eva parameśvare vyākartari saukaryam apekṣya draṣṭavyaḥ yathā lūyate kedāraḥ svayam eva iti sati eva pūrṇake lavitari yad vā karmaṇi eva eṣa lakāror atha ākṣiptam kartāram apekṣya draṣṭavyaḥ yathā gamyate grāma iti kauṣītaki brāhmaṇe bāla ākya jāta śatru saṃvāde śrūyate iti tatra kim jīvaḥ  veditavya tvena upadiśyata uta mukhyaḥ prāṇa uta paramātmā iti viśayaḥ kim tāvat prāptam prāṇa iti kutas  ayasya vaitat karma iti śravaṇāt  parispanda lakṣaṇasya ca karmaṇaḥ prāṇa āśraya tvāt vākya śeṣe ca aatha asmin prāṇa eva ekadhā bhavati iti prāṇa śabda darśanāt  prāṇa śabdasya ca mukhye prāṇe prasiddha tvāt  ye ca ete purastāt dhālākinā aāditye puruṣaḥ candramasi puruṣaḥ iti evamādayaḥ puruṣā nirdiṣṭāḥ teṣām api bhavati prāṇaḥ kartā prāṇa avasthā viśeṣa tvāt ityādi devatā ātmanām akatama ekaḥ  deva iti prāṇa iti sa brahma tyat iti ācakṣate iti śruti antara prasiddheḥ jīvaḥ  vā ayam iha veditavyatayā upadiśyate tasya api dharma adharma lakṣaṇam karma śakyate śrāvayitum ayasya vaitat karma iti saḥ  api bhoktṛ tvāt bhoga upakaraṇa bhūtānām eteṣām puruṣāṇām kartā upapadyate vākya śeṣe ca jīva liṅgam avagamyate yad kāraṇam vedita vyatayā upanyastasya puruṣāṇām kartuḥ vedanāya upetam bālākim prati bubodhayiṣuḥ ajātaśatruḥ suptam puruṣam āmantrya āmantraṇa śabda aśravaṇāt prāṇa ādīnām abhoktṛ tvam pratibodhya yaṣṭi ghāta utthānāt prāṇa ādi vyatiriktam jīvam bhoktāram pratibodhayati tathā parastāt api jīva liṅgam avagamyate iti prāṇabhṛt tvāt ca jīvasya upapannam prāṇa śabda tvam tasmāt jīva mukhya prāṇayoḥ anyatara iha grahaṇīyaḥ  na parameśvaraḥ tad liṅga an avagamāt iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ parameśvara eva ayam eteṣām puruṣāṇām kartā syāt  kasmāt  upakrama sāmarthyāt  iha hi bālākirajātaśatruṇā saha abrahma te bravāṇi iti saṃvaditum upacakrame sa ca katicid ādityādi adhikaraṇān puruṣānamukhya brahma dṛṣṭi bhāja uktvā tūṣṇīm babhūva tam ajātaśatruḥ amṛṣā vai khalu mā saṃvadiṣṭā brahma te bravāṇi iti amukhya brahma vāditayā apodya tad kartāram anyam veditavyatayā upacikṣepa yadi saḥ  api amukhya brahma dṛṣṭi bhāj  syāt upakramaḥ  bādhyeta tasmāt parameśvara eva ayam bhavitum arhati kartṛ tvam ca eteṣām puruṣāṇām na parameśvarāt anyasya svātantryeṇa avakalpate ayasya vaitat karma iti api na ayam parispanda lakṣaṇasya dharma adharma lakṣaṇasya vā karmaṇaḥ  nirdeśaḥ tayoḥ anyatarasya api aprakṛta tvāt  asaṃśabdita tvāt ca na api puruṣāṇām ayam nirdeśaḥ eteṣām puruṣāṇām kartā iti eva teṣām nirdiṣṭa tvāt  liṅga vacana vigānāt ca na api puruṣa viṣayasya karoti arthasya kriyā phalasya vāyam nirdeśaḥ kartṛ śabdena eva tayoḥ apapātta tvāt pāriśeṣyāt pratyakṣa saṃnihitam jagat sarva nāmnā etad śabdena nirdiśyate kriyata iti ca tadā eva jagatkarma nanu jagat api aprakṛtam asaṃśabditam ca satyam etad  tathā api asati viśeṣa upādāne sādhāraṇena arthena saṃnidhānena saṃnihita vastu mātrasya ayam nirdeśa iti gamyate na viśiṣṭasya kasyacid  viśeṣa saṃnidhāna abhāvāt pūrvatra ca jagat eka deśa bhūtānām puruṣāṇām viśeṣa upādāna da viśeṣitam jagat eva iha upādīyata iti gamyate etad uktam bhavati ya eteṣām puruṣāṇām jagat eka deśa bhūtānām kartā kim anena viśeṣeṇa yasya kṛtsnam eva jagat aviśeṣitam karma iti vā śabda eka deśa avacchinna kartṛ tva vyāvṛtti arthaḥ ye bālākinā brahma tva abhimatāḥ puruṣāḥ kīrtitāḥ teṣām abrahma tva khyāpanāya viśeṣa upādānam evam brāhmaṇa parivrājaka nyāyena sāmānya viśeṣābhyām jagataḥ kartā veditavyatayā upadiśyate parameśvaraḥ ca sarva jagataḥ kartā sarva vedānteṣu avadhāritaḥ ata yad uktam vākya śeṣa gatāt jīva liṅgān mukhya prāṇa liṅgāt ca tayoḥ eva anyatarasya iha grahaṇam nyāyyam na parameśvarasya iti tad parihartavyam yatra ucyate parihṛtam ca etad  anopāsa atraividhyāt āśrita tvāt iha tad yogāt iti atra trividham hi atra upāsanam evam sati prasajjyeta jīva upāsanam mukhya prāṇa upāsanam brahma upāsanam ca iti na ca etad nyāyyam upakrama upasaṃhārābhyām hi brahviṣaya tvam asya vākyasya avagamyate tatra upakramasya tāvat brahma viṣaya tvam darśitam upasaṃhārasya api niratiśaya phala śravaṇāt brahma viṣaya tvam dṛśyate pahṛtya sarveṣām ca bhūtānām śraiṣṭhyam svārājyam ādhipatyam paryeti ya evam veda iti nanu evam sati pratardana vākya nirṇayena eva idam api vākyam nirṇīyeta na nirṇīyate ayasya ca etad karma iti asya brahma viṣaya tvena tatra anirdhārita tvāt tasmāt atra jīva mukhya prāṇa śaṅkā punar utpadyamānā nirvartyate prāṇa śabdaḥ  api brahma viṣayaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ aprāṇa bandhanam hi somya manaḥ iti atra jīliṅgam api upakrama upasaṃhārayoḥ brahma viṣaya tvāt abheda abhiprāyeṇa yojayitavyam apica na eva atra vivaditavyam jīva pradhānam vedam vākyam syāt brahma pradhānam vā iti yatas  anya artham jīva parāmarśam brahma pratipatti artham asmin vākye jaiminiḥ ācāryaḥ  manyante kasmāt  praśna vyākhyānābhyām praśnaḥ tāvat suṣupta puruṣa pratibodhanena prāṇa ādi vyatirikte jīve pratibodhite punar jīva vyatirikta viṣayaḥ  dṛśyate śayiṣṭa kva vā etad abhūt kuta etad āgāt iti prativacanam api ayadā suptaḥ svapnam na kañcana paśyati atha asmin prāṇa eva ekadhā bhavati ityādi aetasmāt ātmanaḥ prāṇā yathā āyatanam vipratiṣṭhante prāṇebhyaḥ  devāḥ  devebhyaḥ  lokāḥ iti ca suṣupti kāle ca pareṇa brahmaṇā jīva ekatām gacchati parasmāt ca brahmaṇaḥ prāṇa ādikam jagat jāyata iti vedānta maryādā tasmāt yatra asya jīvasya niḥsaṃbodha tā svacchata arūpaḥ svāpa upādhi janita viśeṣa vijñāna rahitam svarūpam yatas tad haṃśa rūpam āgamanam saḥ  atra paramātmā veditavyatayā śrāvita iti gamyate api cā evam eke śākhinaḥ  vājasaneyino asmin  eva bāla ākya jāta śatru saṃvāde spaṣṭam vijñāna maya śabdena jīvam āmnāya tad vyatiriktam paramātmānam āmananti iti praśne prativacane api aya eṣaḥ  antar hṛdaya ākāśaḥ tasmin śete iti ākāśa śabdaḥ ca parama ātmani prayuktaḥ adaharaḥ  asmin  antara ākāśaḥ iti atra asarva eta ātmanaḥ  vyuccaranti iti ca upādhimatām ātmanām anyato vyuccaraṇamām anantaḥ paramātmānam eva kāraṇa tvena āmananti iti gamyate prāṇa nara akaraṇasya api suṣupta puruṣa utthāpanena prāṇa ādi vyatirikta upadeśaḥ  abhyuccayaḥ bṛhadāraṇyake maitreyī brāhmaṇe adhīyate iti upakramya ana vā are sarvasya kāmāya sarvam priyam bhavati ātmanaḥ tu kāmāya sarvam priyam bhavati ātmā vā are draṣṭavyaḥ śrotavyaḥ  mantavyaḥ  nididhya asitavyaḥ  maitreyī ātmanaḥ  vā are darśanena śravaṇena matyā vijñānena idam sarvam viditam iti tatra etad vicikitsyate kim vijñāna ātmā eva ayam draṣṭavya śrotavya tva ādi rūpeṇa upadiśyata āhosvit paramātmā iti kutas  punar eṣā vicikitsā priya saṃsūcitena ātmanā bhoka tra upakramāt vijñāna tma upadeśa iti kim tāvat prāptam vijñāna ātmā upadeśa iti kasmāt  upakrama sāmarthyāt  pati jāyā putra vitta ādikam hi bhogya bhūtam sarvam jagat ātma artha tayā priyam bhavati iti priya saṃsūcitam bhoktāram ātmānam ukramya anantaram idam ātmanaḥ  darśana ādi upadiśyamānam kasya anyasya ātmanaḥ syāt  madhye api aidam mahat bhūtam anantam apāram vijñāna ghana eva etebhyaḥ  bhūtebhyaḥ samutthāya tāni eva anuvinaśyati na pretya saṃjñā asti iti prakṛtasya eva mahataḥ  bhūtasya draṣṭavyasya bhūtebhyaḥ samutthānam vijñāna ātma bhāvena bruvan vijñāna ātmanam eva idam draṣṭavya tvam darśayati tathā avijñāta āram are kena vijānīyāt iti kartṛ vacanena śabdena upasaṃharan vijñāna ātmānam eva iha upadiṣṭam darśayati tasmāt ātma vijñānena sarva vijñānam bhoktṛ artha tvāt bhogya jātasya aupacārikam draṣṭavyam iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ paramātma upadeśa eva ayam kasmāt  vākya anvayāt vākyam hi idam paurvāparyeṇa avekṣyamāṇam paramātmā anaṃprati anvita avayavam lakṣyate katham iti tad upapādyate iti yājñavalkyāt upaśrutya ayena aham na amṛtā syām kim aham tena kuryām yad eva bhagavān veda tad eva me brūhi iti amṛta tvam āśāsānāya maitreyyā yājñavalkya ātma vijñānam idam upadiśati naca anyatra parama ātma vijñānāt am ṛtvam asti iti śruti smṛti vādā vadanti tathā ca ātma vijñānena sarva vijñānam ucyamānam na anyatra parama kāraṇa vijñānāt mukhyam avakalpate naca etad aupacārikam āśrayitum śakyam yad kāraṇam ātma vijñānena sarva vijñānam pratijñāya anantareṇa granthena tad eva upapādayati nyatra ātmanaḥ  brahma veda ityādinā yaḥ  hi brahma kṣatra ādikam jagat ātmanā ūnyatra svātantryeṇa labdha sadbhāvam paśyati tam mithyā darśinam tad eva mithyā dṛṣṭam brahma kṣatra ādikam jagatparākaroti iti bheda dṛṣṭim apodya aidam sarvam yad ayam ātmā iti sarvasya vastu jātasya ātma avyatirekam avatārayati dundubhi ādi dṛṣṭāntaiḥ ca tam eva avyatirekam draḍhayati aasya mahataḥ  bhūtasya niḥśvasitam etad yadṛgvedaḥ ityādinā ca prakṛtasya ātmanaḥ  nāma rūpa karma prapañca kāraṇa tām vyācakṣāṇaḥ paramātmānam enam gamayati tathā eva ekāyana prakriyāyām api sa viṣayasya sa indriyasya sa antaḥkaraṇasya prapañcasya ekāyanam anantaram abāhyam kṛtsnam prajñāna ghanam vyācakṣāṇaḥ paramātmānam enam gamayati tasmāt paramātmana eva ayam darśana ādi upadeśa iti gamyate yad punaruktam priya saṃsūcita upakramāt vijñāna ātmana eva ayam darśana ādi upadeśa iti atra brūmaḥ asti atra pratijñā aātmani vijñāte sarvam idam vijñātam bhavati aidam sarvam yad ayam ātmā iti ca tasyāḥ pratijñāyāḥ siddhim sūcayati etad liṅgam yad priya saṃsūcitasya ātmanaḥ  draṣṭavya tva ādi saṃkīrtanam yadi hi vijñāna ātmā paramātmanaḥ  anyaḥ syāt tatas  paramātma vijñāne api vijñāna ātmā na vijñāta iti eka vijñānena sarva vijñānam yad pratijñātam tad hīyeta tasmāt pratijñā siddhi artham vijñāna ātma parama ātmanā urabheda aṃśena upakramaṇam iti āśmarathya ācāryaḥ  manyate utkramiṣyata evam bhāvāt  iti  auḍulomiḥ vijñāna ātmana eva deha indriya manaḥ buddhi saṃghāta upādhi saṃparkāt kaluṣībhūtasya jñāna dhyāna ādi sādhana anuṣṭhāna asaṃprasannasya deha ādi saṃghātāt utkramiṣyataḥ paramātma aikya upapatteḥ idam abhedena upakramaṇam iti auḍulomiḥ ācāryaḥ  manyate śrutiḥ ca evam bhavati smāt śarīrāt samutthāya param jyotiḥ upasaṃpadya svena rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyate iti kvacid ca jīva āśrayam api nāma rūpam nadī nidarśanena jñāpayati stam gacchanti nāma rūpe vihāya tathā vidvān nāma rūpāt vimuktaḥ parāt param puruṣam upaiti divyam iti yathā loke nadyaḥ sva āśrayam eva nāma rūpam vihāya samudram upayanti evam jīvaḥ  api sva āśrayam eva nāma rūpam vihāya param puruṣam upaiti iti hi tatra arthaḥ pratīyate dṛṣṭānta dārṣṭa antikayoḥ tulya tāyai asya eva paramātmanaḥ  anena api vijñāna ātma bhāvena avasthānāt upapannam idam abhedena upakramaṇam iti kāśa kṛt sna ācāryaḥ  manyate tathā ca brāhmaṇam iti evan jātīyakam parasya eva ātmanaḥ  jīva bhāvena avasthānam darśayati mantra varṇaḥ ca nyasta dvi kāraḥ  jīvaḥ syāt  kāśa kṛt snasya ācāryasya avikṛtaḥ parameśvaraḥ  jīvaḥ  na anya iti matam āśmarathyasya tu yadi api jīvasya parasmāt ananya tvam abhipretam tathā api pratijñā siddheḥ iti sa apekṣa tva abhidhānāt kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ kiyān api abhipreta iti gamyate auḍulomi pakṣe punar  spaṣṭam eva avasthā antara apekṣau bheda abhedau gamyete tatra kāśa kṛt snīyam matam śruti anusārī iti gamyate pratipādayiṣita artha anusārāt  atattvam asi ityādi śrutibhyaḥ evañca sati tad jñānāt amṛta tvam avakalpate vikāra ātmaka tve hi jīvasya abhyupagamyamāne vikārasya prakṛti saṃbandhe pralaya prasaṅgāt na tad jñānāt amṛtam avakalpeta atas ca sva āśrayasya nāma rūpasya asaṃbhavāt upādhi āśrayam nāma rūpam jīva upacaryate ata eva utpattiḥ api jīvasya kvacid agni visphuliṅga udāharaṇena śrāvyamāṇa upādhi āśrayā eva veditavyā yad api uktam prakṛtasya eva mahataḥ  bhūtasya draṣṭavyasya bhūtebhyaḥ samutthānam vijñāna ātma bhāvena darśayan vijñāna ātmana eva idam draṣṭavya tvam darśayati iti tatra apiyam eva trisūtrī yojayitavyā apratijñā siddheḥ liṅgam āśmarathyaḥ idam atra pratijñātam aidam sarvam yad ayam ātmā iti ca upapāditam ca sarvasya nāma rūpa karma prapañcasya eka prasava tvāt eka pralaya tvāt ca dundubhi ādi dṛṣṭāntaiḥ ca kārya kāraṇayoḥ avyatireka pratipādanāt  tasyāḥ  eva pratijñāyāḥ siddhim sūcati etad liṅgam yad mahataḥ  bhūtasya draṣṭavyasya bhūtebhyaḥ samutthānam vijñāna ātma bhāvena kathitam iti āśmarathya ācāryaḥ  manyate abhede hi sati eka vijñānena sarva vijñānam pratijñātam avakalpayata iti autkramiṣyata evaṃbhāvāt iti auḍu lomiḥ utkramiṣyataḥ  vijñāna ātmanaḥ  jñāna dhyāna ādi sāmarthyāt saṃprasannasya pareṇa ātmanā aikya saṃbhava ādi dama bheda abhidhānam iti auḍulomiḥ ācāryaḥ  manyate aavasthiteḥ iti kāśa kṛtsnaḥ asya eva paramātmanaḥ  anena api vijñāna ātma bhāvena avasthānāt upapannam idam abheda abhidhānam iti kāśa kṛt sna ācāryaḥ  manyate nanu uccheda abhidhānam etad  aetebhyaḥ  bhūtebhyaḥ samutthāya tāni eva anuvinaśyati na pretya saṃjñā asti iti kathameda bheda abhidhānam na eṣa doṣaḥ viśeṣa vijñāna vināśa abhiprāyam etad vināśa abhidhānam na ātma uccheda abhiprāyam aatra eva mā bhagavān amūmuhanna pretya saṃjñā asti iti paryanuyujya svayam eva śrutyā artha antarasya darśita tvāt  ham moham bravīmi avināśī vā are ayam ātma anucchitti dharmā mātrā saṃsargaḥ tu asya bhavati iti etad uktam bhavati kūṭastha nitya eva ayam vijñāna ghana ātmā na asya uccheda prasaṅgaḥ  asti mātrābhiḥ tu asya bhūta indriya lakṣaṇābhiḥ avidyā kṛtābhiḥ asaṃsargaḥ  vidyayā bhavati saṃsarga abhāve ca prakṛtasya viśeṣa vijñānasya abhāvāt na pretya saṃjñā asti iti uktam iti yad api uktam iti kartṛ vacanena śabdena upasaṃhārāt vijñāna ātmana eva idam draṣṭavyam iti tad api kāśa kṛt snīyena eva darśanena parihapaṇīyam apica ayatra hi dvaitam iva bhavati tad itara itaram paśyati iti ārabhya avidyā viṣaye tasya eva darśana ādi lakṣaṇam viśeṣa jñānam prapañcya ayatra tu asya sarvām ātmā eva abhūt tad kena kam paśyet ityādinā vidyā viṣaye tasya eva darśana ādi lakṣaṇasya viśeṣa vijñānasya abhāvam abhidadhāti punar ca viṣaya abhāve api ātmānam vijānīyāt  iti āśaṅkya avijñāta āram are kena vijānīyāt iti āha tatas ca viśeṣa vijñāna abhāva upapādāna para tvāt vākyasya vijñāna dhātuḥ eva kevalaḥ saṃnbhūta pūrva gatyā kartṛ vacanena tṛcā nirdiṣṭa iti gamyate darśitam tu purastāt kāśa kṛt snīyasya pakṣasya śrutimat tvam atas ca vijñānāt paramātmanoḥ avidyā pratyupasthāpita nāma rūpa racita deha ādi upādhi nim itto bhedaḥ  na pāramārthika iti eṣor athaḥ sarvaiḥ vedāntava ādibhiḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ asat eva somya idam agra āsīt ekam eva advitīyam aātmā evedam sarvam brahma eva idam sarvam aidam sarvam yad ayam ātmā anānyaḥ  atas  asti draṣṭā anān yadatas  asti draṣṭṛ iti evaṃrūpābhyaḥ śrutibhyaḥ smṛtibhyaḥ ca avāsudevaḥ sarvam iti akṣetra jñam ca api mām viddhi sarva kṣetreṣu bhārata asamam sarveṣu bhūteṣu tiṣṭhantam parameśvaram iti evaṃrūpābhyaḥ bheda darśana apavādāt ca aanyaḥ  asau  anyaḥ  aham asmi iti na sa veda yathā paśuḥ amṛtyoḥ sa mṛtyum āpnoti ca iha na anā iva paśyati iti evan jātīyakāt  asa vā eṣa mahān aja ātma ajaraḥ  amaraḥ  amṛtaḥ  abhayaḥ  brahma iti ca ātmani sarva vikriyā pratiṣedhāt anyathā ca mumukṣūṇām nirapavāda vijñāna anupapatteḥ su niścita artha tva anupapatteḥ ca nirapavādam hi vijñānam sarva ākāṅkṣā nivartakam ātma viṣayam iṣyate avedānta vijñāna su nuḥ cita arthāḥ iti ca śruteḥ atatra kaḥ  mohaḥ kaḥ śoka eka tvam anupaśyataḥ iti ca śthita prajña lakṣaṇa smṛteḥ ca sthite ca kṣetrajña parama ātmā ekatva viṣaya samyak darśane kṣetrajñaḥ paramātmā iti nāma mātra bhaidāt  kṣetrajñaḥ  ayam paramātmanaḥ  bhinnaḥ paramātmā ayam kṣetrajñāt bhinna iti evan jātīyaka ātma bhaida viṣayaḥ  nirbandhaḥ  nirarthakaḥ ekaḥ  hi ayam ātmā nāma mātra bhedena bahudhā abhidhīyata iti na hi asatyam jñānam antam brahma yaḥ  veda nihitam guhāyām iti kāñcid eva ekām guhām adhikṛtya etad uktam na ca brahmaṇaḥ  anyaḥ  guhāyām nihitaḥ  asti atat sṛṣṭvā tad eva anuprāviśat iti sraṣṭuḥ eva praveśa śravaṇāt  ye tu nirbandham kurvanti te vedānta artham bādhamānāḥ śreyaḥ dvāram samyak darśanam eva bādhante kṛtakam anityam ca mokṣam kalpayanti nyāyena ca na saṃgacchanta iti yathā abhyudaya hetutvāt dharmaḥ  jijñāsya evam niḥśreyasa hetu tvāt brahma jijñāsyam iti uktam brahma ca ajanmādyasya yataḥ iti lakṣitam tad ca lakṣaṇam ghaṭa rucaka ādīnām mṛd suvarṇa ādivat prakṛti tve kulāla suvarṇakāra ādivat nimitta tve ca samānam iti atas  bhavati vimarśaḥ kimātmakam punar brahmaṇaḥ kāraṇa tvam syāt iti tatra nimitta kāraṇam eva tāvat kevalam syāt iti pratibhāti kasmāt  īkṣā pūrvaka kartṛ tva śravaṇāt īkṣā pūrvakam hi brahmaṇaḥ kartṛ tvam avagamyate asa prāṇam asṛjata iti adiśrutibhyaḥ īkṣā pūrvakam ca kartṛ tvam nimitta kāraṇeṣu eva kulāla ādiṣu dṛṣṭam aneka kāraka pūrvikā ca kriyā phala siddhiḥ loke dṛṣṭā sa ca nyāya ādikartari api yuktaḥ saṃkramayitum īśvara tva prasiddheḥ ca īśvarāṇām hi rāja vaivasvata ādīnām nimitta kāraṇa tvam eva kevalam pratīyate tadvat parameśvarasya api nimitta kāraṇa tvam eva yuktam pratipattum kāryam ca idam jagat sāvayavam acetanam aśuddham ca dṛśyate kāraṇena api tasya tādṛśena eva bhavitavyam kārya kāraṇayoḥ sārūpya darśanāt brahma ca na evaṃlakṣaṇam avagamyate aniṣkalam niṣkriyam śāntam niravadyam nirañjanam ityādi śrutibhyaḥ pāriśeṣyāt brahmaṇaḥ  anyat upādāna kāraṇam aśuddhi ādi guṇakam smṛti prasiddham abhyupagantavyam brahma kāraṇa tva śruteḥ nimitta tva mātre paryavasānāt iti evam prāpte brūmaḥ prakṛtiḥ ca upādāna kāraṇam ca brahma abhyupagantavyam nimitta kāraṇam ca na kevalam nimitta kāraṇam eva kasmāt  pratijñā dṛṣṭānta an uparodhāt evam pratijñā dṛṣṭāntau śrautau na uparudhyete pratijñā tāvat  iti tatra ca ekena vijñātena sarva manda vijñātam api vijñātam bhavati iti pratīyate tad ca upādāna kāraṇa vijñāne sarva vijñānam saṃbhavati upādāna kāraṇa vyatirekāt kāryasya nimitta kāraṇā vyatirekāḥ tu kāryasya na asti loke takṣṇaḥ prāsāda vyatireka darśanāt  dṛṣṭāntaḥ  api yathā asomya ekena mṛd piṇḍena sarvam mṛd mayam vijñātam syāt vācā ārambhaṇam vikāraḥ  nāmadheyam mṛttikā iti eva satyam iti upādānakāraṇa gocara evam āmnāyate tathā aekena loha maṇinā sarvam loha mayam vijñātam syāt aekena nakha nikṛntanena sarvam kārṣṇāyasam vijñātam syāt iti ca tathā anyatra api akasmin  u bhagavaḥ  vijñāte sarvam idam vijñātam bhavati iti pratijñā ayathā pṛthivyām oṣadhayaḥ saṃbhavanti iti dṛṣṭāntaḥ tathā aātmani kalvare dṛṣṭe śrute mate vijñāta idam sarvam viditam iti pratijñā asa yathā dundubheḥ hanyamānasya na bāhyān śabdān śaknuyāt grahaṇāya dundubheḥ tu grahaṇena dundubhi āghātasya vā śabdaḥ  gṛhītaḥ iti dṛṣṭāntaḥ evam yathāsaṃbhavam prativeda antam pratijñā dṛṣṭāntau prakṛti tva sādhanau pratyetavyau yata iti iyam pañcamī ayataḥ  vā imāni bhūtāni jāyante iti atra ajanikartuḥ prakṛtiḥ iti viśeṣa smaraṇāt prakṛti lakṣaṇa eva apādāne draṣṭavyā nimitta tvam tu adhiṣṭhā trantara abhāvāt adhigantavyam yathā hi loke mṛd suvarṇa ādikam upādāna kāraṇam kulāla suvarṇakāra ādīn adhiṣṭhātṛ napekṣya pravartate na evam brahmaṇa upādānakāraṇasya sataḥ  anyaḥ  adhiṣṭhāta apekṣyaḥ  asti prāk utpatteḥ ekam eva advitīyam iti avadhāraṇāt adhiṣṭhātṛ antara abhāvaḥ  api pratijñā dṛṣṭānta anuparodhāt eva uditaḥ  veditavyaḥ adhiṣṭhātari hi upādānāt anyasmin  abhyupagamyamāne punar api eka vijñānena sarva vijñānasya asaṃbhavāt pratijñā dṛṣṭānta uparodha eva syāt  tasmāt adhiṣṭhātṛ antara abhāvāt ātmanaḥ kartṛ tvam upādāna antara abhāvāt ca prakṛti tvam kutas ca ātmanaḥ kartṛ tva prakṛti tve abhidhyā upadeśaḥ ca ātmanaḥ kartṛ tva prakṛti tve gamayati asaḥ  akāmayata bahu syām prajāyeya iti atadaikṣata bahu syām prajāyeya iti ca tatra abhidhyāna pūrvikāyāḥ svātantrya pravṛtteḥ kartā iti gamyate bahu syām iti pratyagātma viṣaya tvāt bahu bhavana abhidhyānasyaprakṛtiḥ iti api gamyate prakṛti tvasya ayam abhyuccayaḥ itas ca prakṛtiḥ brahma yad kāraṇam sākṣāt brahmā eva kāraṇam upādāya ubhau prabhava pralayauvāmnāyate iti yad hi yasmāt prabhavati yasmin  ca pralīyate tad tasya upādānam prasiddham yathā vrīhi yava ādīnām pṛthivī sākṣāt ite sākṣāt iti ca upādāna antara anupādānam darśayati ākāśāt eva iti pratyasta mayaḥ ca na upādānāt anyatra kāryasya dṛṣṭaḥ itas ca prakṛtiḥ brahma yad kāraṇam brahma prakriyāyām atadātmānam svayam akuruta iti ātmanaḥ karma tvam kartṛ tvam ta darśayati ātmānam iti karma tvam svayam akurutā iti kartṛ tvam katham punar  pūrva siddhasya sataḥ kartṛ tvena vyavasthitasya kriyamāṇa tvam śakyam saṃpādayitum pariṇāmāt iti brūmaḥ pūrva siddhaḥ  api hi san  ātmā viśeṣeṇa vikāra ātmanā pariṇamayāmāsa ātmānam iti vikāra ātmanā ca pariṇāmaḥ  mṛdā ādyāsu prakṛtiṣu upalabdhaḥ svayam iti ca viśeṣaṇāt nimitta antara anapekṣa tvam api pratīyate pariṇāmāt iti vā pṛthak sūtram tasya eṣor athaḥ itas ca prakṛtiḥ brahma yad kāraṇam brahmaṇa eva vikāra ātmanā pariṇāmaḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyena āmnāyate asat ca tyat ca abhavat niruktam ca aniruktam ca ityādinā iti itas ca prakṛtiḥ brahma yoniḥ iti api paṭhyate vedānteṣu akartāram īśam puruṣam brahma yonim iti ayat bhūta yoni paripaśyanti dhīrāḥ iti ca yoni śabdaḥ ca prakṛti vacanaḥ samadhigataḥ  loke apṛthivī yoniḥ oṣadhi vanaspatīnām iti strī yoneḥ api asti eva ayavat vāreṇa garbham pratyupādāna kāraṇa tvam kacid sthāna vacanaḥ  api yoni śabdaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ iti vāki aśeṣāt tu atra prakṛti vacana tā parigṛhyate ayathā ūrṇanābhiḥ sṛjate gṛhyate ca iti evan jātīyakāt  evam prakṛti tvam brahmaṇaḥ prasiddham yad punar idam uktam īkṣā pūrvakam kartṛ tvam nimitta kāraṇeṣu eva kulāla ādiṣu loke dṛṣṭam na upādāneṣu ityādi tad pratyucyate na lokavat iha bhavitavyam na hi ayam anumāna gamyor athaḥ śabda gamya tvāt tvasya arthasya yathāśabdam iha bhavitavyam śabdaḥ ca īkṣituḥ īśvarasya prakṛti tvam pratidayatā atyavocāma punar ca etad sarvam vistareṇa prativakṣyāmaḥ aīkṣateḥ na aśabdam iti ārabhya pradhāna kāraṇa vādaḥ sūtraiḥ eva punar  punar āśaṅkya nirākṛtaḥ tasya hi pakṣasya upodbalakāni kānicid liṅga ābhāsāni vedānteṣu āpātena mandam atīn pratibhānti iti sa ca kārya kāraṇa nanya tva abhyupagamāt pratyāsannaḥ  vedānta vādasya devala prabhṛtibhiḥ ca kaiścid dharma sūtra kāraiḥ sva grantheṣu āśritaḥ tena tad pratiṣedhe yatnaḥ  atīva kṛtaḥ  na aṇvādi kāraṇa vāda pratiṣedhe te api tu brahma kāraṇa vāda pakṣasya pratipakṣa tvāt pratiṣeddhavyāḥ teṣām api upodvalakam vaidikam kiñcid liṅgam āpātena mandam atīn prati bhāyāt iti atas  pradhāna malla nibarhaṇa nyāyena atidiśati etena pradhāna kāraṇa vāda pratiṣedha nyāya kalāpena sarve aṇvādi kāraṇa vādā api pratiṣiddha tayā vyākhyātā veditavyāḥ teṣām api pradhānavat aśabda tvāt śabda virodhi tvāt ca iti vyākhyātā vyākhyātā iti pada abhyāsaḥ  adhyāya parisamāptim dyotayati iti smṛti adhikaraṇam sū prathame adhyāye sarvajñaḥ sarva īśvaraḥ jagata utpatti kāraṇam mṛd suvarṇa ādaya iva ghaṭa rucaka ādīnām utpannasya jagataḥ  niyantṛ tvena stithi kāraṇam māyā avī iva māyāyāḥ prasāritasya ca jagataḥ punar  sva ātmani eva upasaṃhāra kāraṇam avaniḥ iva caturvidhasya bhūta grāmasya sa eva ca sarveṣām na ātmā iti etad vedānta vākya samanvaya pratipādanena pratipāditam pradhāna ādi kāraṇa vādāḥ ca aśabda tvena nirākṛtāḥ idānīm sva pakṣe smṛti nyāya virodha parihāraḥ pradhāna ādi vādānām ca nyāya abhāsa upabṛṃhita tvam prativeda antam ca sṛṣṭi ādi prakriyāyāḥ  avigīta tvam isi artha jātasya pratipādanāya dvitīyaḥ  adhyāya ārabhyate tatra prathamam tāvat smṛti virodham upanyasya pariharati yad uktam brahmā eva sarvajñam jagataḥ kāraṇam iti tad ayuktam kutas  smṛti anavakāśa doṣa prasaṅgāt  smṛtiḥ ca tantra ākhyā parama ṛṣi praṇītā śiṣṭa parigṛhītā anyāḥ ca tad anusīriṇyaḥ smṛtayaḥ evam satya nava ākāśāḥ prasajyeran tāsu hi acetanam pradhānam svatantram jagataḥ kāraṇam upanibadhyate manu ādi samṛtayaḥ tāvat codanā lakṣaṇena agnihotra ādinā dharma jātena apekṣitam artham samarpayanti aḥsa avakāśā bhavanti asya varṇasya asmin kāle anena vidhānaṃna upanayanam īdṛśaḥ ca ācāraḥ ittham veda adhyayanam ittham sahadharma cāriṇī saṃyoga iti tathā puruṣa arthāḥ ca varṇa āśrama dharmān nānāvidhān vidadhati na evam kapila ādi smṛtīnām anuṣṭheye viṣaye avakāśaḥ  asti mokṣa sādhanam eva hi samyak darśanam adhikṛtya tāḥ praṇītāḥ yadi tatra api anavakāśāḥ syuḥ ānarthakyam eva āsām prasajyeta tasmāt tad avirodhena vedāntā vyākhyātavyāḥ katham punar īkṣati ādibhyaḥ  hetubhyaḥ  brahmā eva sarvajñam jagataḥ kāraṇam iti avadhāritaḥ śruti arthaḥ smṛti anavakāśa doṣa prasaṅgena punar ākṣipyate bhava deyam anākṣepaḥ svatantra prajñānām paratantra prajñāḥ tu prāyeṇa janāḥ svātantryeṇa śruti artham avadhārayitum aśaknuvantaḥ prakhyāta praṇetṛkāsu smṛtiṣu avalamberan tad balena ca śruti artham pratipitseran asmad kṛte ca vyākhyāne na viśvasyuḥ bahu mānāt smṛtīnām praṇetṛṣu kapila prabhṛtīnām cārṣam jñānam apratihatam smaryate śrutiḥ ca bhavati iti tasmāt na eṣām matam ayathārtham śakyam saṃbhāvayitum tarka  aṣṭambhena ca eter atham pratiṣṭhāpayanti tasmāt api smṛti balena vedāntā vyākhyeyā iti punar ākṣepaḥ tasya samādhiḥ na anya smṛti anavakāśa doṣa prasaṅgāt iti yadi smṛti anavakāśa doṣa prasaṅgena īśvara kāraṇa vāda ākṣipyeta evam api anyā īśvara kāraṇa vādinyaḥ smṛtayo anavakāśāḥ prasajyeran tā udāhariṣyāmaḥ iti param brahma prakṛtya asa hi antarātmā bhūtānām kṣetrajñaḥ ca iti kathyate iti ca uktvā atasmāt avyaktam utpannam triguṇam dvijasattama iti āha tathā anyatra api aavyaktam puruṣe brahman nirguṇe saṃpralīyate iti āha aatas ca saṃkṣepam imam śṛṇudhvam nārāyaṇaḥ sarvam idam purāṇaḥ sa sarga kāle ca karoti sarvam saṃhāra kāle ca tadatti bhūyaḥ iti purāṇe bhagavadgītāsu ca iti paramātmānam eva ca prakṛti ā apaḥ tam abaḥ paṭhati yam anya smṛti anavakāśa doṣa upanyāsaḥ darśitam tu śrutīnām īśvara kāraṇa vādam prati tātparyam vipratipattau ca smṛtīnām avaśya kartavye anyatara parigrahe anyatara parityāge ca śruti anusāriṇyaḥ smṛtayaḥ pramāṇam anapekṣyā itarāḥ tad uktam pramāṇa lakṣaṇe iti na ca atīndriya anarthan śrutim antareṇa kaścid upalabhata iti śakyam saṃbhāvayitum nimitta abhāvāt śakyam kapila ādīnām siddhānām apratihata jñāna tvāt iti ced  na siddheḥ api sa apekṣa tvāt  dharma anuṣṭhāna apekṣā hi siddhiḥ sa ca dharmaḥ codanā lakṣaṇaḥ tatas ca pūrva siddhāyāḥ codanāyāḥ  arthaḥ  na paścima siddha puruṣa vacana vaśena atiśaṅkitum śakyate siddha vyapāśraya kalpanāyām api bahu tvāt siddhānām pradraśitena prakāreṇa smṛti vipratipattau satyām na śruti vyapāśrayāt anyat nirṇaya kāraṇam asti paratantra prajñasya api na akasmāt smṛti viśeṣa viṣayaḥ pakṣapātaḥ  yuktaḥ kasyacid kvacid pakṣapāte sati puruṣam ativauśvarūpyeṇa tattva avyavasthāna prasaṅgāt tasmāt tasya api smṛti vipratipatti upanyāsena smṛti anusāra aviṣaya vivecanena ca sat mārge prajñā saṃgrahaṇīyā yā tu śrutiḥ kapilasya jñāna atiśayam pradarśayantī pradarśitā na tayā śruti viruddham api kāpilam matam śraddhātum śakyam kāpilam iti śruti sāmānya mātra tvāt anyasya ca kapilasya sagara putrāṇām prataptuḥ vāsudeva nāmnaḥ smaraṇāt  anya artha darśanasya ca prāpti rahitasya asādhaka tvāt bhavati ca anyā manoḥ māhātmyam prakhyāpayantī śrutiḥ iti manunā ca asarva bhūteṣu ca ātmānam sarva bhūtāni ca ātmani saṃpaśyan  ātma yājī vai svārājyam adhigacchati iti sarva ātma tva darśanam praśaṃsatā kāpilam matam nindyata iti gamyate kapilaḥ  hi na sarva ātma tva darśanam anumanyate ātma bheda abhyupagamāt mahābhārate api ca abahavaḥ puruṣā brahman  uta aho eka eva tu iti vicārya abahavaḥ puruṣā rājan sāṃkhya yoga vicāriṇām iti para pakṣam upanyasya tad vyudāsena iti upakramya amama antarātmā tava ca ye ca anye deha saṃsthitāḥ sarveṣām sākṣi bhūtaḥ  asau na grāhyaḥ kenacid kvacid  viśvamūrdhā viśvabhujaḥ  visvapāda akṣi nāsikaḥ ekaḥ carati bhūteṣu svaira cārī yathāsukham iti sarva ātma tā eva nirdhāritā śrutiḥ ca sarva ātma tāyām bhavati iti evaṃvidhā atas ca siddham ātma bheda kalpanayā api kapilasya tantram veda viruddham veda anusāri manu vacana viruddham ca na kevalam svatantra prakṛti kalpanayā eva iti vedasya hi nirapekṣam sva arthe prāmāṇyam raveḥ iva rūpa viṣaye puruṣa vacasām tu mūla antara apekṣam vaktu smṛti vyavahitam ca iti viprakarṣaḥ tasmāt veda viruddhe viṣaye smṛti anavakāśa prasaṅgaḥ  na doṣaḥ pradhānāt itarāṇi yāni pradhāna pariṇāma tvam na samṛtau kalpitāni mahat ādīni na tāni vede loke vā upalabhyante bhūta indriyāṇi tāvat loka veda prasiddha tvāt śakyante smartum aloka veda prasiddha tvāt tu mahat ādīnām ṣaṣṭhasi iva indriya arthasya na smṛtiḥ avakalpate yad api kvacid tad param iva śravaṇam avabhāsate tad api atat param vyākhyātam aānumānikam api ekeṣām iti atra kārya smṛteḥ aprāmāṇyāt kāraṇa smṛteḥ api aprāmāṇyam yuktam iti abhiprāyaḥ tasmāt api na smṛti anavakāśa prasaṅgaḥ  doṣaḥ tarka avaṣṭambham tu ana vilakṣaṇa tvāt iti ārabhyonmathiṣyati yoga pratyukti adhikaraṇam sū etena yogaḥ pratyuktaḥ etena sāṃkhya smṛti pratyākhyānena yoga smṛtiḥ api pratyākhyātā draṣṭavyā iti atidiśati tatra api śruti virodhena pradhānam svatantram eva kāraṇam mahat ādīni ca kāryāṇi aloka veda prasiddhāni kalpyante nanu evam sati samāna nyāya tvāt pūrveṇa eva etad gatam kimartham punar atidiśyate asti hi atra abhyadhika āśaṅkā samyak darśana abhyupāyo hi yogaḥ  vede vihitaḥ aśrotavyaḥ  mantavyaḥ  nididhyāsitavyaḥ iti atri unnatam sthāpya samam śarīram ityādinā ca āsana ādi kalpanā puraḥsaram bahu prapañcam yoga vidhānam śvetāśvatara upaniṣadi dṛśyate liṅgāni ca vaidikāni yoga viṣayāṇi sahasraśa upalabhyante atām yogam iti manyante sthirām indriya dhāraṇām iti avidyām etām yoga vidhim ca kṛtsnam iti ca evamādīni yoga śāstre api aatha tattva darśana upāyo yogaḥ iti samyak darśanābhyupāya tvena eva yoga uṅgīkriyate atas  saṃpratipanna artha eka deśa tvāt aṣṭaka ādi smṛtivat yoga smṛtiḥ api anapavadanīyā bhaviṣyati iti iyam api adhikā śaṅkā atideśena nivartyate artha eka deśa saṃpratipattau  api artha eka deśa vipratipatteḥ pūrva uktāyāḥ  darśanāt  satīṣu api adhyātma viṣayāsu bahvīṣu smṛtiṣu sāṃkhya yoga smṛtyoḥ eva nirākaraṇe yatnaḥ kṛtaḥ sāṃkhya yogau hi parama puruṣa artha sādhana tvena loke prakhyātau śiṣṭaiḥ ca parigṛhītau liṅgena na śrautena upabṛṃhitau atad kāraṇam sāṃkhya yoga abhipannam jñātvā devam mucyate sarva pāśaiḥ iti nirākaraṇam tu na sāṃkhya jñānena veda nirapekṣeṇa yoga mārgeṇa vā niḥśreyasam adhigamyata iti śrutiḥ hi vaidikāt ātmā ekatva vijñānāt anyat niḥśreyasa sādhanam vārayati atam eva viditvā atimṛtyum eti na anyaḥ panthā vidyate ayanāya iti dvaitinaḥ  hi te sāṃkhyā yogāḥ ca na ātma ekatva darśinaḥ yad tu darśanamuktam atad kāraṇam sāṃkhya yoga abhipannam iti vaidikam eva tatra jñānam dhyānam ca sāṃkhya yoga śabdābhyām abhilapyate pratyāsatteḥ iti avagantavyam yena tu aṃśena na virudhyete tena iṣṭam eva sāṃkhya yoga smṛtyoḥ sa avakāśa tvam tad yathā iti evamādi śruti prasiddham eva puruṣasya viśuddha tvam nirguṇa puruṣa nirūpaṇena sāṃkhyaiḥ abhyupagamyate tathā ca yogaiḥ api aatha parivrāj vivarṇa vāsāḥ  muṇḍaḥ  aparigrahaḥ iti evamādi śruti prasiddham eva nivṛtti niṣṭha tvam pravrajyā ādi upadeśena anugamyate etena sarvāṇi tarka smaraṇāni prativaktavyāni tāni api tarka upapattibhyām tattva jñānāya upakurvanti iti ced upakurvantu nāma tattva jñānam tu vedānta vākyebhyaḥ  eva bhavati anāveda vinmanute tam bṛhantam atam tu aupaniṣadam puruṣam pṛcchāmi iti evamādi śrutibhyaḥ brahma asya jagataḥ  nimitta kāraṇam prakṛtiḥ ca iti asya pakṣasya ākṣepaḥ smṛti nimittaḥ parihṛtaḥ tarka nimitta idānīm ākṣepaḥ parihriyate kutas  punar asmin  avadhārita āgama arthe tarka nimittasya ākṣepasya avakāśaḥ nanu dharma iva brahmaṇi anapekṣa āgamaḥ  bhavitum arhati bhavet ayam avaṣṭambhaḥ  yadi pramāṇa antara anavagāhya āgama mātra prameyaḥ  ayam arthaḥ syāt anuṣṭheya rūpa iva dharmaḥ pariniṣpanna rūpam tu brahma avagamyate pariniṣpanne ca vastuni pramāṇa antarāṇām asti avakāśaḥ  yathā pṛthivī ādiṣu yathā ca śrutīnām paraspara virodhe sati eka vaśena itarā nīyante evam pramāṇa antara virodhe api tad vaśena eva śrutiḥ nīyeta dṛṣṭa sāmyena ca adṛṣṭam artham samarthayantī yuktiḥ anubhavasya saṃnikṛṣyate viprakṛṣyate tu śrutiḥ aitihya mātreṇa sva artha abhidhānāt  anubhava avasānam ca brahma vijñānam avidyāyāḥ  nivartakam mokṣa sādhanam ca dṛṣṭa phalatayā iṣyate śrutiḥ api iti śravaṇa vyatirekeṇa mananam vidadhatī tarkam api atra ādartavyam darśayati atas tarka nimittaḥ punar ākṣepaḥ kriyate ana vilakṣaṇa tvāt asya iti yad uktam cetanam brahma jagataḥ kāraṇam prakṛtiḥ iti tad na upapadyate kasmāt  vilakṣaṇa tvāt asya vikārasya prakṛtyāḥ idam hi brahma kārya tvena abhipreyamāṇam jagat  brahma vilakṣaṇam acetanam aśuddham ca dṛśyate brahma ca jagat vilakṣaṇam cetanam śuddham ca śrūyate na ca vilakṣaṇa tvam prakṛti vikāra bhāvaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ na hi rucakāt ayaḥ  vikārā mṛd prakṛtikā bhavanti śarāvāt ayaḥ  vā suvarṇa prakṛtikāḥ mṛdā eva tu mṛdā anvitā vikārāḥ kriyante suvarṇena ca suvarṇa anvitāḥ tathā idam api jagat acetanam sukha duḥkha moha anvitam sat acetanasya eva sukha duḥkha moha ātmakasya kāraṇasya kāryam bhavitum arhati iti na vilakṣaṇasya brahmaṇaḥ brahma vilakṣaṇam ca asya jagataḥ  aśuddhi acetana tva darśanāt avagantavyam aśuddham hi jagat sukha duḥkha moha ātmaka tayā prīti paritāpa viṣāda ādi hetu tvāt svarga naraka ādi uccāvaca prapañca tvāt ca acetanam ca idam jagat cetanam prati kārya kāraṇa bhāvena upakaraṇa bhāva upagamāt na hi sāmye sati upakārya upakāraka bhāvaḥ  bhavati na hi pradīpau parasparasya upakurutaḥ nanu cetanam api kārya kāraṇam svāmi bhṛtya nyāyena bhoktuḥ upakariṣyati na svāmi bhṛtyayoḥ api acetana aṃśasya eva cetanam pratyupakāraka tvāt  yaḥ  hi ekasya cetanasya parigrahaḥ  buddhi ādi cetana bhāgaḥ sa eva anyasya cetanasya upakaroti na tu svayam eva cetanaḥ cetanā antarasya upakaroti apakaroti vā niratiśayā hi akartāraḥ cetanā iti sāṃkhyā manyante tasmāt acetanam kārya kāraṇam na ca kāṣṭa loṣṭa ādīnām cetana tve kim cit pramāṇam asti prasiddhaḥ ca ayam cetana acetana vibhāgaḥ  loke tasmāt brahma vilakṣaṇa tvāt na idam jagat tad prakṛtikam yaḥ  api kaścid ācakṣīta śrutvā jagataḥ cetana prakṛtikatām tad balena eva samastam jagat cetanam avagamayiṣyāmi prakṛti rūpasya vikāre anvaya darśanāt  avibhāvanam tu caitanyasya pariṇāma viśeṣāt bhaviṣyati yathā spaṣṭa caitanyānām api ātmanām svāpa mūrcchā ādi avasthāsu caitanyam na vibhāvyata evam kāṣṭha loṣṭa ādīnām api caitanyam na vibhāvayiṣyate etasmāt eva ca vibhāvita avibhāvita tva kṛtāt viśeṣāt rūpa ādi bhāva abhāvābhyām ca kārya kāraṇānām ātmanām ca cetanatva aviśeṣe api guṇa pradhāna bhāvaḥ  na virotsyate yathā ca pārthiva tva aviśeṣe api māṃsa sūpa odana ādīnām pratyātma vartinaḥ  viśeṣāt paraspara upakāri tvam bhavati evam iha api bhaviṣyati pravibhāga prasiddhiḥ apyata eva na virotsyata iti tena api kathañcid cetana acetana tva lakṣaṇam vilakṣaṇa tvam parihriyeta śuddhi aśuddhi tva lakṣaṇam tu vilakṣaṇa tvam na eva parihriyate naca itarat api vilakṣaṇa tvam parihartum śakyata iti āha tathā tvam ca śabdāt iti anavagamyamānam evam hi idam loke samastasya vastunaḥ cetana tvam cetana prakṛtika tva śravaṇāt śabda śaraṇa tayā kevalayā utprekṣata tad ca śabdena eva virudhyate yatas  śabdāt api tathā tvam avagamyate tathātvam iti prakṛti vilakṣaṇa tvam kathayati śabda eva avijñānam ca avijñānam ca iti kasyacid vibhāgasya acetanatām śrāvayan  cetanāt brahmaṇaḥ  vilakṣaṇam acetanam jagat śrāvayati tuśabda āśaṅkām apanudati na khalu mṛd abravīt iti evan jātīyakayā śrutyā bhūta indriyāṇām cetana tvam āśaṅkanīyam yatas  abhimāni vyapadeśa eṣaḥ mṛd ādi abhimāninyaḥ  vāc ādi abhimāninyaḥ ca cetanā devatā vadana saṃvadana ādiṣu cetana uciteṣu vyavahāreṣu vyapadiśyante na bhūta indriya mātram kasmāt  viśeṣa anugatibhyām viśeṣaḥ  hi bhoktṛṇām bhūta indriyāṇām ca cetana acetana pravibhāga lakṣaṇaḥ prāc abhihitaḥ sarva cetana tāyām ca asau na upapadyeta apica kauṣītakinaḥ prāṇa saṃvāde karaṇa mātra āśaṅkā vinivṛttaye adhiṣṭhātṛ cetana parigrahāya devatā śabdena viśiṣanti iti atā vā etāḥ sarvā devatāḥ prāṇe niḥśreyasam viditvā iti ca anugatāḥ ca sarvatra abhimāninyaḥ cetanā devatā mantra artha vāda itihāsa purāṇa ādibhyaḥ  avagamyante aagniḥ vāc bhūtvā mukham prāviśat iti evamādikā ca śrutiḥ karaṇeṣu anugrāhikām devatām anugatām darśayati prāṇa saṃvāda vākya śeṣe ca ate ha prāṇāḥ prajāpatim pitaram eti ūcuḥ iti śreṣṭha tva nirdhāraṇāya prajāpati gamanam tad vacanāca ekaika utkramaṇena anvaya vyatirkābhyām prāṇa śraiṣṭhya pratipattiḥ atasmai bali haraṇam iti ca evan jātīyakaḥ  asmad ādiṣu iva vyavahāraḥ  anugamyamānaḥ  abhimāni vyapadeśam draḍhayati atat teja aikṣata iti api parasya eva devatāyāḥ  adhiṣṭa atryāḥ sva vikāreṣu anugatāya iyam īkṣā vyapadiśyata iti draṣṭavyam tasmāt vilakṣaṇam eva idam brahmaṇaḥ  jagat  vilakṣaṇa tvāt ca na brahma prakṛtikam iti ākṣipte pratividhatte tuśabdaḥ pakṣam vyāvartayati yad uktam vilakṣaṇa tvāt na idam jagat brahmaprakṛtikam iti na ayam ekāntaḥ dṛśyate hi loke cetana tvena prasiddhebhyaḥ puruṣa ādibhyaḥ  vilakṣaṇānām keśa nakha ādīnām utpattiḥ acetana tvena ca prasiddhebhyaḥ  gomaya ādibhyaḥ  vṛścika ādīnām nanu acetanāni eva puruṣa ādi śarīrāṇi acetanānām keśa nakha ādīnām kāraṇāni acetanāni eva ca vṛścika ādi śarīrāṇi acetanānām gomaya ādīnām kāryāṇi iti ucyate evam api kiñcid acetanam cetanasya āyatana bhāvam upagacchati kiñcid nā iti asti eva vailakṣaṇyam mahān  ca ayam pāriṇāmikaḥ svabhāva viprakarṣaḥ puruṣa ādīnām keśa nakha ādīnām ca sva rūpa ādi bhedāt tathā gomaya ādīnām vṛścika ādīnām ca atyanta sārūpye ca prakṛti vikāra bhāva eva pralīyeta atha ucyeta asti kaścid pārthiva tva ādi svabhāvaḥ puruṣa ādīnām keśa nakha ādiṣu anuvartamānaḥ  gomaya ādīnām vṛścika ādiṣu iti brahmaṇaḥ  api tarhi sattā lakṣaṇaḥ svabhāva ākāśa ādiṣu anuvartamāna udṛśyate vilakṣaṇa tvena ca kāraṇena brahma prakṛti tvam jagataḥ  dūṣayatā kim aśeṣasya brahma svabhāvasya ananuvartanam vilakṣaṇa tvam abhipreyata uta yasya kasyacid asya caitanyasya iti vaktavyam prathame vikalpe samasta prakṛti vikāra uccheda prasaṅgaḥ na hi asati atiśaye prakṛti vikāra iti bhavati dvitīye ca asiddhatvam dṛśyate hi sattā la kṣaṇaḥ  brahma svabhāva ākāśa ādiṣu anuvartamāna iti uktam tṛtīye tu dṛṣṭānta abhāvaḥ kim hi yad caitanyena ananvitam tad abrahma prakṛtikam dṛṣṭam iti brahma vādinam pratyudāhriyeta samastasya vastu jāyasya brahma prakṛti tva abhyupagamāt āgama virodhaḥ tu prasiddha eva cetanam brahma jagataḥ kāraṇam prakṛtiḥ ca iti āgama tātparyasya prasādhita tvāt  yad tu uktam pariniṣpanna tvāt brahmaṇi pramāṇa antarāṇi saṃbhaveyuḥ iti tad api manoratha mātram rūpa ādi abhāvāt hi na ayam arthaḥ pratyakṣasya gocaraḥ liṅga ādi abhāvāt ca na anumāna ādīnām āgama mātra samadhigamya eva tu ayam arthaḥ  dharmavat  tathā ca śrutiḥ iti ako addhā veda ka iha pravocat aiyam visṛṣṭiḥ yata ābabhūva iti ca ete ṛcau siddhānām api īśvarāṇām durbodhatām jagat kāraṇasya darśayataḥ smṛtiḥ api bhavati iti aavyaktaḥ  ayam acintyaḥ  ayam avikārya uyam ucyate iti ca ana me viduḥ sura gaṇāḥ prabhavam na mahā ṛṣayaḥ aham ādiḥ hi devānām mahā ṛṣīṇām ca sarvaśaḥ iti ca evan jātīyakā yad api śravaṇa vyatirekeṇa mananam vidadhat śabda eva tarkam api ādartavyam darśayati iti uktam na anena miṣeṇa śuṣka tarkasya atra ātma lābhaḥ saṃbhavati śruti anugṛhīta eva hi atra tarkaḥ  anubhava aṅga tvena āśrīyate svapna anta buddha antayoḥ ubhayoḥ itaretara vyabhicārāt ātmanaḥ  ananvāgata tvam saṃprasāde ca prapañca parityāgena sat ātmanā saṃpatteḥ niṣprapañca sat ātma tvam prapañcasya brahma prabhava tvāt kārya kāraṇa ananya tva nyāyena brahma avyatireka iti evan jātīyakaḥ atarka apratiṣṭhānāt iti ca kevalasya tarkasya vipralambhaka tvam darśayiṣyati yaḥ  api cetana kāraṇa śravaṇa balena eva samastasya jagataḥ cetana tām utprekṣate tasya api vijñānam ca avijñānam ca iti cetana acetana vibhāga śravaṇam vibhāvanā vibhāvanābhyām caitanyasya śakyata eva yojayitum parasya eva tu idam api vibhāga śravaṇam na yujyate katham parama kāraṇasya hi atra samasta jagat ātmanā samavasthānam śrāvyate avijñānam ca avijñānam ca abhavat iti tatra yathā cetanasya acetana bhāvaḥ  na upapadyate vilakṣaṇa tvāt  evam acetanasya api cetana bhāvaḥ  na upapadyate pratyukta tvāt tu vilakṣaṇa tvasya yathāśrutyā eva kāraṇam grahītavyam bhavati yadi cetanam śuddham śabda vihīnam ca brahma tad viparūtasya acetanasya aśuddhasya śabda ādi mataḥ ca kāryasya kāraṇam iṣyeta asat tarhi kāryam prāk utpatteḥ iti prasajyeta aniṣṭam ca etad sat kārya vādinaḥ tava iti ced  na eṣa doṣaḥ pratiṣedha mātra tvāt  pratiṣedha mātram hi idam na asya pratiṣedhasya pratiṣedhyam asti na hi ayam pratiṣedhaḥ prāk utpatteḥ sattvam kāryasya pratiṣeddhum śaknoti katham yathā eva hi idānām api idam kāryam kāraṇa ātmanā sadevam prāk utpatteḥ api iti gamyate na hi idānām api idam kāryam kāraṇa ātmānam antareṇa svatantram eva asti asarvam tam parāda āt yaḥ  anyatra ātmanaḥ sarvam veda ityādi śravaṇāt  kāraṇa ātmanā tu sattvam kāryasya prāk utpatteḥ aviśiṣṭam nanu śabda ādi hīnam brahma jagataḥ kāraṇam bāḍham na tu śabda ādimat kāryam kāraṇa ātmanā hīnam prāk utpatteḥ idānīm vā asti tena na śakyate vaktum prāk utpatteḥ asatkāryam iti vistareṇa ca etad kārya kāraṇa ananya tva vāde vakṣyāmaḥ api itau tadvat prasaṅgāt  asamañjasam atra āha yadi sthaulya sāvayava tva acetana tva paricchinna tva aśuddhi ādi dharmakam kāryam brahma kāraṇam abhyupagamyeta tad apītau pralaye pratisaṃsṛjyamānam kāryam kāraṇā vibhāgam āpadyamānam kāraṇam ātmīyena dharmeṇa dūṣayet iti apītau kāraṇasya api brahmaṇaḥ kāryasya iva aśuddhi ādi rūpa prasaṅgāt sarvajñam brahma jagat kāraṇam iti asamañjasam idam aupaniṣadam darśanam apica samastasya vibhāgasya avibhāga prāpteḥ punarutpattau niyama kāraṇa abhāvāt bhoktṛ bhogya ādi vibhāgena utpattiḥ na prāpnoti iti asamañjasam apica bhoktṛṇām pareṇa brahmaṇā vibhāgam gatānām karma ādi nimitta pralaye api punar utpattau  abhyupagamyamānāyām muktānām api punar uttatti prasaṅgāt asamañjasam atha idam jagat apītau  api vibhaktam eva pareṇa brahmaṇā avatiṣṭheta evam api apītīḥ ca na saṃbhavati kāraṇa avyatiriktam ca kāryam na saṃbhavati iti asamañjasam eva iti atra ucyate na eva asmadīye darśane kiñcid asām añjasyam asti yad tāvat abhihitam kāraṇam apigacchat kāryam kāraṇam ātmīyena dharmeṇa dūṣayet iti tad adūṣaṇam kasmāt  dṛṣṭānta abhāvāt santi hi dṛṣṭāntā yathā kāraṇam apigacchat kāryam kāraṇam ātmīyena dharmeṇa na dūṣayati tad yathā śarāvāt ayaḥ  mṛd prakṛtikā vikārā vibhāga avasthāyām uccāvaca madhyama prabhedāḥ santaḥ punar  prakṛtim apigacchantaḥ  na tām ātmīyena dharmeṇa saṃsṛjanti rucaka ādayaḥ ca suvarṇa vikārā api itau na suvarṇam ātmīyena dharmeṇa saṃsṛjanti pṛthivī vikāraḥ caturvidhaḥ  bhūta grāmaḥ  na pṛthivīm apītau  ātmīyena dharmeṇa saṃsṛjati tvad pakṣasya tu na kaścid dṛṣṭāntaḥ  asti apītiḥ eva hi na saṃbhavet yadi kāraṇe kāryam svadharmeṇa eva avatiṣṭheta ananya tve api kārya kāraṇayoḥ kāryasya kāraṇa ātma tvam na tu kāraṇasya kārya ātma tvam aārambhaṇa śabda ādibhyaḥ iti vakṣyāmaḥ ati alpam ca idam ucyate kāryam apītau  ātmīyena dharmeṇa kāraṇam saṃsṛjet iti sthitau  api samānaḥ  ayam prasaṅgaḥ kārya kāraṇayoḥ ananya tva abhyupagamāt aidam sarva yad ayam ātmā aātmā evedam sarvam abrahma eva idam amṛtam purastāt asarvam khalu idam brahma iti evamādyābhiḥ hi śrutibhiḥ aviśeṣeṇa triṣu api kāleṣu kāryasya kāraṇa ananya tvam śrāvyate tatra yaḥ parihāraḥ kāryasya tad dharmāṇām ca avidyā adhyāropita tvāt na taiḥ kāraṇam saṃsṛjyata iti apītau  api sa samānaḥ asti ca ayam aparaḥ  dṛṣṭāntaḥ  yathā svayam prasāritayā māyayā māyāvī triṣu api kāleṣu na saṃspaśyate avastu tvāt  evam paramātmā api saṃsāra māyayā na saṃspṛśyata iti yathā ca svapna dṛś ekaḥ svapna darśana māyayā na saṃspṛśyata iti prabodha saṃpradāyoḥ ananu āgata tvāt  evam avasthā traya sākṣi ekaḥ  avyabhicāryavasthā trayeṇa vyabhicāriṇā na saṃspṛśyate māyā mātram hi etad yad paramātmanaḥ  avasthā traya ātmanā avabhāsanam rajjvā iva sarpa ādi bhāvena iti atra uktam vedānta artha saṃpradāya vidbhiḥ ācāryaiḥ iti tatra yad uktam apītau kāraṇasya api kāryasya iva sthaulya ādi doṣa prasaṅga iti etad ayuktam yad punar etad uktam samastasya vibhāgasya avibhāga prāpteḥ punar vibhāgena utpattau niyama kāraṇam na upapadyata iti ayam api adoṣaḥ dṛṣṭānta bhāvāt eva yathā hi suṣupti samādhi ādau  api satyām svābhāvikyāma vibhāga prāptau mithyājñānasya anapodita tvāt pūrvavat punar  prabodhe vibhāgaḥ  bhavati evam iha api bhaviṣyati śrutiḥ ca atra bhavati iti yathā hi avibhāge api parama ātmani mithyājñāna pratibaddhaḥ  vibhāga vyavahāraḥ svapnavat avyāhataḥ sthitaḥ  dṛśyate evam apītau  api mithyājñāna pratibaddhā eva vibhāga śaktiḥ anumāsyate etena muktānām punarutpatti prasaṅgaḥ pratyuktaḥ samyak jñānena mithyājñānasya āpodita tvāt yaḥ punar ayam ante aparaḥ  vikalpa utprekṣitaḥ  atha idam jagat apītau  api vibhaktam eva pareṇa brahmaṇā avatiṣṭheta iti saḥ  api anabhyupagamāt eva pratiṣiddhaḥ tasmāt samañjasam idam aupaniṣadam darśanam sva pakṣe ca ete prativādinaḥ sādhāraṇā doṣāḥ prāduṣyuḥ katham iti ucyate yad tāvat abhihitam vilakṣaṇa tvāt na idam jagat brahmaprakṛtikam iti pradhāna prakṛtikatāyām api samānam etad  śabda ādi hīnāt pradhānāt śabda ādimataḥ  jagata utpatti abhyupagamāt  ata eva ca vilakṣaṇa kārya utpatti abhyupagamāt samānaḥ prāk utpatteḥ asatkārya vāda prasaṅgaḥ tathā apītau kāryasya kāraṇa vibhāga abhyupagamāt tadvat prasaṅgaḥ  api samānaḥ tathā mṛdita sarva viśeṣeṣu vikāreṣu apītau  avibhāga ātma tām gateṣu idam asya puruṣasya upādānam idam asya iti prāc pralayāt prati puruṣam ye niyatā bhedā na te tathā eva punar utpatau niyantum śakyante kāraṇa abhāvāt vinā eva kāraṇena niyame abhyupagamyamāne kāraṇa abhāva sāmyāt muktānām api punar bandha prasaṅgaḥ atha kecid bhedā api itauvavibhāgam āpadyante kenacid na iti ced  ye na āpadyante teṣām pradhāna kārya tvam na prāpnoti iti evam ete doṣāḥ sādhāraṇa tvāt na anyatarasmin pakṣe codayitavyā bhavanti iti adoṣa tām eva eṣām draḍhayati avaśya āśrayitavya tvāt itas ca na āgama gamyer athe kevalena tarkeṇa pratyavasthātavyam yasmin nirāgamāḥ puruṣa utprekṣā mātra nibandhanāḥ tarkā apratiṣṭhitā bhavanti utprekṣāyā niraṅ kuśa tvāt  tathā hi kaiścid abhiyuktaiḥ yatnena utprekṣitāḥ tarkā abhiyuktaraiḥ anyaiḥ ābhāsyamānā dṛśyante taiḥ api utprekṣitāḥ santaḥ tatas  anyaiḥ ābhāsyanta iti na pratiṣṭhita tvam tarkāṇām śakyam āśrayitum puruṣam ati vairūpyāt  atha kasyacid prasiddha māhātmyasya kapilasya ca anyasya vā saṃmataḥ tarkaḥ pratiṣṭhita iti āśrīyeta evam api apratiṣṭhita tvam eva prasiddha māhātmya anumatānām api tīrthakarāṇām kapila kaṇa bhuj prabhṛtīnām paraspara vipratipatti darśanāt atas cyeta anyathā vayam anumāsyāmahe yathā na apratiṣṭhā doṣaḥ  bhaviṣyati na hi pratiṣṭhitaḥ tarka eva na asti iti śakyate vaktum etad api hi tarkāṇām apratiṣṭhita tvam tarkeṇa eva pratiṣṭhāpyate keṣāñcittarkāṇām apratiṣṭhita tva darśanena anyeṣām api tad  sū pratiṣedhāt  iti ced  na śārīrāt  aamṛta tvam ca anupoṣya iti atas  viśeṣaṇāt  ātyantike amṛta tve gati utkrāntyoḥ abhāvaḥ  abhyupagataḥ tatra api kenacid  kāraṇena utkrāntim āśaṅkya pratiṣedhati kāmaḥ  niṣkāma āpta kāma  ātma kāmaḥ  bhavati na tasya prāṇā utkrāmanti brahmā eva san brahmā apyeti iti atas  para vidyā viṣayāt pratiṣedhāt  na para brahma vidaḥ  dehāt  prāṇānām utkrāntiḥ asti iti ced  na iti ucyate yatas  śārīrāt  ātmana eṣa utkrānti pratiṣedhaḥ prāṇānām na śarīrāt  katham avagamyate ana tasmāt prāṇā utkrāmanti iti śākhā antare pañcamī prayogāt  saṃbandha sāmānya viṣayā hi ṣaṣṭhī śākhā antara gatayā pañcamyā saṃbandha viśeṣe vyavasthāpyate tasmāt  iti ca prādhānyāt  abhyudaya niḥśreyasa adhikṛtaḥ  dehī saṃbadhyate na dehaḥ na tasmāt  uccikramiṣoḥ jīvāt  prāṇā apakrāmanti saha eva tena bhavanti iti arthaḥ sa prāṇasya ca pravasataḥ  bhavati utkrāntiḥ dehāt  iti evam prāpte prati ucyate na tad  asti yad  uktam para brahma vidaḥ api dehāt  asti utkrāntiḥ utkrānti pratiṣedhasya deha upādāna tvāt  iti yatas  deha upādāna eva utkrānti pratiṣedha ekeṣām samāmnā tṛṇām spaṣṭa upalabhyate tathā hi ārta bhāga praśne ayatra ayam puruṣaḥ  mriyata udasmāt prāṇāḥ krāmanti āho na iti iti atra aneti ha uvāca yājñavalkyaḥ iti anutkrānti pakṣam parigṛhya na tarhi ayam anutkrānteṣu prāṇeṣu mriyata iti asyām āśaṅkāyām aatra eva samavanīyanta iti pravilayam prāṇānām pratijñāya tad  siddhaye asa ucchvayati ādhyātmāyati ādhmātaḥ  mṛtaḥ śete iti sa śabda parāmṛṣṭasya prakṛtasya utkrānti avadheḥ ucchvayana ādīni samāmananti dehasya ca etāni syuḥ na dehinaḥ tad  sāmānyāt  ana tasmāt prāṇā utkrāmanti atra eva samavanīyante iti atra api abheda upacāreṇa deha āpādānasya eva utkramaṇasya pratiṣedhaḥ yadi api prādhānyam dehina iti vyākhyeyam yeṣām pañcamī pāṭhaḥ yeṣām tu ṣaṣṭhī pāṭhaḥ teṣām vidvat  saṃbandhini utkrāntiḥ pratiṣidhyata iti prāpta utkrānti pratiṣedha artha tvāt asya vākyasya deha pādāna eva sā pratiṣiddhā bhavati dehāt  utkrāntiḥ prāptā na dehinaḥ api ca acakṣuṣaḥ  vā mūrdhno vā anyebhyaḥ  vā śarīra deśebhyaḥ tam utkrāmantam prāṇaḥ  anūtkrāmati prāṇaḥ  anūtkrāmantam sarve prāṇā anūtkrāmanti iti evam avidvat  viṣayam sa prapañcam utkramaṇam saṃsāra gamanam ca darśayitvā aiti nu kāmayamānaḥ iti upasaṃhṛtya avidvat  kathām aatha akāmayamānaḥ iti vyapadiśya vidvāṃsam yadi tad  viṣaye api utkrāntam eva prāpadeya samañjasa eva vyapadeśaḥ syāt  tasmāt  avidviṣaye prāptayoḥ gati utkrāntyoḥ vidvat  viṣaye pratiṣedha iti evam eva vyākhyeyam vyapadeśa arthavat tvāya na ca brahma vidaḥ sarva gata brahma ātma bhūtasya prakṣīṇa kāma karmaṇa utkrāntiḥ gatiḥ vā upapadyate nimitta abhāvāt  aatra brahma samaśnute iti ca evan jātīyakāḥ śrutayo gati utkrāntyoḥ abhāvam sūcayanti smaryate ca smaryate api ca mahābhārate gati utkrāntyoḥ abhāvaḥ iti nanu gatiḥ iti brahma vidaḥ sarva gata brahma ātma bhūtasya smaryate aśukaḥ kila vaiyāsakiḥ mumukṣuḥ āditya maṇḍalam abhipratasthe pitrā ca anugamya āhūtaḥ  bho iti pratiśuśrāva iti na sa śarīrasya eva ayam yoga balena viśiṣṭa deśa prāpti pūrvakaḥ śarīra utsarga iti draṣṭavyam sarva bhūta dṛśya tva ādi upanyāsāt  na hi aśarīram gacchantam sarva bhūtāni draṣṭum śaknuyuḥ tathā ca tatra eva aupasaṃhṛtam bhavat iti tasmāt  abhāvaḥ para brahma vidaḥ  gati utkrāntyoḥ gati śrutīnām tu viṣayam upariṣṭāt  vyākhyāsyāmaḥ vāc ādi laya adhikaraṇam sū tāni pare tathā hi  āha tāni punar  prāṇa śabda uditāni indriyāṇi bhūtāni ca para brahma vidaḥ tasmin eva parasmin ātmani pralīyante kasmāt  tathā hi āha śrutiḥ gatāḥ kalāḥ pañcadaśa pratiṣṭhāḥ iti vidvat  viṣaya eva aparā śrutiḥ parasmāt  ātmanaḥ anyatra api kalānām pralayam āha sma na sā khalu vyavahāra apekṣā pārthiva ādyāḥ kalāḥ pṛthivī ādiḥ eva sva prakṛtīḥ apīyanti iti itarā tu vidvat  pratipatti apekṣā kṛtsnam kalā jātam para brahma vidaḥ  brahma eva saṃpadyata iti tasmāt  adoṣaḥ avibhāga adhikaraṇam sū avibhāgaḥ  vacanāt  sa puna viduṣaḥ kalā pralayaḥ kim itareṣām iva sa avaśeṣaḥ  bhavati āhosvit  niravaśeṣa iti tatra pralaya sāmānyāt  śakti avaśeṣa tā prasaktau bravīti avibhāga āpattiḥ eva iti kutas  vacanāt  tathā hi kalā pralayam uktvā vakti kalo amṛtaḥ  bhavati iti avidyā nimittānām ca kalānām na vidyā nimitte pralaye sa avaśeṣa tva upapattiḥ tasmāt  avibhāga eva iti tad okaḥ adhikaraṇam sū tad oka ugra jvalanam tad prakāśi ta dvāraḥ  vidyā sāmarthyāt  tad śeṣa gati anusmṛti yoga āt  ca hārda anugṛhītāḥ śata adhikayā samāptā prāsaṅgikī para vidyā āgatā cintā saṃpratitu apara vidyā viṣayām eva cintām anuvartayati samānā ca asṛti upakramāt  vidvat  aviduṣoḥ utkrāntiḥ iti uktam tam idānīm sati upakramam darśayati tasya upasaṃhṛta vāc ādi kalāpasya uccikramiṣataḥ  vijñāna ātmana oka āyatanam hṛdayam asa etāḥ tejaḥ mātrāḥ samabhyāda dānaḥ  hṛdayam eva anvavakrāmati iti śruteḥ tad  agra prajvalana pūrvikā cakṣuḥ ādi sthāna apādānā ca utkrāntiḥ śrūyate iti sā kim aniyamena eva vidvat  aviduṣoḥ bhavati atha asti kaścid  viduṣaḥ  viśeṣa niyama iti vicikitsāyām śruti aviśeṣāt  aniyama prāptau ācaṣṭe samā api hi vidvat  aviduṣoḥ hṛdaya agra pradyotane tad  prakāśi ta dvāra tve ca mūrdha sthānāt  eva vidvān niṣkrāmati sthāna antarebhyaḥ tu itare kutas  vidyā sāmarthyāt  yadi vidvān api itaravat  yatas  kutaścid  deha deśāt  utkrāmeta na eva utkṛṣṭam lokam labheta tatra ānarthikā eva vidyā syāt  tad  śeṣa gati anusmṛti yogāt  ca vidyā śeṣa bhūtāḥ  ca mūrdhani anāḍī saṃbaddhā gatiḥ anuśīlayitavyā vidyā viśeṣeṣu vihitā tām abhyasyan tasya eva pratiṣṭhita iti yuktam tasmāt  hṛdaya ālayena brahmaṇā su upāsitena anugṛhītaḥ tad bhāvam samāpannaḥ  vidvān mūrdhanyayā eva śata adhikayā śatāt  atiriktayā eka śatatamyā nāḍyā niṣkrāmati itarābhiḥ itare tathā hi hārdavidyām prakṛtya samāmananti iti raśmi adhikaraṇam sū raśmi anusārī asti hārdavidyā iti upakramya vihitā tad  prakriyāyām aatha yā etā hṛdayasya nāḍyaḥ iti upakramya sa prapañcam nāḍī raśmi saṃbandham uktvā uktam aatha yatra etad asmāt śarīrāt utkrāmati atha etaiḥ eva raśmibhiḥ ūrdhvam ākramate iti punar  ca uktam ataya ūrdhvamāyan  amṛta tvam eti iti tasmāt  śata adhikayā nāḍyā niṣkrāman raśmi anusārī niṣkrāmati iti gamyate tad  kiṃm aviśeṣeṇa eva ahani rātrau vā mriyamāṇasya raśmi anusāri tvam āhosvit  ahani eva iti saṃśaye sati aviśeṣa śravaṇāt  aviśeṣeṇa eva tāvat  raśmi anusāri iti pratijñāyate niśi na iti ced  na sambandhasya yāvat deha bhāvi tvāt  darśayati ca asti ahani nāḍī raśmi saṃbandha iti ahani mṛtasya syāt  raśmi anusāri tvam rātrau tu pretasya na syāt  nāḍī raśmi saṃbandha vicchedāt iti ced  na nāḍī raśmi saṃbandhasya yāvat  deha bhāvi tvāt  yāvat  deha bhāvī hi śirā kiraṇa saṃparkaḥ darśayati ca etam artham śrutiḥ muṣmin  āditye sṛptāḥ iti nidāgha samaye ca niśāsu api kiraṇa anuvṛttiḥ upalabhyate pratāpa ādi kārya darśanāt stoka anuvṛtteḥ tu durlakṣya tvam ṛtu antara rajanīṣu śaiśireṣu iva durdineṣu aahar eva etad rātrau dadhāti iti ca etad eva darśayati yadi ca rātrau pretaḥ  vinā eva raśmi anusāreṇa ūrdhvam ākrameta raśmi anusāra ānarthakyam bhavet  na hi etad  viśiṣya adhīyate yaḥ  divā praiti sa raśmīn apekṣya ūrdvam ākramate yaḥ tu rātrau saḥ anapekṣya eva iti atha tu vidvān api rātri prāyaṇa aparādha mātreṇa na ūrdhvam ākrameta pākṣikaphalā vidyā iti apravṛttiḥ eva tasyām syāt  mṛtyu kāla aniyamāt atha api rātrau uparataḥ ahar āgamam udīkṣeta ahar āgame api asya kadācid  araśmi saṃbandha arham śarīram syāt  pāvaka ādi saṃparkāt  asa yāvat kṣipyet manaḥ tāvat ādityam gacchati iti ca śrutiḥ anudīkṣām darśayati tasmāt  tad  aviśeṣeṇa eva idam rātri divam raśmi anusāri tvam dakṣiṇāyana adhikaraṇam sū atas  ca ayane api dakṣiṇe ata eva ca udīkṣā anupapatteḥ apākṣika phala tvāt  ca vidyāyā aniyata kāla tvāt  ca mṛtyoḥ dakṣiṇa ayane api mriyamāṇaḥ  vidvān prāpnoti eva vidyā phalam uttarāyaṇa maraṇa prāśasti aprasiddheḥ bhīṣmasya ca pratīkṣā darśanāt  aāpūryamāṇa pakṣa ādyān ṣaṣ udaṅṅā iti māsān  tān iti ca śruteḥ apekṣitavyam uttarāyaṇam iti imām āśaṅkām anena sūtreṇa apanudati prāśasti aprasiddhiḥ avidvat  viṣayā bhīṣmasya pratipālanam ācāra pratipālana artham pitṛ prasāda labdha svacchanda mṛtyu tā khyāpana artham ca śruteḥ tu artham vakṣyati aātivāhikāḥ tad liṅgāt iti nanu ca iti kāla prādhānyena upakramya aharādi kāla viśeṣaḥ smṛtau apunarāvṛttaye niyamitaḥ katham rātrau dakṣiṇāyane vā prayātaḥ  anāvṛttim yāyāt iti atra ucyate yoginaḥ prati ca ayam aharādi kāla viniyogaḥ anāvṛttaye smaryate smārte ca ete yoga sāṃkhye na śraute atas  viṣaya bhedāt  pramāṇa aviśeṣāt  ca na asya smārtasya kāla viniyogasya śrauteṣu vijñāneṣu avatāraḥ nanu a
